### [1] [NeuroFlake: A Neuro-Symbolic LLM Framework for Flaky Test Classification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11482v1)
*Khondaker Tasnia Hoque,Toukir Ahammed*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出NeuroFlake，一种神经符号框架，通过判别性标记挖掘和注入LLM注意力机制，在不平衡数据集上改进易碎测试分类F1分数至69.34%，并提升鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM方法在易碎测试分类中过度拟合表面文本伪影，缺乏对实际逻辑的理解，导致泛化性差且易受扰动。

Method: 集成判别性标记挖掘（DTM）模块自动发现高保真代码标记，并将这些信号注入LLM注意力机制，实现神经符号融合。

Result: 在FlakeBench上F1分数达69.34%（优于先前最佳65.79%），对抗扰动下性能下降仅4-7个百分点（基线下降8-18个百分点）。

Conclusion: 神经符号融合能有效提升易碎测试分类的准确性和鲁棒性，优于纯神经网络方法。

中文摘要：易碎测试（flaky tests）对于同一版本代码表现出非确定性的通过/失败行为，给可靠的回归测试带来了重大挑战。虽然大型语言模型（LLMs）有望用于自动化易碎测试分类，但它们常常无法理解测试易碎性背后的实际逻辑，反而过度拟合表面的文本伪影（例如特定的变量名）。这种语义脆弱性导致在现实世界的不平衡数据集上泛化能力差，且容易受到扰动的影响。在本文中，我们提出了NeuroFlake，一种新颖的神经符号框架，用于对高度不平衡的真实世界数据集（FlakeBench）上的易碎测试进行分类。与先前依赖脆弱的手工规则和黑盒学习的方法不同，NeuroFlake集成了一个判别性标记挖掘（DTM）模块，以自动发现高保真、统计显著的源代码标记（例如，特定的并发原语或异步等待）。通过将这些强潜信号直接注入LLM的注意力机制，我们弥合了神经直觉与符号精度之间的差距。我们的实验表明，神经符号融合通过将分类F1分数提升至69.34%显著提高了分类性能，而先前最先进的方法的最佳F1分数为65.79%。此外，我们通过对抗性压力测试严格评估了NeuroFlake的鲁棒性，引入了语义保持的增强（例如，死代码注入、变量重命名）。虽然基线模型在扰动测试上表现下降8-18个百分点，但NeuroFlake在未见过的增强上保持了性能稳定性，仅下降4-7个百分点。

Original abstract: Flaky tests, which exhibit non-deterministic pass/fail behavior for the same version of code, pose significant challenges to reliable regression testing. While large language models (LLMs) promise for automated flaky test classification, they often fail to comprehend the actual logic behind test flakiness, instead overfitting to superficial textual artifacts (e.g., specific variable names). This semantic fragility leads to poor generalization on real-world imbalance dataset and vulnerability to perturbations. In this paper, we introduce NeuroFlake, a novel neuro-Symbolic framework for classifying flaky tests on highly imbalanced, real-world datasets (FlakeBench). Unlike prior approaches that rely on brittle manual rule and black box learning, NeuroFlake integrates a Discriminative Token Mining (DTM) module to automate the discovery of high-fidelity, statistically significant source code tokens (e.g., specific concurrency primitives or async waits). By injecting these strong latent signals directly into LLM's attention mechanism, we bridge the gap between neural intuition and symbolic precision. Our experiments demonstrate that neuro-symbolic fusion significantly improves classification performance by leveraging classification F1-score to 69.34% while prior state-of-art shows best F1-score 65.79%. However, we rigorously evaluate NeuroFlake's robustness through adversarial stress testing, introducing semantic preserving augmentations (e.g., dead code injection, variable renaming). While baseline models exhibit performance degradation of 8-18 percentage points (pp) on perturbed tests, NeuroFlake maintains performance stability on unseen augmentations dropping only 4-7 pp.

</details>


### [2] [Decaf: Improving Neural Decompilation with Automatic Feedback and Search](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11501v1)
*Alexander Shypula,Osbert Bastani,Edward Schwartz*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Decaf系统，利用编译器反馈通过搜索提高神经反编译的语义正确性，在ExeBench数据集上将反编译率从26.0%提升至83.9%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经反编译器存在幻觉问题，产生不正确的编程结构和语义，而单纯增加数据和训练难以解决。

Method: 在神经反编译器输出后，使用编译器反馈进行搜索优化，自动调整生成代码以通过编译且保持语义正确。

Result: 在Real -O2分割上将反编译率从26.0%提升至83.9%，同时不牺牲与原始源代码的相似性，且对弱模型同样有效。

Conclusion: 编译器反馈是提升神经反编译器语义正确性的有效手段，Decaf系统证明了该方法的有效性。

中文摘要：反编译器是逆向工程中用于理解编译后源代码的有用工具。从编译后的二进制文件重建源代码是一项具有挑战性的任务，因为当编译器将人类可读的代码转换为低级机器码时，高级语法、标识符和自定义数据类型通常会丢失。确定性反编译器是用于二进制分析的有用工具，但在推断惯用语法和标识符名称方面可能表现不佳。生成式人工智能模型自然适合重建高级语法、标识符和类型，但它们仍然可能因产生不当的编程结构和语义而出现幻觉。我们主张，与其尝试通过更多数据和更多训练来改进神经反编译器，不如利用编译器反馈通过搜索来显著提高神经反编译器输出的语义正确性。我们的系统Decaf（具有自动反馈的反编译）将ExeBench上的神经反编译率从26.0%提高到Real -O2拆分上的83.9%，而不会牺牲与原始源代码的相似性。我们还发现，我们的自动反馈方法对于改进较弱的神经反编译模型非常有效。

Original abstract: Decompilers are useful tools used in reverse engineering to understand compiled source code. Reconstructing source code from compiled binaries is a challenging task, because high-level syntax, identifiers, and custom data types are generally lost as the compiler translates human-readable code to low-level machine code. Deterministic decompilers are useful tools for binary analysis, but can struggle to infer idiomatic syntax and identifier names. Generative AI models are a natural fit for reconstructing high-level syntax, identifiers, and types, but they can still suffer by hallucinating improper programming constructs and semantics. Instead of attempting to improve neural decompilers with more data and more training, we argue that compiler feedback can be used to dramatically improve the semantic correctness of neural decompiler outputs via search. Our system, Decaf (DECompilation with Automated Feedback), raises the neural decompilation rate from 26.0% on ExeBench to 83.9% on the Real -O2 split without sacrificing similarity to the original source code. We also find our automatic feedback methodology is highly effective for improving weaker neural decompilation models.

</details>


### [3] [A Research Agenda on Agents and Software Engineering: Outcomes from the Rio A2SE Seminar](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11720v1)
*Davide Taibi,Henry Muccini,Karthik Vaidhyanathan,Marcos Kalinowski,Michele Albano,Antonio Pedro Santos Alves,Renato Cerqueira,Mateus Devino,Matteo Esposito,Rodrigo Falcão,Vinicius Henning,Foutse Khomh,Valentina Lenarduzzi,Qinghua Lu,Matías Martínez,Henrique Mello,Daniel Mendez,Lucas Romao*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 代理型AI与软件工程双向影响，通过专家研讨会确定六个主题领域并形成研究议程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代理型AI正在重塑软件工程，需要协调研究议程以覆盖代理支持软件工程和代理系统自身工程化两个方向。

Method: 组织A2SE研讨会，汇集18位专家，通过结构化演示、协作主题聚类和聚焦小组讨论识别主题并优先排序研究方向。

Result: 确定了治理、面向代理的软件工程、面向软件架构的代理、质量与评估、可持续性、代码六个主题领域及对应的短期和长期研究方向。

Conclusion: 提出了社区驱动的、有主见的研究议程，为软件工程社区提供结构化基础以协调未来工作。

中文摘要：代理型AI的兴起正在以两个交织的方向重塑软件工程：代理越来越多地被应用于支持软件工程任务，而代理型AI系统本身也是复杂的系统，需要重新思考当前已建立的软件工程实践。为了绘制涵盖这两个方向的连贯研究议程，我们在里约热内卢组织了A2SE研讨会，汇集了来自学术界和工业界的18位专家。通过结构化演示、协作主题聚类和聚焦小组讨论，参与者确定了六个主题领域：治理、面向代理的软件工程、面向软件架构的代理、质量与评估、可持续性以及代码，并为每个领域优先排序了短期和长期研究方向。本文介绍了由此产生的社区驱动、有主见的研究议程，为SE社区在此关键时刻协调努力提供了结构化基础。

Original abstract: The rise of agentic AI is reshaping software engineering in two intertwined directions: agents are increasingly applied to support software engineering tasks, and Agentic AI systems themselves are complex systems that require re-thinking currently established software engineering practices. To chart a coherent research agenda covering the two directions, we organized the A2SE seminar in Rio de Janeiro, bringing together 18 experts from academia and industry. Through structured presentations, collaborative topic clustering, and focused group discussions, participants identified six thematic areas: Governance, Software Engineering for Agents, Agents for Software Architecture, Quality and Evaluation, Sustainability, and Code, and they prioritized short-term and long-term research directions for each. This paper presents the resulting community-driven, opinionated research agenda, offering the SE community a structured foundation for coordinating efforts at this critical juncture.

</details>


### [4] [Breaking the Dependency Chaos: A Constraint-Driven Python Dependency Resolution Strategy with Selective LLM Imputation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11772v1)
*Kowshik Chowdhury,Dipayan Banik,Shazibul Islam Shamim*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出SMT-LLM，一种结合形式约束求解与LLM的混合系统，在Python依赖解析中显著提升准确率和速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Python生态系统中依赖解析任务因版本不兼容、弃用包和元数据缺失而极具挑战，现有LLM方法效率低、精度不足。

Method: SMT-LLM使用AST分析、vermin工具和五级导入解析器进行确定性提取，构建约束图并通过Z3 SMT求解器求解一致版本。

Result: 在HG2.9K基准上，SMT-LLM解析率83.6%（对比PLLM的54.8%），中位时间减少6.3倍，LLM调用减少11倍。

Conclusion: 混合形式求解与LLM的方法能更有效、更高效地解决Python依赖解析问题。

中文摘要：依赖解析是选择可以一起安装而不发生冲突的软件包版本的任务。它在现代软件项目中占据了构建失败的很大一部分。在Python生态系统中，由于Python 2/3不兼容、已弃用的软件包以及大量缺失的元数据，这项任务尤其具有挑战性。最近的工作，如PLLM，通过使用大型语言模型（LLM）从代码中推断Python和包版本，并根据构建错误迭代修复它们来解决这个问题。我们提出了SMT-LLM，一个混合系统，用形式约束求解替代了仅依赖LLM的版本猜测。SMT-LLM使用确定性导入提取和通过抽象语法树（AST）分析的Python版本检测、vermin工具来推断最低Python版本，以及一个五级导入到包解析器，该解析器在任何LLM调用之前查询PyPI。我们从PyPI元数据和LLM为缺失元数据的包推断的依赖关系构建约束图，然后使用Z3可满足性模理论（SMT）求解器求解一致的版本分配。在使用Gemma2:9B（10 GB VRAM）的HG2.9K基准测试中，SMT-LLM解析了83.6%的代码片段，而PLLM为54.8%，同时将中位解析时间从151.5秒减少到23.9秒（快6.3倍），每个片段的平均LLM调用次数从约24.9次减少到2.26次（减少11倍）。

Original abstract: Dependency resolution is the task of selecting package versions that can be installed together without conflicts. It accounts for a significant share of build failures in modern software projects. In the Python ecosystem, this task is especially challenging due to Python 2/3 incompatibilities, deprecated packages, and widespread missing metadata. Recent work, such as PLLM, tackles this problem by using large language models (LLMs) to infer Python and package versions from code and iteratively repairing them based on build errors. We present SMT-LLM, a hybrid system that replaces LLM-only version guessing with formal constraint solving. SMT-LLM uses deterministic import extraction and Python version detection via abstract syntax tree (AST) analysis, the vermin tool to infer minimum Python versions, and a five-tier import-to-package resolver that queries PyPI before any LLM call. We construct a constraint graph from PyPI metadata and LLM-imputed dependencies for packages with missing metadata, then solve for consistent version assignments using a Z3 satisfiability modulo theories (SMT) solver. On the HG2.9K benchmark using Gemma2:9B (10 GB VRAM), SMT-LLM resolves 83.6% of snippets compared to PLLM's 54.8%, while reducing median resolution time from 151.5 s to 23.9 s (6.3x faster) and average LLM calls from ~24.9 to 2.26 per snippet (11x reduction).

</details>


### [5] [An Extensive Replication Study of the ABLoTS Approach for Bug Localization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11790v1)
*Feifei Niu,Enshuo Zhang,Christoph Mayr-Dorn,Wesley Klewerton Guez Assunção,Liguo Huang,Jidong Ge,Bin Luo,Alexander Egyed*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 对ABLoTS方法的复制研究发现其核心组件TraceScore在扩展数据集上表现良好，但由于错误截止日期导致的数据泄露，无法重现原始论文结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了评估ABLoTS方法结果的准确性，并深入了解其在实际应用中的适用性。

Method: 使用原始数据集及两个扩展数据集（额外的Java和Python项目）对ABLoTS方法进行复制研究。

Result: TraceScore组件在扩展数据集上产生了可比较甚至更好的结果，但由于错误选择截止日期导致测试数据泄露到训练数据中，无法重现原始论文中报告的结果。

Conclusion: 错误截止日期导致的数据泄露是影响ABLoTS结果重现性的关键因素，该副作用对性能有显著影响。

中文摘要：Bug定位是一项推荐源代码位置（通常是文件）的任务，这些位置包含导致Bug的原因，因此需要修改以修复Bug。沿着这一思路，基于信息检索的Bug定位（IRBL）方法已被采用，这些方法从源代码空间中识别最易出现Bug的文件。目前，一系列最先进的IRBL技术利用不同组件（如相似报告、版本历史和代码结构）的组合来实现更好的性能。ABLoTS是最近提出的一种方法，其核心组件TraceScore利用需求以及不同问题报告（即功能请求和Bug报告）之间的可追溯性信息来识别有Bug的源代码片段，并取得了有希望的结果。为了评估这些结果的准确性，并深入了解ABLoTS的实际适用性，我们使用原始数据集以及两个扩展数据集（即额外的Java数据集和Python数据集）对该方法进行了复制研究。原始数据集包含11个开源Java项目，共8,494个Bug报告。扩展的Java数据集包括另外16个项目，包含25,893个Bug报告以及相应的源代码提交。扩展的Python数据集包括12个项目，共1,289个Bug报告。我们发现，ABLoTS的核心组件TraceScore在扩展数据集上产生了可比较甚至更好的结果，但我们也发现，由于一个被忽视的副作用（错误地选择了截止日期，导致测试数据泄露到训练数据中，对性能产生了显著影响），我们无法重现ABLoTS在其原始论文中报告的结果。

Original abstract: Bug localization is the task of recommending source code locations (typically files) that contain the cause of a bug and hence need to be changed to fix the bug. Along these lines, information retrieval-based bug localization (IRBL) approaches have been adopted, which identify the most bug-prone files from the source code space. In current practice, a series of state-of-the-art IRBL techniques leverage the combination of different components (e.g., similar reports, version history, and code structure) to achieve better performance. ABLoTS is a recently proposed approach with the core component, TraceScore, that utilizes requirements and traceability information between different issue reports (i.e., feature requests and bug reports) to identify buggy source code snippets with promising results. To evaluate the accuracy of these results and obtain additional insights into the practical applicability of ABLoTS, we conducted a replication study of this approach with the original dataset and also on two extended datasets (i.e., additional Java dataset and Python dataset). The original dataset consists of 11 open source Java projects with 8,494 bug reports. The extended Java dataset includes 16 more projects comprising 25,893 bug reports and corresponding source code commits. The extended Python dataset consists of 12 projects with 1,289 bug reports. While we find that the TraceScore component, which is the core of ABLoTS, produces comparable or even better results with the extended datasets, we also find that we cannot reproduce the ABLoTS results, as reported in its original paper, due to an overlooked side effect of incorrectly choosing a cut-off date that led to test data leaking into training data with significant effects on performance.

</details>


### [6] [The Death Spiral of Open Source Projects: A Post-Mortem Analysis of Pull Request Workflow Dynamics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11844v1)
*Mohit Kaushik,Kuljit Kaur Chahal*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过对大量GitHub仓库的拉取请求工作流分析，发现项目消亡主要由生态价值和创新驱动，而非工作流效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究主要关注宏观指标，忽略PR工作流微观动态，而本研究旨在填补这一空白，深入理解OSS项目消亡的微观机制。

Method: 采用混合方法量化设计，对1,736个不活跃GitHub仓库及130万个人工PR进行后验分析，包括比较描述性分析、演化分析和解释性建模。

Result: 工作流摩擦和负面情绪是平台固有属性；项目崩溃呈现“死亡螺旋”模式；项目寿命由流行度和创新预测，而非工作流效率。

Conclusion: OSS项目消亡是社会技术现象，主要由生态系统价值和放弃驱动，PR工作流纪律是次要因素。

中文摘要：开源软件项目（OSS）是现代技术的核心，但其存活率仍然很低。以往研究通过宏观指标（如提交活动、开发者放弃和生态系统依赖）考察项目消亡，但拉取请求（PR）工作流的微观动态在很大程度上被忽视。本研究首次对1,736个不活跃的GitHub仓库和130万个由人驱动的PR进行了大规模的后验分析。采用混合方法的量化设计，我们从三个维度探讨项目消亡。首先，我们的比较描述性分析表明，工作流摩擦、延长的审查周期和负面惩罚是GitHub平台整体的固有属性，无论项目健康与否。被拒绝的PR始终吸引更多的讨论和负面情绪。其次，我们的演化分析识别出一个普遍的“死亡螺旋”，表现为创新率下降、积压呈指数增长、合并延迟上升。崩溃以沉默和脱离为特征。标签形式化在整个生命周期中普遍存在，而毒性并未加剧。最后，我们的解释性建模表明，项目寿命并非由工作流效率决定，而是由内在价值和生态系统动态决定。流行度和创新成为生存的强正向预测因子，而摩擦、拒绝率、标签形式化和负面情绪随寿命增长，是失败的结果而非原因。对不同不活跃阈值的稳健性检验证实了这些发现。总之，这项工作将OSS消亡重新定义为一个社会技术现象，其中放弃和生态系统价值主导生存结果，而PR级别的工作流纪律起次要作用。

Original abstract: Open Source Software projects (OSS) are central to modern technology, yet their survival rates remain low. Prior research has examined project mortality through macro-level indicators such as commit activity, developer abandonment, and ecosystem dependencies, but the micro-level dynamics of the Pull Request (PR) workflow have been largely overlooked. This study provides the first large-scale post-mortem analysis of PR workflows across 1,736 inactive GitHub repositories and 1.3 million human-driven PRs. Using a mixed-method quantitative design, we investigate three dimensions of mortality. First, our comparative descriptive analysis shows that workflow friction, extended review cycles, and negativity penalties are endemic properties of the entire GitHub platform across both active and inactive projects. Rejected PRs consistently attract higher discussion and negativity regardless of project health. Second, our evolutionary analysis identifies a universal ``death spiral" marked by declining innovation rates, exponential backlog growth, rising merge latency. The collapse was defined by silence and disengagement. Labeling formalization remained endemic throughout the lifecycle, while toxicity did not intensify. Finally, our explanatory modeling demonstrates that project lifespan is not determined by workflow efficiency but by inherent value and ecosystem dynamics. Popularity and innovation emerge as strong positive predictors of survival, while friction, rejection rates, labeling formalization, and negativity scale with longevity as byproducts rather than causes of failure. Robustness checks across alternative inactivity thresholds confirm these findings. Together, this work reframes OSS mortality as a socio-technical phenomenon in which abandonment and ecosystem value dominate survival outcomes, while PR-level workflow discipline plays a secondary role.

</details>


### [7] [SemChunk-C: Semantic Segmentation for C Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23697v1)
*Boris Nazarov,Darya Frolova,Shaked Leibzirer,Pavel Kisilev*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出针对C族语言的轻量级语义分块模型SemChunk-C，通过LLM分类器实现灵活边界和功能属性分配，在边界准确性和语义连贯性上优于或匹敌大模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分块方法无法有效捕获C族语言中的语义单元，限制了下游任务性能，需要一种能适应复杂语法和宏的语义分块方法。

Method: 定义代码块类别，训练LLM分类器同时识别块边界和分配功能属性；基于Ettin编码器构建轻量级模型SemChunk-C（17M-150M参数），利用LLM语义理解实现灵活分块。

Result: 在多个数据集上，SemChunk-C在边界准确性、语义连贯性上匹配或超越基于大型LLM的分块器，并在下游任务基准上验证了改进性能。

Conclusion: 本文证明了轻量级模型能够有效进行C族语言语义分块，灵活边界方法优于传统固定或语法方法，为高效代码理解提供了新途径。

中文摘要：C族语言的代码语义分割仍然是一个具有挑战性的问题，原因在于该语言复杂的语法、宏展开以及不规律的结构模式。现有的分块方法，如固定大小窗口、启发式分割和基于句法的工具，往往无法捕获有意义的函数单元，限制了检索和其他下游LLM驱动任务的效果。本文解决了C相关语言中的分块问题。首先，我们定义了一组代码块类别。其次，我们训练了一个基于LLM的分类器，用于a)识别块边界，b)为每个块分配一个描述性的功能属性（类别），这对下游任务很有用。通过利用LLM捕获代码中语义上下文的能力，我们采用灵活的分块边界，使其能够适应每个实例的特定结构和上下文。第三，我们介绍了SemChunk-C，一组轻量级语言模型，用于C相关文件（.c, .cpp, .h, .cs等）的语义分块。这些模型基于前四个Ettin编码器[1]，参数分别为17M、32M、68M和150M。尽管规模相对较小，但它们能够识别连贯的代码单元，如数据结构、接口块和其他组件。此外，我们展示了我们的方法在真实世界代码上的鲁棒性，包括嵌套定义和宏等具有挑战性的结构。我们在各种数据集上测试了我们的方法，并显示其在边界准确性和语义连贯性上表现良好，匹配或超越了基于更大代码导向LLM的分块器。我们还通过在几个精选基准上验证了下游任务的改进性能。

Original abstract: Semantic segmentation of code written in a C-family language remains a challenging problem, due to the language's complex syntax, macro expansion, and irregular structural patterns. Existing chunking methods, such as fixed-sized windows, heuristic splitting, and syntax-based tools, often fail to capture meaningful functional units, limiting the efficacy of retrieval and other downstream LLM driven tasks.
  In this paper, we address the problem of chunking in C-related languages. First, we define a set of code chunk categories. Second, we train an LLM-based classifier to a) identify chunk boundaries, and b) assign each chunk a descriptive functional attribute (a category), which can be useful for downstream tasks. By leveraging the LLM's ability to capture semantic context within the code, we assume flexible chunk boundaries, allowing to adapt to the specific structure and context of each instance. Third, we introduce SemChunk-C, a family of lightweight language models for semantic chunking of C-related files (.c, .cpp, .h, .cs, etc.). These models are based on the first four Ettin encoders [1] with 17M, 32M, 68M, and 150M parameters. Despite their relatively small size, they are capable of identifying cohesive code units, such as data structures, interface blocks, and other components. Furthermore, we demonstrate the robustness of our approach on real-world code, including challenging constructs such as nested definitions and macros.
  We test our approach on various datasets, and show that it achieves high boundary accuracy and semantic coherence, matching or outperforming chunkers that are based on much larger code-oriented LLMs. We also validate the improved performance of the downstream tasks on a few curated benchmarks.

### [8] [StepCodeReasoner: Aligning Code Reasoning with Stepwise Execution Traces via Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11922v1)
*Hao Wang,Rui Li,Lei Sha,Jie M. Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: StepCodeReasoner通过引入中间执行状态监督和双层GRPO强化学习，在代码推理中取得SOTA，7B模型超越多项基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有代码推理方法仅监督最终输出，忽略中间状态，易导致奖励黑客问题。

Method: 提出StepCodeReasoner框架，自动插入执行轨迹锚点进行逐步状态预测，并设计Bi-Level GRPO算法进行轨迹间和轨迹内的结构化信用分配。

Result: 7B模型在CRUXEval达91.1%，LiveCodeBench达86.5%，REval达82.9%，均超越基线和GPT-4o。

Conclusion: 显式执行建模有效提升代码推理和代码生成性能。

中文摘要：现有的代码推理方法主要监督最终代码输出，忽略中间状态，常常导致奖励黑客行为，即通过不一致的推理获得正确答案。我们提出了StepCodeReasoner，一个引入显式中间执行状态监督的框架。通过自动将结构化的基于打印的执行轨迹锚点插入代码中，模型被训练为预测每一步的运行时状态，将代码推理转化为可验证的逐步执行建模问题。基于这种执行感知方法，我们引入了Bi-Level GRPO，一种用于在两层进行结构化信用分配的强化学习算法：轨迹间，比较替代执行路径；轨迹内，根据中间准确性对下游正确性的影响进行奖励。大量实验表明，StepCodeReasoner在代码推理中达到了最先进的性能。特别是，我们的7B模型在CRUXEval上达到91.1%，在LiveCodeBench上达到86.5%，优于CodeReasoner-7B基线（86.0%和77.7%）和GPT-4o（85.6%和75.1%）。此外，在执行轨迹基准REval上，我们的模型得分为82.9%，优于基线CodeReasoner-7B（72.3%）、其14B对应版本（81.1%）和GPT-4o（77.3%）。另外，我们的方法还提高了代码生成性能，表明显式执行建模同时增强了代码推理和代码生成。

Original abstract: Existing code reasoning methods primarily supervise final code outputs, ignoring intermediate states, often leading to reward hacking where correct answers are obtained through inconsistent reasoning. We propose StepCodeReasoner, a framework that introduces explicit intermediate execution-state supervision. By automatically inserting structured print-based execution-trace anchors into code, the model is trained to predict runtime states at each step, transforming code reasoning into a verifiable, stepwise execution modeling problem. Building on this execution-aware method, we introduce Bi-Level GRPO, a reinforcement learning algorithm for structured credit assignment at two levels: inter-trajectory, comparing alternative execution paths, and intra-trajectory, rewarding intermediate accuracy based on its impact on downstream correctness. Extensive experiments demonstrate that StepCodeReasoner achieves SOTA performance in code reasoning. In particular, our 7B model achieves 91.1\% on CRUXEval and 86.5\% on LiveCodeBench, outperforming the CodeReasoner-7B baseline (86.0\% and 77.7\%) and GPT-4o (85.6\% and 75.1\%). Furthermore, on the execution-trace benchmark REval, our model scores 82.9\%, outperforming baseline CodeReasoner-7B (72.3\%), its 14B counterpart (81.1\%), and GPT-4o (77.3\%). Additionally, our approach also improves code generation performance, demonstrating that explicit execution modeling enhances both code reasoning and code generation.

</details>


### [9] [Neural Code Translation of Legacy Code: APL to C#](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13896v1)
*Abdulrahman Ramadan,Hanen Borchani,Iben Lilholm,Mikkel Almind,Allan Peter Engsig-Karup*

中文摘要：编程语言之间的自动翻译仍然是一个具有挑战性的问题，特别是当源语言高度简洁且专业化时。本文研究了使用大语言模型将APL翻译为C#。由于APL稀疏的语法、大规模并行语料库的缺乏以及解释APL程序所需的专业知识，这项任务十分困难。为了应对这些挑战，我们引入了一个新颖的APL到C#翻译框架，通过比较三种引导策略，即自然语言描述中介、检索增强和迭代细化，与基线直接翻译模型进行对比。我们构建了多个功能等价代码对的数据集，涵盖不同复杂程度，并为了严格评估翻译质量，开发了一个自动化评估流水线，验证生成的C#代码的语法编译和功能执行。我们的结果表明，神经代码翻译能够成功弥合APL与C#之间的差距，适用于各种程序，并且引入额外的上下文和引导显著提高了模型性能。

Original abstract: Automatic translation between programming languages remains a challenging problem, particularly when the source language is highly concise and specialized. This paper investigates the translation of APL into C# using large language models. The task is difficult due to APL's sparse syntax, the scarcity of large-scale parallel corpora, and the requirement for specialized knowledge to interpret APL programs. To address these challenges, we introduce a novel framework for APL-to-C# translation by comparing three guided strategies, namely natural language description-mediated, retrieval-augmented, and iterative refinement, against a baseline direct translation model. We constructed multiple datasets of functionally equivalent code pairs spanning various levels of complexity, and to rigorously assess translation quality, we developed an automated evaluation pipeline that verifies both syntactic compilation and functional execution of the generated C# code. Our results demonstrate that neural code translation can successfully bridge the gap between APL and C# for a wide range of programs, and that incorporating additional context and guidance significantly improves model performance.

### [10] [Property-Level Reconstructability of Agent Decisions: An Anchor-Level Pilot Across Vendor SDK Adapter Regimes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12078v1)
*Oleg Solozobov*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究提出决策追踪重构器，应用于六个供应商SDK体制，发现代理决策属性的可重构性因体制而异，严格治理完整性在42.9%到85.7%之间。

  <summary>Details</summary>

中文摘要：智能代理AI的失败需要事后重构：代理做了什么、基于谁的授权、违反了哪项政策、以及基于什么推理。跨体制的可行性仍未在一个属性级模式中得到衡量。我们将未经修改的决策追踪重构器应用于来自六个公开供应商SDK体制（涵盖云代理、可观测性、工具使用、遥测和协议追踪，加上两个比较列）的固定工作示例锚点。每个决策事件模式（DES）属性被分类为完全可填充、部分可填充、结构上不可填充或不透明。在此锚点规模下，代理决策的每个属性的可重构性已经因体制而异。严格治理完整性分为三个层级，范围从42.9%到85.7%，产生一个体制无关的缺口（推理轨迹）、四个体制相关的缺口和一个混合属性；该试点是单标注者、每单元一个锚点、描述性的，输出可从存储的可复现包中进行校验和验证。

Original abstract: Agentic AI failures need post-hoc reconstruction: what the agent did, on whose authority, against which policy, and from what reasoning. Cross-regime feasibility remains unmeasured under one property-level schema. We apply the Decision Trace Reconstructor unmodified to pinned worked-example anchors from six public vendor SDK regimes spanning cloud-agent, observability, tool-use, telemetry, and protocol traces, plus two comparator columns. Each Decision Event Schema (DES) property is classified as fully fillable, partially fillable, structurally unfillable, or opaque. Per-property reconstructability of an agent decision already varies between regimes at this anchor scale. Strict-governance-completeness separates into three tiers ranging from 42.9% to 85.7%, yielding one regime-independent gap (reasoning trace), four regime-dependent gaps, and one Mixed property; the pilot is single-annotator, one anchor per cell, descriptive, with outputs checksum-verifiable from a deposited reproducibility package.

### [11] [HM-Req: A Framework for Embedding Values within CPS Human Monitoring Requirements](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12100v2)
*Zoe Pfister,Ruth Breu,Michael Vierhauser*

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类价值观在需求工程中常被忽略，自然语言需求存在歧义，导致伦理和隐私问题。

Method: HM-Req框架包括受控自然语言（CNL）用于定义人类监控需求，通过价值仪表盘整合利益相关者价值观并检测冲突。

Result: 应用CNL到不同数据集及调查、专家访谈表明CNL能捕获多样化需求，且HM-Req对需求获取有用。

中文摘要：监控人类，例如他们的移动或位置，对于信息物理系统（CPS）中安全高效的人机协作至关重要。这些信息使CPS能够确保安全属性、动态调整其行为并与人类协调。为确保CPS的设计尊重伦理原则及其利益相关者的隐私，系统需求（特别是与人类监控相关的）必须反映所有相关利益相关者的人类价值观。然而，人类价值观在软件工程中往往代表性不足——尤其是在需求获取和系统设计这些引入伦理关键功能的关键阶段。利益相关者的价值观通常是隐含且相互冲突的，但很少被系统地捕获。此外，非结构化的自然语言需求引入了歧义和模糊性，使冲突解决复杂化。为解决这些问题，我们提出了HM-Req，一个需求获取框架，包括一个用于定义人类监控需求的受控自然语言（CNL）。这些需求随后被来自相关利益相关者的人类价值观增强，并整合到一个价值仪表盘中，以检测需要进一步讨论和解决的潜在冲突。将CNL应用于不同数据集、进行一项调查和专家访谈的验证结果，提供了CNL能够捕获多样化人类监控需求的证据，并证明了HM-Req在需求获取活动中的有用性。

Original abstract: Monitoring humans, for example, their movement or location, is essential for safe and efficient human-machine collaboration in Cyber-Physical Systems (CPS). This information allows CPS to ensure safety properties, adapt their behaviour dynamically, and coordinate with humans. To ensure that the design of a CPS respects ethical principles and the privacy of its stakeholders, system requirements, particularly those related to human monitoring, must reflect the human values of all involved stakeholders. However, human values are often underrepresented in Software Engineering -- particularly during requirements elicitation and system design, crucial phases when introducing ethically critical functionality. Stakeholder values are often implicit and conflicting, yet rarely systematically captured. Furthermore, unstructured natural language requirements introduce ambiguity and vagueness, complicating conflict resolution. To address these problems, we propose HM-Req, a requirements elicitation framework including a Controlled Natural Language (CNL) for defining human monitoring requirements. These requirements are then augmented with human values from relevant stakeholders and integrated into a Value Dashboard to detect potential conflicts that require further discussion and resolution. Validation results, applying the CNL to different datasets and conducting a survey and expert interview, provide evidence of the CNL's ability to capture diverse human monitoring requirements and demonstrate HM-Req's usefulness for requirements elicitation activities.

### [12] [Bidirectional Empowerment of Metamorphic Testing and Large Language Models: A Systematic Survey](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13898v1)
*Zheng Zheng,Zenghui Zhou,Yinwang Xu,Daixu Ren,Tsong Yueh Chen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 系统综述93篇论文，提出蜕变测试（MT）与大型语言模型（LLM）的双向赋能关系，包括MT测试LLM和LLM自动化MT，并构建分类法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM的生成性、概率性特点导致传统测试方法失效，MT虽有前景但人工密集；LLM的语义能力可自动化MT，需系统梳理两者协同。

Method: 系统综述93篇主要研究，提出双向赋能分类法，涵盖MT for LLM和LLM for MT两个互补方向。

Result: 建立了结构化分类，展示了MT在测试LLM各种问题（幻觉、公平性、鲁棒性等）的应用，以及LLM在发现蜕变关系、生成测试输入、实现自动化测试中的作用。

Conclusion: 为理解MT和LLM协同提供基础，指明未来构建更严谨、可扩展、可信赖AI质量保证方法的方向。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）由于其生成性、概率性和开放性的特点，给软件质量保证带来了重大挑战，这加剧了预言家问题并限制了传统测试方法的适用性。蜕变测试（MT）通过检查多个相关执行之间的必要关系而非依赖精确预期输出，已成为测试LLM及其他缺乏预言机系统的有前景方法。同时，LLM强大的语义理解、推理和代码生成能力为自动化传统上劳动密集型的MT阶段创造了新的机会。本综述系统回顾了93项主要研究，并将这种互惠关系描述为MT和LLM的双向赋能。我们提出了一个涵盖两个互补方向的分类法：用于LLM的MT，即使用MT来验证、确认、评估和理解LLM及基于LLM的系统，涉及幻觉、公平性、鲁棒性、代码可靠性、检索增强生成、对话和自主智能体等问题；以及用于MT的LLM，即利用LLM支持蜕变关系发现、输入转换和合成、可执行的测试实现以及智能体闭环测试。通过综合这些发展，本综述为理解MT和LLM之间不断发展的协同效应提供了结构化基础，并强调了构建更严谨、可扩展和可信赖的AI质量保证方法的未来方向。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have introduced substantial challenges to software quality assurance due to their generative, probabilistic, and open-ended nature, which intensifies the oracle problem and limits the applicability of traditional testing methods. Metamorphic testing (MT), which checks necessary relations among multiple related executions rather than relying on exact expected outputs, has emerged as a promising approach for testing LLMs and other oracle-deficient systems. At the same time, the strong semantic understanding, reasoning, and code generation capabilities of LLMs create new opportunities to automate the traditionally labor-intensive phases of MT. This survey systematically reviews 93 primary studies and characterizes this reciprocal relationship as the bidirectional empowerment of MT and LLMs. We propose a taxonomy spanning two complementary directions: MT for LLMs, which uses MT to verify, validate, assess, and understand LLMs and LLM-based systems across issues such as hallucination, fairness, robustness, code reliability, retrieval-augmented generation, dialogue, and autonomous agents; and LLMs for MT, which leverages LLMs to support metamorphic relation discovery, input transformation and synthesis, executable test implementation, and agentic closed-loop testing. By synthesizing these developments, this survey provides a structured foundation for understanding the evolving synergy between MT and LLMs and highlights future directions for building more rigorous, scalable, and trustworthy AI quality assurance methodologies.

</details>


### [13] [It's Not the Size: Harness Design Determines Operational Stability in Small Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12129v1)
*Yong-eun Cho*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过实验比较了不同提示工程水平对小语言模型任务成功率的影响，发现流水线提示显著提升性能，并揭示了支架崩塌现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了提高小语言模型在复杂任务中的操作性能，探索不同级别的提示工程对其影响。

Method: 对三个小语言模型（Gemma4 E2B、Qwen3.5:2B、LLaMA 3.2 3B）应用三种提示工程条件（仅模型、最小外壳、四阶段流水线），在24个任务上比较任务成功率和有效任务成功率。

Result: 流水线提示在Gemma4 E2B上达到最高性能（TSR=0.952, VTSR=1.000）；观察到非单调现象（最小外壳TSR低于仅模型）；LLaMA 3.2 3B在仅模型条件下出现支架崩塌（TSR=0.429）；消融实验表明计划和恢复各贡献约24.7%的增益；VCR为0.625。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，适当的提示工程对于小语言模型执行结构化任务至关重要，简单的包装标签可能适得其反，而流水线框架能有效提升可靠性和格式合规性。

中文摘要：本文实验分析了工程化提示（harness engineering）水平如何影响小语言模型（SLMs，2-3B参数）的操作性能。三种提示工程条件——仅模型（原始提示）、最小外壳（包装标签）和四阶段流水线（计划->执行->验证->恢复）——应用于三个模型（Gemma4 E2B、Qwen3.5:2B、LLaMA 3.2 3B）的24个任务，比较任务成功率（TSR）和有效任务成功率（VTSR）。流水线提示在Gemma4 E2B上（T1-T5，21个任务）实现了TSR=0.952和VTSR=1.000。在两个模型中观察到非单调现象——最小外壳的TSR低于仅模型的TSR。在LLaMA 3.2 3B仅模型条件下，七个格式违规导致TSR=0.429，揭示了支架崩塌：在没有提示工程支持的情况下，模型在复杂格式要求下放弃了JSON结构。消融实验表明，计划和恢复各自贡献了约24.7%的总增益。所有流水线运行中的VCR（验证捕获率）=0.625。

Original abstract: This paper experimentally analyzes how the level of harness engineering affects the operational performance of small language models (SLMs, 2-3B parameters). Three harness conditions - model-only (raw prompt), minimal-shell (wrapper tags), and a 4-stage pipeline (plan->execute->verify->recover) - are applied to three models (Gemma4 E2B, Qwen3.5:2B, LLaMA 3.2 3B) across 24 tasks, comparing Task Success Rate (TSR) and Valid TSR (VTSR). The pipeline harness achieves TSR=0.952 and VTSR=1.000 on Gemma4 E2B (T1-T5, 21 tasks). A non-monotonic phenomenon - minimal-shell TSR < model-only TSR - is observed in two models. In LLaMA 3.2 3B model-only, seven format violations yield TSR=0.429, revealing scaffold collapse: the model abandons JSON structure under complex format requirements without harness support. Ablation shows planning and recovery each contribute approximately 24.7% of total gain. VCR (Verification Catch Rate)=0.625 across all pipeline runs.

</details>

*Vladislav Savenkov*

Method: 通过与12家工业组织建立正式数据共享协议收集代码库，经过结构化合作伙伴加入、两阶段质量选择（自动化元数据过滤+手动代码审查）以及覆盖完整版本历史的确定性匿名化流水线处理。

中文摘要：我们提出了工业开发者仓库精选集（CIDR），这是一个通过与12家工业合作伙伴组织直接合作收集的、包含真实世界软件仓库的大规模数据集。该数据集包含2,440个仓库，涵盖138种编程语言，总计3.73亿行代码，并附有结构化的每个仓库元数据。与源自公共开源平台的现有代码语料库不同，CIDR仅包含在正式数据共享协议下贡献的专有生产代码库，涵盖企业Web和移动开发、金融科技以及定制软件咨询等应用领域。所有仓库都经过了一个多阶段流水线处理，包括结构化的合作伙伴加入、结合自动化元数据过滤和手动代码审查的两阶段质量选择，以及涵盖完整版本控制历史的确定性匿名化流水线。该数据集旨在支持代码智能、软件质量分析、代码语言模型的预训练与微调、开发者行为研究以及智能体评估基准构建等研究。访问在限制性商业许可下提供；详情请访问https://fermatix.ai/#Contact。

Original abstract: We present Curated Industrial Developer Repository (CIDR), a large-scale dataset of real-world software repositories collected through direct collaboration with 12 industrial partner organizations. The dataset comprises 2,440 repositories spanning 138 programming languages and totalling 373 million lines of code, accompanied by structured per-repository metadata. Unlike existing code corpora derived from public open-source platforms, CIDR consists exclusively of proprietary production codebases contributed under formal data sharing agreements, covering application domains including enterprise web and mobile development, fintech, and custom software consultancy. All repositories were processed through a multi-stage pipeline encompassing structured partner onboarding, two-stage quality selection combining automated metadata filtering with manual code review, and a deterministic anonymization pipeline covering the full version control history. The dataset is intended to support research in code intelligence, software quality analysis, pre-training and fine-tuning of code language models, developer behaviour studies, and construction of agent evaluation benchmarks. Access is provided under a restricted commercial license; details are available at https://fermatix.ai/#Contact.

### [15] [ReproBreak: A Dataset of Reproducible Web Locator Breaks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12158v1)
*Thiago Santos de Moura,Leon Adamietz,Samra Mehboob,Yannic Noller*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出了ReproBreak数据集，包含449个可重现的定位器中断，用于评估GUI测试中定位器的脆弱性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前缺乏大规模评估Cypress和Playwright中定位器脆弱性的数据集，而定位器中断严重影响测试维护。

Method: 分析359个开源仓库，识别包含定位器变更的提交，并在定位器变更最多的4个项目中重现确认，最终得到449个定位器中断。

Result: 构建了ReproBreak数据集，包含449个定位器中断和自动重现脚本。

Conclusion: ReproBreak为定位器脆弱性、修复技术和测试健壮性的研究提供了有价值的资源。

中文摘要：自动化的GUI测试框架（如Cypress和Playwright）依赖于定位器来查找并与网页元素进行交互。当被测应用的结构性变化导致定位器无法再找到其目标元素时，就会发生定位器中断，即使底层功能保持不变，也会导致测试失败。尽管这对测试维护有影响，但目前尚无数据集可用于大规模评估Cypress和Playwright中定位器的脆弱性。在本文中，我们提出了ReproBreak，一个可重现的Web应用GUI测试中定位器中断的数据集。我们分析了359个开源仓库，识别出包含定位器变更的提交。为了确认这些变更是否确实是定位器中断，我们在定位器变更数量最多的前4个项目中进行了重现，发现了449个定位器中断，这些中断连同自动重现脚本一起被包含在数据集中。我们相信ReproBreak是一个有价值的资源，可以支持关于定位器脆弱性、修复技术和测试健壮性的研究。视频地址：https://youtu.be/mZByS_TnCvE。数据集地址：https://github.com/rub-sq/ReproBreak。

Original abstract: Automated GUI testing frameworks such as Cypress and Playwright rely on locators to find and interact with web elements. A locator break occurs when a structural change in the application under test causes a locator to no longer find its target element, resulting in test breakages even when the underlying functionality remains unchanged. Despite its impact on test maintenance, no dataset exists to evaluate locator fragility in Cypress and Playwright at scale. In this paper, we present ReproBreak, a dataset of reproducible locator breaks in web application GUI tests. We analyzed 359 open-source repositories to identify commits that contain locator changes. To confirm whether these changes are indeed locator breaks, we reproduced them in the top 4 projects with the largest number of locator changes and found 449 locator breaks, which are provided in the dataset along with scripts for automated reproduction. We believe ReproBreak serves as a valuable artifact to support research on locator fragility, repair techniques, and test robustness. The video is available at: https://youtu.be/mZByS_TnCvE. The dataset is at https://github.com/rub-sq/ReproBreak.

</details>


### [16] [Uncertainty Quantification for LLM-based Code Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12201v1)
*Senrong Xu,Yuhao Tan,Yanke Zhou,Guangyuan Wu,Zenan Li,Yuan Yao,Taolue Chen,Feng Xu,Xiaoxing Ma*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出RisCoSet方法，利用多重假设检验为LLM代码生成构建风险控制预测集，显著降低代码移除率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PAC预测集方法受限于强单调性假设和单标签分类框架，无法适应代码生成中多个有效输出的特性。

Method: 提出RisCoSet，利用多重假设检验为基于LLM的代码生成构建风险控制预测集，输出部分程序作为预测集。

Result: 在三个LLM上实验，相比最先进方法，在相同风险水平下代码移除率降低高达24.5%。

Conclusion: RisCoSet方法有效，能生成保证包含正确解的预测集，并显著减少代码移除。

中文摘要：预测集为量化机器学习模型的不确定性提供了理论框架。将其适应到结构化生成任务，特别是基于大型语言模型（LLM）的代码生成，仍然是一个挑战性问题。现有的一种尝试提出了PAC预测集，但受到其强单调性风险假设和单标签分类框架的限制，严重限制了候选程序的空间，并且无法容纳代码生成固有的多个有效输出。为了解决这些限制，我们提出了一种方法RisCoSet，利用多重假设检验为基于LLM的代码生成构建风险控制预测。给定一个训练好的代码生成模型，我们生成一个由部分程序表示的预测集，保证以高置信度包含一个正确解。在三个LLM上的大量实验证明了所提出方法的有效性。例如，与现有最先进方法相比，我们的方法可以在相同风险水平下将代码移除率降低高达24.5%。

Original abstract: Prediction sets provide a theoretically grounded framework for quantifying uncertainty in machine learning models. Adapting them to structured generation tasks, in particular, large language model (LLM) based code generation, remains a challenging problem. An existing attempt proposes PAC prediction sets but is limited by its strong monotonicity assumption on risk and single-label classification framework, which severely limits the space of candidate programs and cannot accommodate the multiple valid outputs inherent to code generation. To address these limitations, we propose an approach RisCoSet that leverages multiple hypothesis testing to construct risk-controlling predictions for LLM-based code generation. Given a trained code generation model, we produce a prediction set represented by a partial program, which is guaranteed to contain a correct solution with high confidence. Extensive experiments on three LLMs demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method. For instance, compared with the state-of-the-art, our method can significantly reduce the code removal by up to 24.5%, at the same level of risk.

</details>


### [17] [Characterizing the Failure Modes of LLMs in Resolving Real-World GitHub Issues](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12270v1)
*Yanjie Jiang,Yian Huang,Guancheng Wang,Junjie Chen,Hui Liu,Lionel Briand*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文评估了三个LLM在SWE-bench上的失败模式，发现策略制定和逻辑综合是最易出错的阶段，而故障定位表现最好，并提出了缓解策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLM被用于解决GitHub问题，但其具体失败模式尚不明确，需要系统分析以改进。

Method: 在SWE-bench Verified数据集上，对Claude 4.5 Sonnet、Gemini 3 Pro和GPT-5进行900次试验，手动分析243次失败的症状和根本原因，构建分类法。

Result: 故障定位失败率最低，策略制定和逻辑综合失败率最高；模型间鲁棒性和成本差异大；现有评估工具可能误判正确补丁。

Conclusion: 研究表明LLM在故障定位上可能有优势，但策略和逻辑阶段需要改进，同时需注意评估工具的局限性，为提升LLM修复可靠性提供了方向。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被部署用于解决现实世界中的GitHub问题。然而，尽管它们具有潜力，这些模型在复杂修复任务中的具体失败模式仍然鲜为人知。为了描述LLM行为与人类开发者实践的差异，本文评估了三种最先进的模型，即Claude 4.5 Sonnet、Gemini 3 Pro和GPT-5，在SWE-bench Verified数据集上的表现。我们对900次试验中的243次失败尝试进行了严格的手动分析，包括症状和根本原因。我们的研究首先产生了一个统一的失败分类法，涵盖修复流程的五个不同阶段，我们对其中典型的失败症状及其普遍性进行了分类。其次，我们的发现表明，对于所有评估的LLM，策略制定和逻辑综合构成了最容易出错的阶段，其次是问题理解，而定位则表现出最低的失败率。这表明LLM可能在故障定位方面表现出色，而故障定位传统上被认为是自动程序修复中最艰巨的挑战之一。此外，我们观察到鲁棒性和运营成本（特别是在失败场景中）在不同模型之间差异显著。最后，我们揭示了这些失败的根本原因，并提出了可行的缓解策略。一个特别显著的发现是，现有的评估工具偶尔会因表面差异或隐藏约束而误判正确的补丁。总的来说，我们的见解可能为增强基于LLM的问题解决的有效性和可靠性提供有希望的方向。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed to resolve real-world GitHub issues. However, despite their potential, the specific failure modes of these models in complex repair tasks remain poorly understood. To characterize how LLM behavior diverges from human developer practices, this paper evaluates three state-of-the-art models, i.e., Claude 4.5 Sonnet, Gemini 3 Pro, and GPT-5, on the SWE-bench Verified dataset. We conduct a rigorous manual analysis of the symptoms and root causes underlying 243 failed attempts across 900 total trials. Our investigation first yields a unified failure taxonomy encompassing five distinct stages of the repair pipeline, within which we categorize typical failure symptoms and their prevalence. Secondly, our findings reveal that for all evaluated LLMs, strategy formulation and logic synthesis constitutes the most error-prone stage, followed by problem understanding, whereas localization exhibits the lowest failure rate. This suggests that LLMs may excel at fault localization, a task traditionally regarded as one of the most formidable challenges in automated program repair. Furthermore, we observe that robustness and operational costs (particularly in failure scenarios) vary significantly across different models. Finally, we uncover the root causes of these failures and propose actionable strategies to mitigate them. A particularly notable finding is that existing evaluation harnesses occasionally misjudge correct patches due to superficial discrepancies or hidden constraints. Collectively, our insights may provide promising directions for enhancing the effectiveness and reliability of LLM-based issue resolution.

</details>


### [18] [Minimalistic Terminal Editor for Julia Programming -- MinTEJ: A Friendly Approach for a Scientific Programmer](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12275v1)
*Poornachandratejasvi Laxman Bhattar,Payal V. Dahiwale,Krishnarjunulu Thota,Anurag Sharma*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: MinTEJ是一个基于终端的Julia编辑器，通过顺序模态交互架构（SMIA）统一了编辑、执行、文件管理和调试，相比VS Code和Notepad++具有更低的内存和CPU开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具对Julia集成工作流支持有限，导致上下文切换和碎片化交互，需要轻量级的终端原生编辑器。

Method: 提出了MinTEJ和SMIA架构，其中缓冲区为中心数据结构，中央控制器管理模式顺序转换，实现命令式工作流。

Result: 性能基准测试显示MinTEJ在内存消耗和CPU利用率上低于VS Code和Notepad++。

Conclusion: 集成终端编辑器环境是实用的轻量级工具，支持高效迭代开发。

中文摘要：开发者依赖轻量级、以终端为中心的工作流以实现快速的代码迭代。然而，在Julia编程语言的统一环境中，现有工具对集成工作流（如编辑、执行、文件管理和调试）的支持有限。因此，开发者经常面临上下文切换开销和碎片化的工具交互。因此，所提出的工作主要侧重于为Julia编程语言开发原生终端编辑器的极简方法。本文介绍了MinTEJ，一个用Julia构建的基于终端的编辑器，并提出了一个顺序模态交互架构（SMIA），通过面向命令的工作流统一了文件管理、代码编辑、执行和调试。所提出的工作形式化了模态交互，并减少了在不同模式间转换时的认知负荷和错误。在SMIA中，缓冲区是跨所有模式持久化的中心数据结构。每个模式根据模式特定规则解释和操作缓冲区。中央控制器调解对缓冲区的访问并强制模式之间的顺序转换。为了评估该方法，将MinTEJ的性能基准与现有工具（即VS Code和Notepad++）进行比较。基于内存消耗和CPU利用率评估所提出的MinTEJ的有效性，表明其资源开销更少。研究结果表明，集成化的基于终端的编辑器环境是一种实用的轻量级软件工具，能够实现高效的迭代开发。

Original abstract: Developers rely on lightweight, terminal-centric workflows for rapid code iteration. However, within a unified environment for Julia programming language, existing tools provide limited support for integrated workflow such as editing, execution, file management, and debugging. As a result, developers frequently incur context-switching overhead and fragmented tool interactions. Therefore, the proposed work predominantly focuses on the minimalistic approach for developing native terminal editor for Julia programming language. This paper introduces MinTEJ, a terminal-based editor built in Julia, and proposes a Sequential Modal Interaction Architecture (SMIA) that unifies file management, code editing, execution, and debugging through a command-oriented workflow. The presented work formalizes model interaction and reduces cognitive load & errors while transitioning among different modes. In SMIA, buffer is the central data structure that persists across all modes. Each mode interprets and manipulates the buffer according to mode-specific rules. The central controller mediates access to the buffer and enforces sequential transitions between modes. To evaluate the approach, the performance benchmarking of MinTEJ is compared against existing tools i.e., VS code and Notepad++. The effectiveness of the proposed MinTEJ is evaluated based on memory consumption and CPU utilization demonstrating that it has less resource overhead. Findings suggest that integrated terminal-based editor environment is a practical lightweight software tool enabling efficient iterative development.

### [19] [Iterative Audit Convergence in LLM-Managed Multi-Agent Systems: A Case Study in Prompt-Engineering Quality Assurance](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12280v2)
*Elias Calboreanu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 对AEGIS系统进行九轮迭代审计，发现51个一致性缺陷，提出七类别分类法和锁定审计协议，并通过跨LLM面板和评分者间信度检查验证了方法有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体LLM系统的提示规范缺乏结构化检查，导致数据合约和集成逻辑中的一致性问题未被系统发现。

Method: 采用迭代代理驱动审计方法，对AEGIS系统进行九轮审计；事后建立七类别分类法；通过跨LLM面板（4个供应商）和评分者间信度检查（Cohen's κ）进行部分复制验证。

Result: 共发现51个一致性缺陷（每轮递减）；分类法明确；跨LLM面板检测出全部5个植入缺陷；评分者间信度在类别上κ=0.80，严重性上κ=0.46。

Conclusion: 该审计协议和分类法为多智能体LLM系统提供可重复的结构化检查方法，完整可重复性包已提交。

中文摘要：多智能体大型语言模型系统的提示规范在不同文件之间承载数据合约和集成逻辑，但很少接受结构化检查的严格审查。我们报告了一个单系统案例研究，对AEGIS（自主工程治理与智能系统）进行迭代、代理驱动的审计，这是一个七通道生产流水线，其7152行规范表面经过九轮审计，发现了51个一致性缺陷（每轮数量：15、8、12、2、8、1、4、1、0）。我们提出了一个具有明确编码规则的七类别事后分类法，非单调收敛（与级联编辑和审计范围扩展一致），以及一个锁定审计协议。我们还报告了在公共合成迷你规范上的两个部分复制：一个由四个前沿供应商（OpenAI、Anthropic、Google、xAI）组成的跨LLM小组（12条轨迹；多供应商联合检测所有五个植入缺陷），以及一个对分层子样本的评分者间信度检查（Cohen's κ = 0.80 在类别上，0.46 在严重性上）。完整的可重复性包随提交一同提供。

Original abstract: Prompt specifications for multi-agent large language model (LLM) systems carry data contracts and integration logic across interdependent files but are rarely subjected to structured-inspection rigor. We report a single-system case study of iterative, agent-driven auditing applied to AEGIS (Autonomous Engineering Governance and Intelligence System), a seven-lane production pipeline whose 7152-line specification surface was audited across nine rounds, surfacing 51 consistency defects (per-round counts of 15, 8, 12, 2, 8, 1, 4, 1, 0). We present a seven-category post hoc taxonomy with explicit coding rules, non-monotonic convergence consistent with cascading edits and audit-scope expansion, and a locked audit protocol. We further report two partial replications on a public synthetic mini-specification: a cross-LLM panel of four frontier vendors (OpenAI, Anthropic, Google, xAI; 12 traces; multi-vendor union detects all five seeded defects) and an inter-rater reliability check on a stratified subsample (Cohen's $κ$ = 0.80 on category, 0.46 on severity). The full reproducibility bundle accompanies the submission.

</details>


### [20] [Fine-Tuning Models for Automated Code Review Feedback](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12610v1)
*Smitha S Kumar,Michael A Lones,Manuel Maarek,Hind Zantout*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 论文研究了通过参数高效微调（PEFT）和提示工程提升开源LLM Code Llama的反馈质量，发现PEFT显著优于提示工程，且学生认为其反馈与ChatGPT同样有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 专有模型用于编程教育反馈存在成本、计算需求和伦理问题，开源LLM能力不足，因此需要探索改进开源模型反馈质量的方法。

Method: 使用参数高效微调（PEFT）和提示工程两种技术，从大型模型生成的数据集中提取知识，调整Code Llama；通过学生评估、人工标注和自动指标（BLEU, ROUGE, BERTScore）评估对有缺陷Java代码的反馈质量。

Result: PEFT显著提升反馈质量，优于提示工程；学生认为PEFT模型反馈与ChatGPT同样有效；建议添加技术术语解释。

Conclusion: 微调模型能有效支持批判性思维并指导可扩展教学系统的设计。

中文摘要：大型语言模型通过个性化支持、内容创建和自动反馈为编程教育引入了新的可能性。虽然最近的研究已经展示了反馈生成的潜力，但许多技术依赖于专有模型，引发了对成本、计算需求以及共享学生代码的伦理影响的担忧。开源LLM提供了一种替代方法，但它们目前不具备专有模型的能力。为了解决这个问题，我们研究了参数高效微调（PEFT）和提示工程，两者都从源自更大、更强模型的数据集中提取知识，是否可以用于调整和增强开源LLM Code Llama生成的反馈质量。使用学生评估、人工标注以及自动指标BLEU、ROUGE和BERTScore的组合来评估对有缺陷的Java代码的反馈质量。我们的发现表明，PEFT显著提高了反馈质量，并且明显优于提示工程，为开发可自由部署的反馈工具提供了途径，这些工具可以有效地用于指导学生学习。学生评估表明，学习者重视PEFT模型的反馈，并认为其与专有的ChatGPT模型同样有效。参与者建议在PEFT模型的反馈中加入对技术术语的额外解释可能更有益。这项研究表明，微调模型可以有效支持批判性思维并指导可扩展教学系统的设计。

Original abstract: Large Language Models have introduced new possibilities for programming education through personalized support, content creation, and automated feedback. While recent studies have demonstrated the potential for feedback generation, many techniques rely on proprietary models, raising concerns about cost, computational demands, and the ethical implications of sharing student code. Open LLMs provide an alternative approach, but they do not currently have the capabilities of proprietary models. To address this problem, we investigate whether parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) and prompt engineering, both of which distil knowledge from a dataset derived from a large, more capable model, can be used to adapt and enhance the quality of feedback generated by the open LLM Code Llama. Feedback quality on buggy Java code was assessed using a combination of student evaluation, manual annotation and the automated metrics BLEU, ROUGE, and BERTScore. Our findings indicate that PEFT leads to notable improvements in feedback quality and significantly outperforms prompt engineering, providing an avenue for developing freely deployable feedback tools that can be effectively used to guide student learning. Student evaluation indicates that learners value the PEFT model's feedback and see it as being equally effective as the proprietary ChatGPT model. Participants suggested that incorporating additional explanation for technical terms in the PEFT model's feedback could be more beneficial. This study demonstrates that fine-tuned models can effectively support critical thinking and guide the design of scalable pedagogical systems.

</details>


### [21] [User Reviews as a Source for Usability Requirements: A Precursor Study on Using Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12657v1)
*Cedric Wellhausen,Laura Reinhardt,Kurt Schneider*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 研究LLM在识别用户评论中的可用性需求方面的性能，与人类评分员比较，并构建了数据集和提示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统ML/DL方法需要大量标注数据，成本高；LLM预训练在用户文本上，可能提供更高效的用户中心需求分析。

Method: 收集300条用户评论，由人类和LLM标注；基于尼尔森启发式构建提示；比较性能。

Result: LLM能够识别可用性需求，但性能依赖提示。

Conclusion: LLM可用于快速低成本的需求分析，但提示设计关键。

中文摘要：已知在需求工程中采用以用户为中心的方法通常会为最终用户带来更合适的产品。LLM4RE为支持需求获取过程（例如需求分类）提供了有前景的方法。以往的方法侧重于机器学习或深度学习方面，需要大量人工标注的数据进行密集训练。而LLM在大规模用户生成的文本数据上进行了预训练，使得以用户为中心的工作流能够分析需求。在本文中，我们探索利用LLM改进的自然语言理解（而非严格的机器学习分类）结合用户评论的大规模提取，来分析LLM在理解用户评论方面的性能是否与人类评分员相当。这使得开发团队能够快速且低成本地收集和处理用户需求。本文有三个主要贡献：（1）我们提供了一个完全编码的300条用户评论数据集，包含来自三种不同类型应用的可用性相关方面，由两名人类评分员和一名LLM标注。（2）基于两次提示工程迭代和根据10条尼尔森可用性启发式制定的编码指南，我们构建了一个初始提示，用于LLM过滤可用性相关的用户评论。（3）我们确定LLM通常能够识别用户评论中的可用性作为非功能性需求（基于F值），但性能和可靠性强烈依赖于提示。

Original abstract: It is known that user-centered approaches to requirements engineering in general lead to a better suited product for the end-users. LLM4RE provides promising approaches to support the requirements elicitation process (e.g. classification of requirements). Previous approaches focus on Machine-Learning (ML) or Deep-Learning (DL) aspects, which require intensive training with a large amount of manually labeled data. LLMs, on the other hand, are pre-trained on large amounts of user-generated text data, enabling a user-centric workflow to analyze requirements. In this paper, we explore the possibility of exploiting the improved natural language understanding of LLMs, rather than strict ML classification, together with the mass extraction of user reviews to analyze if the performance of LLMs in understanding user reviews is comparable to the performance of human raters. This enables a quick and cheap workflow for development teams to gather and process their userś requirements. This paper provides three major contributions: (1) We provide a completely coded dataset of 300 user reviews containing usability-relevant aspects from three different types of apps, that were labeled by two human raters and by an LLM. (2) We build an initial prompt, based on two prompt engineering iterations and specifically developed coding guidelines derived from the 10 Nielsen Usability Heuristics, for LLMs to filter usability relevant user reviews. (3) We determine that LLMs are generally able to recognize usability as a non-functional requirement in user reviews, in terms of their F-score, but the performance and reliability is strongly dependent on the prompt.

</details>


### [22] [Agentic Interpretation: Lattice-Structured Evidence for LLM-Based Program Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12694v1)
*Jacqueline L. Mitchell,Chao Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了智能体解释框架，将基于格的静态分析纪律应用于LLM驱动的程序推理，通过分解声明并跟踪判断来解决直接使用LLM进行全程序分析的不透明性和脆弱性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接要求LLM进行一次性全程序分析会压缩多个依赖证据的判断为单一不透明答案，缺乏中间发现来引导后续搜索，导致分析脆弱。需要一种方法将LLM的推理与静态分析的纪律相结合。

Method: 提出智能体解释框架，将高层分析目标分解为局部声明，在有限高度格中跟踪LLM对每个声明的判断，并使用工作列表算法管理声明及其判断的演变。

Result: 通过分析依赖不透明第三方组件的代码示例，展示了智能体解释的有效性；并引入了形式化模型，探索了设计空间。

Conclusion: 智能体解释能够将LLM驱动的程序推理与基于格的静态分析纪律结合，提供更透明和可控的分析过程，特别适用于依赖外部信息或难以用传统静态分析处理的情况。

中文摘要：大型语言模型可以查阅固定静态分析器无法访问的信息，例如文档、当前安全公告、特定版本的元数据以及非正式的API合约。这使得LLMs成为对依赖于源程序之外信息或以其他方式不适用于传统静态分析器的程序分析的有吸引力的选择。然而，直接要求LLM进行一次性的全程序分析是脆弱的，因为它将许多依赖证据的判断压缩成一个单一的不透明答案，而不是揭示哪些结论得到支持或质疑，并利用中间发现引导后续更聚焦的搜索。在本文中，我们提出了“智能体解释”（agentic interpretation）框架，该框架将基于格（lattice）的静态分析纪律引入LLM驱动的程序推理。在高层，智能体解释将高层分析目标分解为局部化声明，并在有限高度的格中跟踪LLM对每个声明的判断。一个工作列表算法控制着声明及其判断在分析过程中的演变。我们引入了智能体解释的形式化模型，探索其打开的设计空间，并通过一个分析依赖于不透明第三方组件的代码的工作示例来说明该方法。

Original abstract: Large language models can consult information that fixed static analyzers cannot, such as documentation, current security advisories, version-specific metadata, and informal API contracts. This makes LLMs a compelling option for program analyses that depend on information beyond the source program, or that are otherwise not amenable to conventional static analyzers. However, directly asking an LLM for a one-shot whole-program analysis is brittle because it compresses many evidence-dependent judgments into a single opaque answer, rather than exposing which conclusions are supported or disputed and using intermediate findings to guide later, more focused searches. In this paper, we propose agentic interpretation, a framework that brings the discipline of lattice-based static analysis to LLM-driven program reasoning. At a high level, agentic interpretation decomposes a high-level analysis goal into localized claims, and tracks the LLM's judgment about each claim in a finite-height lattice. A worklist algorithm governs how claims and their judgments evolve during the analysis. We introduce a formal model of agentic interpretation, explore the design space it opens, and illustrate the approach with a worked example analyzing code that depends on opaque third-party components.

</details>


### [23] [Finding a Crab in the C: Assured Translation via Comparative Symbolic Execution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12731v1)
*Caleb Helbling,Graham Leach-Krouse,Michael Crystal*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Cozy是一种比较二进制分析工具，用于验证从非内存安全代码到内存安全语言翻译的等价性，并让开发者审查差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动翻译代码存在语义差异风险，需要确保翻译后的代码行为正确。

Method: Cozy同时分析原始不安全代码的二进制和翻译后安全代码的二进制，检测行为差异，并让开发者审查每个差异是否预期。

Result: 除了开发者批准的差异，两个二进制被形式化验证为等价。

Conclusion: Cozy可应用于自动翻译、错误纠正、代码审查等场景。

中文摘要：现代高保障软件系统开发倾向于使用内存安全语言，如SPARK（ADA）或Rust。然而，开发者常常在遗留系统和库中遇到非内存安全代码（例如C语言），重写这些代码的成本过高或风险太大。为此，开发者开始转向机器学习/人工智能系统和其他自动代码翻译器。然而，自动翻译本身也带来风险。原始代码和移植后的代码在语义上并不完全相同——否则进行翻译就没有意义。为了降低这些风险，我们开发了cozy，一种比较二进制分析工具，它能同时分析从“不安全”源代码编译而来的二进制文件和从该源代码到内存安全语言的翻译版本编译而来的二进制文件。cozy引导开发者检查两个二进制文件行为上的差异，呈现每个差异并询问用户该差异是预期的（好的）还是错误的。在被标记的差异之外，两个二进制文件被形式化验证为等价。因此，审查过程保证了等价性，但允许开发者批准的变更。cozy可应用于自动翻译、错误纠正、代码审查、操作授权和自动翻译。

Original abstract: Modern high-assurance software systems development favors memory safe languages such as SPARK (ADA) or Rust. However, developers often encounter non-memory safe code (e.g., C) in legacy systems and libraries which would be prohibitively expensive or risky to re-write. In response, developers have begun turning to machine learning/AI systems and other automated code translators. Automated translation comes with its own risks, however. The original and ported code are not precisely the same, semantically - otherwise there would be no point in performing the translation. To reduce these risks, we have developed cozy, a comparative binary analysis tool that simultaneously analyzes a binary compiled from "unsafe" source code and a binary compiled from a translation of the source code to a memory safe language. cozy walks the developer through differences in the behavior of the two binaries, presenting each difference and asking the user to assess whether the difference is intentional (good) or erroneous. Outside of the flagged differences, the binaries are formally verified to be equivalent. Consequently, the review process guarantees equivalence modulo changes approved by the developer. cozy has applications to automated translation, bug correction, code reviews, operation authorization, and automatic translation.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文使用内生增长理论和微分方程建模开源项目开发者的终身参与度动态，并估算项目的终身生产价值。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用先前用于产品生命周期的方法，结合内生增长理论和微分方程组，建立描述开发者参与度与增长水平交互的模型，并通过跨项目数据校准。

Result: 模型校准良好，能够估计开发者终身参与度和增长，从而支持估算项目终身生产价值。

Original abstract: Using methods previously applied to product life cycles, this paper models developer engagement through the project life cycle for open-source projects, and detects similar dynamics in a cross section of projects. Endogenous growth theory is used to model growth dynamics in open-source software engineering, while incorporating the interactions between growth levels and developer activity over time using systems of differential equations. The solution to this model calibrates well to many open-source projects. The model generates an estimate of the lifetime developer engagement and growth, which supports estimating a lifetime production value of open-source projects.

### [25] [CVEvolve: Autonomous Algorithm Discovery for Unstructured Scientific Data Processing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11359v3)
*Ming Du,Xiangyu Yin,Yanqi Luo,Dishant Beniwal,Songyuan Tang,Hemant Sharma,Mathew J. Cherukara*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自主agentic harness用于科学算法发现，多轮搜索与代码执行，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: CVEvolve是一个零代码自主代理框架，通过多轮搜索和谱系感知采样自动发现科学数据处理算法，在多个图像分析任务上优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 领域科学家缺乏计算和图像处理专业知识，难以从噪声、高动态范围、稀疏标记的科学图像数据中开发有效算法。

Method: CVEvolve采用多轮搜索策略，结合代码执行、评估实现、历史管理、保留测试，交替进行发现和改进动作，并使用谱系感知随机候选采样平衡探索与利用。

Result: 在X射线荧光显微镜图像配准、布拉格峰检测、高能衍射显微镜图像分割和混合分析仿射配准任务中，CVEvolve发现的算法优于基线方法，且保留测试有助于识别泛化能力更好的候选。

Conclusion: 零代码、自主LLM驱动的算法开发能够帮助领域科学家将非结构化科学图像数据转化为实用算法，促进科学发现。

中文摘要：科学数据处理通常需要针对特定任务的算法或AI模型，这给需要分析数据但可能缺乏计算或图像处理专业知识的领域科学家造成了障碍。当数据存在噪声、动态范围高、标记稀疏或仅松散指定时，这一障碍尤为明显。我们介绍了CVEvolve，一个自主代理框架，具有零代码接口，用于科学数据处理算法发现。CVEvolve结合了多轮搜索策略与代码执行、评估实现、历史管理、保留测试以及科学数据和视觉输出的可选检查工具。搜索在发现和改进动作之间交替，并使用谱系感知随机候选采样来平衡探索与利用。我们在X射线荧光显微镜图像配准、布拉格峰检测、高能衍射显微镜图像分割以及混合分析学习仿射配准上展示了CVEvolve。在这些任务中，CVEvolve发现了优于基线方法的算法，而保留测试跟踪有助于识别那些比后期过度优化替代方案泛化能力更好的候选算法。这些结果表明，零代码、自主LLM驱动的算法开发可以帮助领域科学家将非结构化的科学图像数据转化为实用算法和下游科学发现。

Original abstract: Scientific data processing often requires task-specific algorithms or AI models, creating a barrier for domain scientists who need to analyze their data but may not have extensive computing or image-processing expertise. This barrier is especially pronounced when data are noisy, have a high dynamic range, are sparsely labeled, or are only loosely specified. We introduce CVEvolve, an autonomous agentic harness with a zero-code interface for scientific data-processing algorithm discovery. CVEvolve combines a multi-round search strategy with tools for code execution, evaluation implementation, history management, holdout testing, and optional inspection of scientific data and visual outputs. The search alternates between discovery and improvement actions, and uses lineage-aware stochastic candidate sampling to balance exploration and exploitation. We demonstrate CVEvolve on X-ray fluorescence microscopy image registration, Bragg peak detection, high-energy diffraction microscopy image segmentation, and hybrid analytical-learning-based affine registration. Across these tasks, CVEvolve discovers algorithms that improve over baseline methods, while holdout test tracking helps identify candidates that generalize better than later over-optimized alternatives. These results show that zero-code, autonomous LLM-powered algorithm development can help domain scientists turn unstructured scientific image data into practical algorithms and downstream scientific discoveries.

</details>


### [26] [LLM-X: A Scalable Negotiation-Oriented Exchange for Communication Among Personal LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11376v1)
*Giuliano Lorenzoni,Paulo Alencar,Donald Cowan*

Original abstract: We propose a personal-LLM exchange (LLM-X), a scalable negotiation-oriented environment that enables direct, structured communication across populations of personal agents (LLMs), each representing an individual user. Unlike existing tool-centric protocols that focus on agent-API interaction, LLM-X introduces a message bus and routing substrate for LLM-to-LLM coordination with guarantees around schema validity and policy enforcement. We contribute: (1) an architecture for LLM-X comprising federated gateways, topic-based routing, and policy enforcement; (2) a typed message protocol supporting capability negotiation and contract-net-style coordination; and (3) the first empirical evaluation of LLM-based multi-agent negotiation at scale. Experiments span 5, 9, and 12 agents, under distinct negotiation policies (Low, Medium, High), and across both short-run (minutes) and long-run (2h, 12h) load conditions. Results highlight clear policy-performance trade-offs: stricter policies improve robustness and fairness but increase latencies and message volume. Extended runs confirm that LLM-X remains stable under sustained load, with bounded latency drift.

### [27] [Attributing Emergence in Million-Agent Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11404v2)
*Ling Tang,Jilin Mei,Qian Chen,Qihan Ren,Linfeng Zhang,Quanshi Zhang,Jing Shao,Xia Hu,Dongrui Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 百万级多agent归因方法，对大规模agent评测有贡献。

TL;DR: 通过将Aumann-Shapley路径积分归因适配到LLM驱动的多智能体系统，实现了百万智能体规模的高效公理化归因，并证明对于非线性宏观指标，全规模归因是必要的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有公理化归因方法在计算上随智能体数量组合增长，局限于小规模（N≤10^3），无法解释现实中大规模（N≥10^6）社会现象。

Method: 改编Aumann-Shapley路径积分归因方法，使其适用于LLM驱动的百万智能体级多智能体系统。

Result: 方法满足所有四个公理，速度比采样Shapley快3-5个数量级，归因规模提升1670倍；实证表明全规模归因与偏倚小样本结果结构不一致，且该偏差无法通过事后全局重新缩放修正。

Conclusion: 对于非线性宏观指标，全规模归因是必要要求而非可选项。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）能够在个体智能体中模拟类似人类的推理和决策。基于LLM的多智能体系统（MAS）将这些智能体组合起来，模拟群体规模的社会现象，如极化、信息级联和市场恐慌。这类研究需要将宏观涌现归因于个体智能体，但现有的公理化方法在计算上随$N$组合增长，且仅限于$N \lesssim 10^3$，而它们所解释的现象发生在$N \geq 10^6$。我们通过将Aumann-Shapley路径积分归因方法适配到百万智能体规模的LLM驱动MAS中，解决了这一差距；所得方法满足所有四个公理，在相同硬件上运行速度比采样Shapley快三到五个数量级，并将可行的公理化归因范围扩大了三个数量级以上（提升$1670$倍）。我们使用该方法实证检验了规模差距：在14天的公开Bluesky数据（$1{,}671{,}587$名活跃用户，五个话题）上，我们计算了全规模以及小规模研究中使用的Visibility偏倚的$N = 10^2$便利样本的归因，两者在结构上不一致。在全规模下，长尾和中层共同承担了大部分；偏倚的小面板将大约两倍的份额转移到了高关注层级（$48\%$对比$24\%$）。然后我们证明，这种不一致通常不能通过事后重新缩放来减少：一个归因缩放偏倚定理表明，当宏观指标相对于智能体是线性时，存在一个协调的全局重新缩放因子，而我们的非线性指标的残差为$0.10$--$0.98$。对于此类非线性指标，全规模归因因此是一个要求，而不是方法上的选择。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can simulate human-like reasoning and decision-making in individual agents. LLM-powered multi-agent systems (MAS) combine such agents to simulate population-scale social phenomena such as polarization, information cascades, and market panics. Such studies require attributing macro emergence to individual agents, but existing axiomatic methods scale combinatorially in $N$ and have been confined to $N \lesssim 10^3$, while the phenomena they explain occur at $N \geq 10^6$. We address this gap by adapting Aumann--Shapley path-integral attribution to LLM-powered MAS at million-agent scale; the resulting method satisfies all four axioms, runs three to five orders of magnitude faster than sampled Shapley on the same hardware, and extends feasible axiomatic attribution by over three orders of magnitude (a $1670\times$ jump). We use this method to test the scale gap empirically: across 14 days of public Bluesky data ($1{,}671{,}587$ active users, five topics), we compute the attribution at both full scale and the visibility-biased $N = 10^2$ convenience sample used by small-scale studies, and the two disagree structurally. At full scale the long tail and middle tier jointly carry the majority; the biased small panel shifts about twice that share onto the upper follower tiers ($48\%$ versus $24\%$). We then prove that the disagreement cannot in general be reduced by post-hoc rescaling: an Attribution Scaling Bias theorem shows that a reconciling global rescaling factor exists exactly when the macro indicator is linear over agents, and our nonlinear indicators give residuals of $0.10$--$0.98$. For such nonlinear indicators, full-scale attribution is therefore a requirement rather than a methodological choice.

### [28] [Under the Hood of SKILL.md: Semantic Supply-chain Attacks on AI Agent Skill Registry](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11418v1)
*Shoumik Saha,Kazem Faghih,Soheil Feizi*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究agent技能注册的语义供应链攻击，对agent安全有启发

TL;DR: 研究表明，Agent Skill的SKILL.md文件作为操作性文本，在发现、选择和治理阶段均易受语义攻击，影响智能体对第三方技能的信任和使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Agent Skills通过SKILL.md描述使用方式，但自然语言元数据引入语义供应链风险，可能被攻击者操纵以影响智能体行为。

Method: 针对Agent Skill生命周期的发现、选择、治理三个阶段，设计仅基于SKILL.md的攻击，利用真实ClawHub技能和模拟注册表机制进行实验。

Result: 发现阶段攻击实现86%成对胜率和80% Top-10排名；选择阶段攻击使对抗性技能在77.6%试验中被选；治理阶段恶意技能在36.5%-100%案例中逃避阻止。

Conclusion: SKILL.md不是被动文档，而是操作文本，能够决定智能体发现、信任和使用的第三方能力，需加强安全防护。

中文摘要：自主AI智能体越来越多地通过Agent Skills扩展其能力：Agent Skills是模块化文件系统包，其SKILL.md文件描述了智能体何时以及如何使用它们。虽然这种设计实现了可扩展的按需能力扩展，但它也引入了一种语义供应链风险，其中自然语言元数据和指令可以影响哪些技能被接纳、展示、选择和加载。我们研究了在Agent Skill生命周期的三个面向注册表的阶段中仅针对SKILL.md的攻击，使用了真实的ClawHub技能和现实的注册表机制。在发现阶段，短文本触发词可以操纵基于嵌入的检索并提高对抗性技能的可见性，实现了高达86%的成对胜率和80%的Top-10排名。在选择阶段，仅限描述的框架使智能体偏向于功能等效的对抗性变体，在平均77.6%的成对试验中被选择。在治理阶段，语义规避策略使恶意技能在36.5%-100%的案例中避免被阻止判决。总体而言，我们的结果表明，SKILL.md不是被动的文档，而是塑造智能体发现、信任和使用的第三方能力的操作性文本。

Original abstract: Autonomous AI agents increasingly extend their capabilities through Agent Skills: modular filesystem packages whose SKILL.md files describe when and how agents should use them. While this design enables scalable, on-demand capability expansion, it also introduces a semantic supply-chain risk in which natural-language metadata and instructions can affect which skills are admitted, surfaced, selected, and loaded. We study SKILL.md - only attacks across three registry-facing stages of the Agent Skill lifecycle, using real ClawHub skills and realistic registry mechanisms. In Discovery, short textual triggers can manipulate embedding-based retrieval and improve adversarial skill visibility, achieving up to 86% pairwise win rate and 80% Top-10 placement. In Selection, description-only framing biases agents toward functionally equivalent adversarial variants, which are selected in 77.6% of paired trials on average. In Governance, semantic evasion strategies cause malicious skills to avoid a blocking verdict in 36.5%-100% of cases. Overall, our results show that SKILL.md is not passive documentation but operational text that shapes which third-party capabilities agents find, trust, and use.

### [29] [Adaptive Teacher Exposure for Self-Distillation in LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11458v3)
*Zihao Han,Tiangang Zhang,Huaibin Wang,Yilun Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自适应教师暴露改进LLM推理自蒸馏，通用训练方法可跟踪

TL;DR: 提出自适应教师暴露自蒸馏（ATESD）方法，通过可学习的暴露控制器解决自蒸馏中教师暴露不匹配问题，在多个数学推理基准上取得一致提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自蒸馏方法默认教师总是看到完整参考推理，导致教师侧暴露不匹配：当教师基于远超学生当前能力的推理进行条件设定时，目标过于强大而难以吸收；并且完全暴露并非总是最佳选择，师生不匹配随暴露增加而单调增加。因此需要将教师暴露从固定超参数变为可学习的训练时控制变量。

Method: ATESD 使用轻量级 Beta 策略控制器（基于紧凑训练状态统计量）对揭示比率建模，在学生更新的短保持窗口中使用一次采样的暴露；通过折扣学习进度奖励优化控制器，该奖励根据决策对学生未来改进的影响（而非即时损失）评分，解决延迟信用分配问题。

Result: 在 AIME 24、AIME 25 和 HMMT 25 上使用 Qwen3-{1.7B, 4B, 8B}，ATESD 持续优于 OPSD 等基线，分别提升 +0.95、+2.05 和 +2.33 个 Average@12 分数。

Conclusion: 自适应教师暴露被确立为推理自蒸馏的一个有效新维度，为提升 LLM 推理能力提供了新的方向。

中文摘要：在策略自蒸馏已成为大语言模型推理的强大方法，其中特权教师通过参考解来监督学生自身的 rollout。然而，几乎所有此类方法共享的设计选择却未被质疑：教师总是看到完整的参考推理过程。我们认为这种默认设置本身就是问题的一部分，并识别出一个教师侧的暴露不匹配：当教师基于远超出学生当前能力的推理进行条件设定时，产生的 token 目标过于强大而难以吸收。一项受控的固定暴露扫描从两个方面具体说明了这一点：1）完全暴露并非总是最佳选择，2）随着教师看到更多特权推理，师生不匹配程度单调增加。这促使将教师暴露视为可学习的训练时控制变量，而非固定的超参数。因此，我们提出了自适应教师暴露自蒸馏（ATESD）。ATESD 使用一个轻量级的 Beta 策略控制器（基于紧凑的训练状态统计量）对揭示比率进行建模，并在学生更新的短保持窗口中采用一个采样的暴露。为了使该暴露控制器可学习，我们使用一个折扣学习进度奖励对其进行优化，该奖励根据每个保留决策对学生未来改进的影响（而非即时损失变化）进行评分，从而解决了在策略蒸馏带来的延迟信用分配问题。在 AIME 24、AIME 25 和 HMMT 25 上使用 Qwen3-{1.7B, 4B, 8B} 进行的实验表明，ATESD 持续优于竞争性的自蒸馏和 RL 基线，在 OPSD 基础上分别提升了 +0.95、+2.05 和 +2.33 个 Average@12 分数，并将自适应教师暴露确立为推理自蒸馏的一个有效新维度。

Original abstract: On-policy self-distillation has become a strong recipe for LLM reasoning, where a privileged teacher supervises the student's own rollouts while conditioning on the reference solution. A design choice shared by nearly all such methods, however, has gone unquestioned: the teacher always sees the full reference reasoning. We argue that this default itself is part of the problem and identify a teacher-side exposure mismatch: when the teacher conditions on reasoning far beyond the student's current competence, the resulting token targets become too strong to absorb. A controlled fixed-exposure sweep makes this concrete on two fronts: 1) full exposure is not reliably the best choice, and 2) student-teacher mismatch grows monotonically as the teacher sees more privileged reasoning. This motivates treating teacher exposure not as a fixed hyperparameter but as a learnable training-time control variable. We therefore propose Adaptive Teacher Exposure for Self-Distillation (ATESD). ATESD models the reveal ratio with a lightweight Beta-policy controller conditioned on compact training-state statistics, and uses one sampled exposure for a short hold window of student updates. To make this exposure controller learnable, we optimize it with a discounted learning-progress reward that scores each held decision by its effect on the student's future improvement rather than its immediate loss change, addressing the delayed credit assignment induced by on-policy distillation. Experiments on AIME 24, AIME 25, and HMMT 25 across Qwen3-{1.7B, 4B, 8B} show that ATESD consistently outperforms competitive self-distillation and RL baselines, improving over OPSD by +0.95, +2.05, and +2.33 Average@12 points respectively, and establishing adaptive teacher exposure as an effective new axis for reasoning self-distillation.

</details>


### [30] [Breaking $\textit{Winner-Takes-All}$: Cooperative Policy Optimization Improves Diverse LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11461v2)
*Haoxuan Chen,Tianming Liang,Wei-Shi Zheng,Jian-Fang Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 合作策略优化提升LLM推理多样性，可视为通用方法

TL;DR: 提出群体协同策略优化（GCPO），通过团队级信用分配和边际贡献奖励机制，将训练从轨迹竞争转为团队合作，解决了RLVR中的探索崩溃问题，显著提升推理准确性和多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RLVR中流行的GRPO等算法因赢家通吃机制导致探索崩溃，模型过早收敛到少数高分模式，缺乏多样性。现有熵正则化或多样性奖励未能改变竞争本质，无法有效促进全局多样性。

Method: GCPO采用团队合作范式：用团队级信用分配替代独立评分，通过奖励加权语义嵌入的行列式体积度量团队有效解覆盖，仅正确且非冗余的轨迹贡献体积；优势估计时根据每条轨迹的平均边际贡献重新分配集体奖励，将优化导向非冗余正确路径。

Result: 在多个推理基准上，GCPO在推理准确性和解决方案多样性方面均显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: GCPO通过团队协作和边际贡献重分配有效缓解探索崩溃，提升了LLM推理的准确性和多样性，是一种更优的RLVR训练范式。

中文摘要：带验证器的强化学习（RLVR）已成为改进LLM推理的核心范式，但流行的基于群体的优化算法（如GRPO）常常遭遇探索崩溃，即模型过早收敛到一组狭窄的高分模式，缺乏探索新解决方案的能力。近期的尝试通过添加熵正则化或多样性奖励来缓解这一问题，然而这些方法并未改变"赢家通吃"的本质，即轨迹仍然为了个体优势而竞争，而非为了最大化全局多样性而合作。在这项工作中，我们提出群体协同策略优化（GCPO），将训练范式从轨迹竞争转变为团队合作。具体而言，GCPO用团队级信用分配取代独立的轨迹评分：一条轨迹的奖励取决于它对团队有效解决方案覆盖率的贡献，而不是其个体准确性。该覆盖率被描述为奖励加权语义嵌入的行列式体积，其中只有正确且非冗余的轨迹才贡献于此体积。在优势估计期间，GCPO根据每条轨迹对团队的平均边际贡献，将集体团队奖励重新分配给每条轨迹。这种协作式训练范式将优化导向非冗余的正确推理路径。跨多个推理基准的实验表明，GCPO在推理准确性和解决方案多样性方面均显著优于现有方法。代码将发布在https://github.com/bradyBuddiemarch/gcpo。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiers (RLVR) has become a central paradigm for improving LLM reasoning, yet popular group-based optimization algorithms like GRPO often suffer from exploration collapse, where the models prematurely converge on a narrow set of high-scoring patterns, lacking the ability to explore new solutions. Recent efforts attempt to alleviate this by adding entropy regularization or diversity bonus. However, these approaches do not change the \textit{winner-takes-all} nature, where rollouts still compete for individual advantage rather than cooperating for maximizing global diversity. In this work, we propose Group Cooperative Policy Optimization (GCPO), which shifts the training paradigm from rollout competition to team cooperation. Specifically, GCPO replaces independent rollout scoring with team-level credit assignment: a rollout is rewarded by how much it contributes to the team's valid solution coverage, rather than its individual accuracy. This coverage is described as a determinant volume over reward-weighted semantic embeddings, where only correct and non-redundant rollouts contribute to this volume. During advantage estimation, GCPO redistributes the collective team reward to each single rollout according to its average marginal contribution to the team. This cooperative training paradigm routes optimization toward non-redundant correct reasoning paths. Experiments across multiple reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that GCPO significantly improves both reasoning accuracy and solution diversity over existing approaches. Code will be released at https://github.com/bradybuddiemarch/gcpo.

</details>


### [31] [Engagement Process: Rethinking the Temporal Interface of Action and Observation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11484v2)
*Jialian Li,Yuchen Cao,Junhong Liu,Weiran Guo,Xutao Wang,Jiaming Song,Jiahao Zhang,Jie Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出Engagement Process形式化模型，显式建模时间，可迁移至agent交互设计

TL;DR: 提出Engagement Process (EP)形式化方法，通过解耦事件流显式建模时间交互，揭示隐藏的时间行为并支持策略适应时间成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于固定步骤的接口无法处理动作和观察在不同时间尺度上解耦的复杂时间交互，需要显式的时间建模。

Method: 提出Engagement Process (EP)，继承POMDP决策理论结构，将动作和观察表示为沿时间的解耦事件流，而非固定步骤配对。

Result: 在玩具、LLM智能体和学习实验中，EP揭示了被步骤接口隐藏的时间行为，并使策略能在显式时间成本下适应。

Conclusion: EP有效建模单智能体时间问题并支持更丰富的交互组织，为处理实际时间延迟和动态环境提供新范式。

中文摘要：在数字和物理环境中完成任务越来越涉及复杂的时间交互，其中动作和观察在不同时间尺度上展开，而不是与固定的观察-动作步骤对齐。为了对这种交互进行建模，我们提出了参与过程（Engagement Process, EP），这是一种交互形式化方法，它继承了POMDP的决策理论结构，同时在动作-观察接口中明确时间。EP将动作和观察表示为沿时间解耦的事件流，而不是在固定的决策步骤中配对的更新。这种接口捕获了单智能体时间问题，如思考延迟、延迟反馈和持续动作，同时支持更丰富的智能体端组织、多速率协调和子系统间的组合交互。通过玩具、LLM智能体和学习实验，EP揭示了被基于步骤的接口隐藏的时间行为，并使策略能够在明确的时间成本下适应。

Original abstract: Task completion in digital and physical environments increasingly involves complex temporal interaction, where actions and observations unfold over different time scales rather than align with fixed observation--action steps. To model such interactions, we propose \emph{Engagement Process} (EP), an interaction formalism that inherits the decision-theoretic structure of POMDPs while making time explicit in the action--observation interface. EP represents actions and observations as decoupled event streams along time, rather than updates paired at fixed decision steps. This interface captures single-agent timing issues such as deliberation latency, delayed feedback, and persistent actions, while supporting richer agent-side organization, multi-rate coordination, and compositional interaction among subsystems. Across toy, LLM-agent, and learning experiments, EP exposes temporal behaviors hidden by step-based interfaces and enables policies to adapt under explicit time costs.

</details>


### [32] [AutoLLMResearch: Training Research Agents for Automating LLM Experiment Configuration - Learning from Cheap, Optimizing Expensive](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11518v2)
*Taicheng Guo,Nitesh V. Chawla,Olaf Wiest,Xiangliang Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: AutoLLMResearch框架训练研究agent，可迁移至代码优化agent自动调优

TL;DR: 提出AutoLLMResearch框架，通过多保真度实验环境学习可泛化配置规则，自动化高成本LLM实验配置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动化方法只适用于低成本试错，高成本LLM实验配置仍依赖人工，需自动化。

Method: 提出包含LLMConfig-Gym环境（四个任务，超百万GPU小时数据）和结构化训练流水线（长时域MDP，跨保真度外推）的框架。

Result: 在保留实验上优于多种强基线，显示有效性、泛化性和可解释性。

Conclusion: 该框架可作为实际LLM实验自动化的实用通用解决方案。

中文摘要：有效配置可扩展的大语言模型（LLM）实验（涵盖架构设计、超参数调优等）对于推进LLM研究至关重要，因为糟糕的配置选择会浪费大量计算资源并阻止模型发挥其全部潜力。先前的自动化方法专为低成本环境设计，其中重复试错是可行的，但可扩展的LLM实验过于昂贵，无法进行如此广泛的迭代。据我们所知，没有工作解决高成本LLM实验配置的自动化问题，使得该问题劳动密集型且依赖于专家直觉。受此差距的启发，我们提出了AutoLLMResearch，一个智能体框架，模仿人类研究人员如何从低保真度实验中学习可泛化的原理，并外推以高效识别昂贵LLM环境中的有前景配置。核心挑战是如何使智能体通过与捕捉LLM配置景观结构的多保真度实验环境交互来学习。为实现这一点，我们提出了一个系统框架，包含两个关键组件：1) LLMConfig-Gym，一个多保真度环境，涵盖四个关键的LLM实验任务，由超过一百万GPU小时的可验证实验结果支持；2) 一个结构化训练流水线，将配置研究表述为长时域马尔可夫决策过程，并相应激励跨保真度外推推理。在保留实验上针对多种强基线的广泛评估证明了我们框架的有效性、泛化能力和可解释性，支持其作为可扩展的实际LLM实验自动化的实用且通用解决方案的潜力。

Original abstract: Effectively configuring scalable large language model (LLM) experiments, spanning architecture design, hyperparameter tuning, and beyond, is crucial for advancing LLM research, as poor configuration choices can waste substantial computational resources and prevent models from realizing their full potential. Prior automated methods are designed for low-cost settings where repeated trial and error is feasible, but scalable LLM experiments are too expensive for such extensive iteration. To our knowledge, no work has addressed the automation of high-cost LLM experiment configurations, leaving this problem labor-intensive and dependent on expert intuition. Motivated by this gap, we propose AutoLLMResearch, an agentic framework that mimics how human researchers learn generalizable principles from low-fidelity experiments and extrapolate to efficiently identify promising configurations in expensive LLM settings. The core challenge is how to enable an agent to learn, through interaction with a multi-fidelity experimental environment that captures the structure of the LLM configuration landscape. To achieve this, we propose a systematic framework with two key components: 1) LLMConfig-Gym, a multi-fidelity environment encompassing four critical LLM experiment tasks, supported by over one million GPU hours of verifiable experiment outcomes; 2) A structured training pipeline that formulates configuration research as a long-horizon Markov Decision Process and accordingly incentivizes cross-fidelity extrapolation reasoning. Extensive evaluation against diverse strong baselines on held-out experiments demonstrates the effectiveness, generalization, and interpretability of our framework, supporting its potential as a practical and general solution for scalable real-world LLM experiment automation.
