### [33] [Controllable User Simulation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11519v1)
*Guy Tennenholtz,Ofer Meshi,Amir Globerson,Uri Shalit,Jihwan Jeong,Craig Boutilier*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 可控用户模拟形式化，off-policy评估方法，可迁移至agent评测

TL;DR: 本文形式化可控用户模拟为因果推断问题，指出标准监督训练存在前视偏差导致可控性崩溃，提出因果基础模拟器消除偏差并保持自然方差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 使用离线数据集评估对话代理无法覆盖罕见场景或支持测试新策略，而现有可控模拟器通过监督训练存在因果一致性问题。

Method: 将可控模拟形式化为因果推断问题，建立理论条件，提出先验控制、逐步动态控制和直接策略条件学习等训练缓解措施。

Result: 因果基础模拟器消除前视偏差，保持自然方差，在未见过的智能体行为上表现出稳健零样本泛化。

Conclusion: 因果基础模拟器优于标准全局控制方法，能够恢复因果一致性并避免可控性崩溃。

中文摘要：使用离线数据集评估对话代理通常无法覆盖罕见场景或支持测试新策略。这推动了使用可控用户模拟器进行有针对性的反事实评估，通常通过提示或微调大型语言模型来实现。在这项工作中，我们将可控模拟形式化为一个因果推断问题。通过将自然语言评估与离线策略评估方法相结合，我们表明，通过监督微调事后轨迹标签来训练模拟器的标准实践会产生结构有偏的模型。具体来说，这些标签与数据生成的行为策略密不可分地耦合，注入了破坏因果一致性的前视偏差。此外，我们证明，在策略偏移下，这种失败会导致评估指标的方差呈几何级数爆炸，我们将这种现象称为可控性崩溃。为了恢复因果一致性，我们建立了准确模拟的理论条件，并提出了实用的训练缓解措施：先验控制、逐步动态控制和直接策略条件学习。实证评估证实，虽然标准的全局控制会扭曲对话分布并坍缩行为多样性，但我们的因果基础模拟器消除了前视偏差，保持了自然方差，并在未见过的智能体行为上表现出稳健的零样本泛化能力。

Original abstract: Using offline datasets to evaluate conversational agents often fails to cover rare scenarios or to support testing new policies. This has motivated the use of controllable user simulators for targeted, counterfactual evaluation, typically implemented by prompting or fine-tuning large language models. In this work, we formalize controllable simulation as a causal inference problem. By bridging natural language evaluation with off-policy evaluation methodology, we show that the standard practice of training simulators via supervised fine-tuning on post-hoc trajectory labels yields a structurally biased model. Specifically, these labels are inextricably coupled to the data-generating behavior policy, injecting a look-ahead bias that breaks causal consistency. Furthermore, we prove that under policy shift this failure causes the variance of evaluation metrics to explode geometrically, a phenomenon we term controllability collapse. To restore causal consistency, we establish theoretical conditions for accurate simulation and propose practical training mitigations: a priori controls, step-wise dynamic controls, and direct policy-conditioned learning. Empirical evaluation confirms that while standard global controls distort conversational distributions and collapse behavioral diversity, our causally grounded simulators eliminate look-ahead bias, preserve natural variance, and exhibit robust zero-shot generalization to unseen agent behaviors.

</details>


### [34] [Read, Grep, and Synthesize: Diagnosing Cross-Domain Seed Exposure for LLM Research Ideation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11532v1)
*Yunju Choi,Min Song*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 利用工具和跨域检索进行LLM研究构思，涉及agent工具使用与合成，可跟踪

TL;DR: 本文提出PaperGym，一种三阶段流程，用于研究LLM构思系统中跨领域检索的效果。实验表明，跨领域检索比无检索或同领域基线获得更多新颖性，但与随机多样种子控制无显著差异，说明LLM受益于多样种子暴露，但未充分利用检索语义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 观察到机器学习中新方法的发现常依赖跨领域技术迁移，但当前LLM构思系统是否真正受益于有针对性的跨领域检索尚不明确。

Method: 提出PaperGym流程：（1）工具增强的种子提取，（2）基于释义的跨领域种子检索，（3）方法合成与基于量规的评估。

Result: 跨领域检索在成对新颖性上优于无检索和同领域基线，但与随机多样种子控制无显著差异。

Conclusion: LLM构思系统受益于多样种子暴露，但尚未可靠利用检索的语义原因；现有系统在利用跨领域知识上仍有局限。

中文摘要：发现新兴问题的新方法论是机器学习中一个持续的循环，通常由跨领域的技术迁移驱动。基于这一观察，我们探究当前的大语言模型构思系统是否受益于有针对性的跨领域检索，还是仅仅受益于接触到多样化的机制。我们通过PaperGym研究这一问题，这是一个三阶段流程：（1）通过读、grep和bash在隔离的论文环境中进行工具增强的种子提取，（2）通过跨七个机器学习领域的释义进行跨领域种子检索，以及（3）从检索到的种子中合成方法，每个方法由基于量规的评判者评分。工具增强的提取提高了特异性，而基于释义的检索拓宽了领域覆盖范围。在合成中，跨领域检索在成对新颖性胜出次数上多于无检索和同领域基线，但与随机多样种子控制组相比没有显著差异。这些发现表明，大语言模型构思系统受益于多样化的种子暴露，但尚未可靠地利用检索特定种子的语义原因。我们在https://github.com/yunjoochoi/PaperGym发布了种子库、量规提示和运行脚本。

Original abstract: The discovery of novel methodologies for emerging problems is a continuing cycle in ML, often driven by the migration of techniques across domains. Building on this observation, we ask whether current LLM ideation systems benefit from targeted cross-domain retrieval or simply from exposure to diverse mechanisms. We study this question through PaperGym, a three-stage pipeline: (1) tool-augmented seed extraction via read, grep, and bash over an isolated paper environment, (2) cross-domain seed retrieval via paraphrasing across seven ML domains, and (3) method synthesis from retrieved seeds, each scored by rubric-based judges. Tool-augmented extraction improves specificity, and paraphrase-based retrieval broadens domain coverage. In synthesis, cross-domain retrieval receives more pairwise novelty wins than no-retrieval and same-domain baselines, but shows no significant difference from a random diverse-seed control. These findings suggest LLM ideation systems benefit from diverse seed exposure, but do not yet reliably exploit the semantic reason particular seeds were retrieved. We release the seed library, rubric prompts, and run scripts at https://github.com/yunjoochoi/PaperGym

</details>


### [35] [Optimal LTLf Synthesis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11544v2)
*Yujian Cao,Sven Schewe,Qiyi Tang,Shufang Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 最优LTLf综合，策略规划方法，可迁移至agent规划

TL;DR: 提出最优LTLf合成方法，在规范不可全部实现时最大化实现目标的数量，包括最大保证合成、最大观察合成和增量最大观察合成，实验证明可行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统策略合成采用全有或全无范式，当规范无法在不确定环境中完全实现时直接返回不可实现，缺乏对部分实现的处理。

Method: 提出三种最优LTLf合成变体：最大保证合成（预先保证最大可满足目标集）、最大观察合成（事后最大化实际实现的目标）、增量最大观察合成（在执行中动态利用更强保证机会）。

Result: 实验表明不同变体扩展性相当，在给定超时内解决了大部分基准实例。

Conclusion: 证明了最优合成方法在实际中的可行性，为处理不可完全实现的规范提供了有效途径。

中文摘要：策略合成通常遵循全有或全无的范式，当规范无法在不确定环境中保证时，返回不可实现。在本文中，我们介绍最优LTLf合成，其目标是从给定由多个目标组成的规范中尽可能多地实现目标，特别是当它们不能全部联合实现时。我们首先考虑最大保证合成，它致力于一组我们能够先验保证实现的最大目标集合。然后，我们引入最大观察合成，它在事后最大化可能在不同执行上不可比较的实现目标。最后，我们提出增量最大观察合成，通过在执行过程中出现更强保证的机会时进一步改进策略。实验结果表明，不同变体的最优合成在规模上大致同样好地扩展，在给定的超时时间内解决大部分基准实例，证明了该方法的实际可行性。

Original abstract: Strategy synthesis typically follows an all-or-nothing paradigm, returning unrealisable whenever a specification cannot be guaranteed in an uncertain environment. In this paper, we introduce optimal LTLf synthesis, where the goal is to realise as many objectives as possible from a given specification consisting of multiple objectives, especially for the case that they are not all jointly realisable. We first consider max-guarantee synthesis, which commits to a maximal set of objectives that we can a priori guarantee to realise. We then introduce max-observation synthesis, which maximises a posteriori realised objectives that may be incomparable on different executions. Finally, we present incremental max-observation synthesis, which further improves strategies by exploiting opportunities for stronger guarantees when they arise during an execution. Experimental results show that different variations of optimal synthesis scale broadly equally well, solving a large fraction of the benchmark instances within the given timeout, demonstrating the practical feasibility of the approach.

</details>


### [36] [Hindsight Hint Distillation: Scaffolded Reasoning for SWE Agents from CoT-free Answers](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11556v1)
*Shengjie Wang,Guanghe Li,Zonghan Yang,Yang Gao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: HHD为SWE agent合成推理路径，直接提升SWE-bench性能，强相关

TL;DR: 提出HHD方法，从无CoT数据中合成事后提示，自蒸馏提升长期任务性能，在SWE-bench上绝对提升8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 获取带有显式思维链推理过程的数据集成本高，需要仅利用易获取的问答对来提升模型在复杂长期任务上的规划与推理能力。

Method: HHD从模型自身的失败自rollout中合成事后提示，用于支撑成功完成任务的在策略rollout，然后模型自蒸馏这些被支撑的轨迹，并在无提示指导下泛化到新问题。

Result: 在SWE-bench Verified上绝对提升8%（基线仅提升约2%），且推理策略有效泛化到分布外任务（如SWE-bench Multilingual）。

Conclusion: HHD能有效从无CoT数据中合成专家级推理，显著提升长期任务性能，并具有良好的泛化能力。

中文摘要：解决复杂的长期任务需要强大的规划和推理能力。尽管带有显式思维链（CoT）推理过程的数据集可以显著促进学习，但获取它们的成本很高。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出了事后提示蒸馏（Hindsight Hint Distillation, HHD），该方法仅需要易于获取的问答对，而无需CoT注释。受人类教师利用学生错误提供针对性指导的启发，HHD从模型自身的失败自 rollout 中合成事后提示，并利用这些提示来支撑成功完成任务的在策略 rollout。然后，模型自蒸馏这些被支撑的轨迹，并在没有提示指导的情况下泛化到新问题。实验表明，HHD显著优于迭代RFT和轨迹合成基线，在SWE-bench Verified上实现了8%的绝对改进，而所有基线的改进仅为约2%。值得注意的是，HHD诱导的推理策略有效泛化到分布外任务，在SWE-bench Multilingual上取得了最大收益，尽管没有在多语言数据上训练。这些结果表明，HHD能够有效地从无CoT数据中合成专家级别的推理，并显著提升长期任务性能。

Original abstract: Solving complex long-horizon tasks requires strong planning and reasoning capabilities. Although datasets with explicit chain-of-thought (CoT) rationales can substantially benefit learning, they are costly to obtain. To address this challenge, we propose Hindsight Hint Distillation (HHD), which only requires easy-to-obtain question-answer pairs without CoT annotations. Inspired by how human teachers use student mistakes to provide targeted guidance, HHD synthesizes hindsight hints from the model's own failed self-rollouts and uses them to scaffold on-policy rollouts that successfully complete the tasks. The model then self-distills these scaffolded trajectories and generalizes to new problems without hint guidance. Experiments show that HHD significantly outperforms iterative RFT and trajectory-synthesis baselines, achieving an absolute improvement of 8\% on SWE-bench Verified, while all baselines improve by only around 2\%. Notably, the reasoning strategies induced by HHD generalize effectively to out-of-distribution tasks, yielding the largest gains on SWE-bench Multilingual despite no training on multilingual data. These results demonstrate that HHD can effectively synthesize expert-like reasoning from CoT-free data and substantially improve long-horizon performance.

</details>


### [37] [CuSearch: Curriculum Rollout Sampling via Search Depth for Agentic RAG](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11611v2)
*Jianghan Shen,Siqi Luo,Xinyu Cheng,Jing Xiong,Yue Li,Jiyao Liu,Jiashi Lin,Yirong Chen,Junjun He*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出课程 rollout 采样框架用于训练 agentic RAG，提升搜索深度利用，属于通用 agent 训练方法。

TL;DR: 提出CuSearch框架，通过基于搜索深度的课程采样策略，在RLVR训练中优先利用深搜索轨迹，显著提升agentic RAG系统的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR训练中均匀采样所有轨迹，忽略了不同轨迹在搜索深度上的信息量差异，导致训练效率低下。

Method: 提出CuSearch框架，包含SDGA-Auto（始终选择最深轨迹）和SDGA-Phase（动态推进深度阈值）两种调度策略，在批次级别重新分配更新预算至深搜索轨迹。

Result: 在ZeroSearch等任务上，CuSearch相比标准GRPO提升高达11.8个精确匹配点，且跨模型和检索框架表现一致。

Conclusion: 每条轨迹的搜索深度可作为RLVR训练中检索监督密度的有效、无注释代理指标，指导课程采样。

中文摘要：基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为一种有前途的范式，用于仅从结果监督中训练代理型检索增强生成（RAG）系统。大多数现有方法从均匀采样的轨迹中优化策略，隐含地认为所有轨迹信息量相等。然而，轨迹在搜索深度上存在显著差异，因此信息量并不相同：更深搜索的轨迹包含更多的检索决策点，并为检索子策略提供更密集的直接监督。此外，随着训练过程中批次内深度分布向更高值偏移，这种异质性会增加，而均匀轨迹采样对这种偏移视而不见。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了CuSearch，一种基于搜索深度贪婪分配（SDGA）的课程轨迹采样框架，SDGA是一种批量级算子，将固定的更新预算重新分配给更深搜索的轨迹。SDGA-Auto始终针对当前批次中最深的可用轨迹，随着深度分布上移，产生隐式的训练对齐课程。SDGA-Phase在更深轨迹变得足够丰富时明确推进课程阈值。跨模型类型和检索框架的实验表明，CuSearch持续提升了性能，在ZeroSearch上相比标准GRPO最高提升了11.8个精确匹配点。这些结果确立了每条轨迹的搜索深度作为RLVR-based代理型RAG训练中检索监督密度的可靠、无需注释的代理指标。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a promising paradigm for training agentic retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems from outcome-only supervision. Most existing methods optimize policies from uniformly sampled rollouts, implicitly treating all trajectories as equally informative. However, trajectories differ substantially in search depth and are therefore not equally informative: deeper-search trajectories contain more retrieval decision points and provide denser direct supervision for the retrieval sub-policy. Moreover, this heterogeneity grows over training as the within-batch depth distribution shifts toward higher values, yet uniform rollout sampling remains blind to this shift. To address this, we propose CuSearch, a curriculum rollout sampling framework built on Search-Depth Greedy Allocation (SDGA), a batch-level operator that reallocates a fixed update budget toward deeper-search trajectories. SDGA-Auto always targets the deepest available trajectories in the current batch, yielding an implicit training-aligned curriculum as the depth distribution shifts upward. SDGA-Phase explicitly advances the curriculum threshold as deeper trajectories become sufficiently abundant. Experiments across model types and retrieval frameworks show that CuSearch consistently improves performance, achieving up to 11.8 exact-match points over standard GRPO on ZeroSearch. These results establish per-trajectory search depth as a reliable, annotation-free proxy for retrieval supervision density in RLVR-based agentic RAG training.

</details>


### [38] [Nice Fold or Hero Call: Learning Budget-Efficient Thinking for Adaptive Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11625v1)
*Zhaomeng Zhou,Lan Zhang,Junyang Wang,Mu Yuan,Junda Lin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出预算高效思考框架，让 LLM 自适应分配推理预算，属于通用 agent 推理规划方法。

TL;DR: 提出预算高效思维框架，根据推理预期回报自适应分配计算，减少约55%推理token并提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有效率方法忽略可解性，导致在不可解问题上浪费计算，而在困难但可解问题上压缩推理，造成预算错配。

Method: 两阶段框架，结合行为冷启动与投资成本感知奖励下的GRPO，将解决或放弃决策与rollout衍生的可解性对齐，学习短解、好弃和英雄调用三种行为。

Result: 在7个基准和3个基础模型上，平均减少约55%推理token，同时整体性能提升，并零样本迁移到科学QA和逻辑推理任务。

Conclusion: BET通过将预算分配与推理预期回报对齐，有效提升推理效率，实现计算节约与性能改进的平衡。

中文摘要：大型推理模型（LRMs）通过扩展推理改进问题求解，但往往错误分配测试时计算。现有的效率方法通过压缩推理痕迹或根据感知难度调节预算来降低计算成本，却在很大程度上忽略了可解性。因此，它们可能在超出模型能力的问题上耗费大量预算，同时压缩需要更深层推理的困难但可解的问题。在本文中，我们将自适应推理形式化为不确定性下的计算投资，其中预算应遵循推理的预期回报，而不仅仅是感知难度。为了实例化这一原则，我们提出了预算高效思维（BET），一个两阶段框架，将行为冷启动与投资成本感知奖励下的GRPO相结合。通过将解决或放弃决策与rollout衍生的可解性对齐，BET学习三种行为：（1）短解：简洁地回答简单问题；（2）好弃：当继续推理的预期回报接近零时尽早放弃；（3）英雄调用：为困难但可解的问题保留足够的计算。在七个基准和三个基础模型上，BET平均减少约55%的推理token，同时实现整体性能提升，并且从数学推理零样本迁移到科学QA和逻辑推理，具有可比的效率提升。

Original abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) improve problem solving through extended reasoning, but often misallocate test-time compute. Existing efficiency methods reduce cost by compressing reasoning traces or conditioning budget on perceived difficulty, yet largely overlook solvability. As a result, they may spend large budgets on queries beyond the model's capability while compressing hard-but-solvable queries that require deeper reasoning. In this work, we formulate adaptive reasoning as a computational investment under uncertainty, where budget should follow the expected return of reasoning rather than perceived difficulty alone. To instantiate this principle, we propose Budget-Efficient Thinking (BET), a two-stage framework that combines behavioral cold-start with GRPO under an investment-cost-aware reward. By aligning solve-or-fold decisions with rollout-derived solvability, BET learns three behaviors: (1) short solve, answering easy queries concisely; (2) nice fold, abstaining early when continued reasoning has near-zero expected return; and (3) hero call, preserving sufficient compute for hard-but-solvable queries. Across seven benchmarks and three base models, BET reduces reasoning tokens by ~55% on average while achieving overall performance improvements, and transfers zero-shot from mathematical reasoning to scientific QA and logical reasoning with comparable efficiency gains.

</details>


### [39] [Can LLM Agents Respond to Disasters? Benchmarking Heterogeneous Geospatial Reasoning in Emergency Operations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11633v1)
*Junjue Wang,Weihao Xuan,Heli Qi,Pengyu Dai,Kunyi Liu,Hongruixuan Chen,Zhuo Zheng,Junshi Xia,Stefano Ermon,Naoto Yokoya*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 发布端到端灾害响应 agent benchmark，涉及多工具使用、规划与长程执行，可直接迁移至 agent 评测。

TL;DR: 提出了首个端到端灾害响应智能体基准DORA，包含515个任务和3500步金标准轨迹，评估13个LLM发现三大挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作孤立遥感感知或通用工具，未探索端到端应急操作流程。

Method: 构建DORA基准，包含45个事件、515个专家任务、5个维度（感知、空间关系、救援规划、时间推理、报告合成）和108工具MCP库，评估13个LLM。

Result: LLM在灾害领域理解、工具选择与参数理解、长流程组合脆弱性上表现不足，金标准提示提升有限。

Conclusion: DORA为操作可靠的灾害响应智能体提供了严格的测试平台。

中文摘要：灾害响应操作不仅限于损害评估，还要求响应者整合多传感器信号、推理道路网络、人口和关键设施、规划疏散并生成可操作报告。然而，先前的工作大多孤立地进行遥感感知或评估通用工具使用，忽视了应急操作的端到端流程。本文介绍了灾害操作响应智能体基准（DORA），这是首个面向端到端灾害响应的智能体基准：包含45个真实世界灾害事件（涵盖10种类型）中的515个专家编写任务，并配有专家验证、可回放的金标准轨迹，总计3,500个工具调用步骤。任务涵盖五个维度，覆盖操作灾害响应流程：灾害感知、空间关系分析、救援与疏散规划、时间演化推理以及多模态报告合成。智能体通过一个包含108个工具的MCP库对异构地理空间数据进行调用：光学、SAR和多光谱影像（单时相、双时相和多时相序列，GSD 0.015-10米），辅以高程和社会矢量图层。我们在基准上全面评估了13个前沿大语言模型，揭示了三个持续存在的挑战：1）灾害领域理解暴露了独特的失败模式（损害语义理解、传感器模态不匹配和灾害流程组合）；2）智能体在工具选择和参数理解上存在双重瓶颈，其中金标准工具顺序提示仅将准确率提高1.08-4.40%，替代框架最多获得3.24%的提升；3）组合脆弱性随轨迹长度增加，智能体与金标准之间的差距在长流程上从7%扩大到56%。DORA为操作上可靠的灾害响应智能体建立了一个严格的测试平台。

Original abstract: Operational disaster response goes beyond damage assessment, requiring responders to integrate multi-sensor signals, reason over road networks, populations and key facilities, plan evacuations, and produce actionable reports. However, prior work largely isolates remote-sensing perception or evaluates generic tool use, leaving the end-to-end workflows of emergency operations underexplored. In this paper, we introduce Disaster Operational Response Agent benchmark (DORA), the first agentic benchmark for end-to-end disaster response: 515 expert-authored tasks across 45 real-world disaster events spanning 10 types, paired with expert-verified, replayable gold trajectories totaling 3,500 tool-call steps. Tasks span five dimensions that cover the operational disaster-response pipeline: disaster perception, spatial relational analysis, rescue and evacuation planning, temporal evolution reasoning, and multi-modal report synthesis. Agents compose calls from a 108-tool MCP library over heterogeneous geospatial data: optical, SAR, and multi-spectral imagery across single-, bi-, and multi-temporal sequences (0.015-10m GSD), complemented by elevation and social vector layers. We comprehensively evaluate 13 frontier LLMs on our benchmark, revealing three persistent challenges: 1) disaster-domain grounding exposes unique failure modes (damage-semantic grounding, sensor-modality mismatch, and disaster-pipeline composition); 2) agents are doubly bottlenecked by tool selection and argument grounding, where gold tool-order hints improve accuracy by only 1.08-4.40%, and alternative scaffolds yield at most a 3.24% gain; 3) compositional fragility scales with trajectory length, the agent-to-gold gap widening from 7% to 56% on long pipelines. DORA establishes a rigorous testbed for operationally reliable disaster-response agents.

### [40] [Seirênes: Adversarial Self-Play with Evolving Distractions for LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11636v1)
*Chi Zhang,Haibo Qiu,Qiming Zhang,Yufei Xu,Xinbo Gao,Jing Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自对弈RL框架，通过对抗干扰提升推理鲁棒性，通用方法可迁移到 agent 推理。

TL;DR: Seirênes是一个自我对弈RL框架，通过让模型自生成干扰上下文并解决问题，显著提升LLM在非理想化上下文中的推理鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在非理想化上下文（如多余信息、干扰指令）中推理脆弱，Seirênes旨在利用这种脆弱性转化为训练信号以增强鲁棒性。

Method: 采用参数共享的对抗性自我对弈循环，训练单个模型同时扮演干扰者（构造合理但使人分心的上下文）和求解者（从扰动中恢复核心逻辑），通过竞争目标实现共同进化。

Result: 在7个数学推理基准上，对4B至30B模型分别取得+10.2、+9.1、+7.2平均提升；4B模型产生的干扰上下文使GPT和Gemini准确率下降4-5点。

Conclusion: Seirênes有效将上下文干扰转化为内部训练信号，迫使模型超越模式匹配，锚定稳健推理，并通过自我博弈持续提升；其干扰上下文具有通用性，能暴露其他模型的盲点。

中文摘要：我们提出了Seirênes，这是一个自我对弈的强化学习框架，它将上下文干扰从LLM推理的失败模式转化为内部训练信号，用于共同进化更具韧性的推理者。虽然具有可验证奖励的RL显著提升了推理能力，但在遇到非理想化上下文时，模型仍可能表现出脆弱性：这些场景具有多余信息、非相关指令或与标准基准典型干净分布不同的偶然相关性。Seirênes通过参数共享和对抗性自我对弈循环来利用这种脆弱性。在此框架内，单个模型被训练来构造既合理又令人分心的上下文，暴露其自身的推理盲点，并通过从这些扰动中辨别出基本任务来恢复核心底层逻辑，从而解决问题。通过将这些相互竞争的目标相互对抗，Seirênes迫使模型超越表面模式匹配，并将其能力锚定在稳健的底层推理上。这种持续的互动维持了一个信息丰富的共同进化课程，随着模型的改进。在七个数学推理基准和模型规模从4B到30B的实验中，Seirênes分别实现了平均+10.2、+9.1和+7.2分的提升。此外，由4B Seirênes模型产生的令人分心的上下文将顶级闭源模型（GPT和Gemini）的准确率降低了大约4-5个百分点，揭示了Seirênes揭示推理模型盲点的普遍能力。

Original abstract: We present Seirênes, a self-play RL framework that transforms contextual interference from a failure mode of LLM reasoning into an internal training signal for co-evolving more resilient reasoners. While RL with verifiable rewards has significantly advanced reasoning capabilities, models can still exhibit fragility when encountering non-idealized contexts: scenarios characterized by superfluous information, tangential instructions, or incidental correlations that differ from the clean distributions typical of standard benchmarks. Seirênes harnesses this vulnerability through a parameter-shared and adversarial self-play loop. Within this framework, a single model is trained to both construct plausible yet distracting contexts that expose its own reasoning blind spots, and solve problems by discerning the essential task from these perturbations to recover the core underlying logic. By pitting these competing objectives against each other, Seirênes compels the model to move beyond superficial pattern matching and anchors its capabilities in robust underlying reasoning. This continuous interaction sustains an informative co-evolutionary curriculum as the model improves. Across seven mathematical reasoning benchmarks and model scales from 4B to 30B, Seirênes achieves average gains of +10.2, +9.1, and +7.2 points. Besides, distracting contexts produced by the 4B Seirênes model reduce the accuracy of top-tier closed-source models (GPT and Gemini) by roughly 4--5 points, revealing Seirênes' general ability to uncover reasoning models' blind spots.

</details>


### [41] [Toward Stable Value Alignment: Introducing Independent Modules for Consistent Value Guidance](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11712v1)
*Wenhao Chen,Sirui Sun,Shengyuan Bai,Guojie Song*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 独立价值模块引导生成，可迁移到 agent 安全控制。

TL;DR: 提出SVGT，通过独立价值观模块和桥接令牌实现稳定价值观对齐，降低有害分数70%以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖后训练或推理时操作参数，但残差流中价值观不稳定，需要更稳定的架构。

Method: 设计独立价值观模块，包含独立价值观建模和显式行为引导，通过可学习桥接令牌影响生成。

Result: 在多个模型和安全基准上，有害分数降低超70%，生成流畅性保持。

Conclusion: SVGT通过架构性价值观建模有效对齐模型行为，代码已开源。

中文摘要：将大型语言模型（LLM）与人类价值观对齐通常依赖于后训练或推理时的引导，直接操作主干网络的参数或表示空间。然而，一个关键差距存在：模型的残差流高度动态，其中价值观作为脆弱、低维的属性存在，本质上与一致价值观表达所需的稳定性不相容。在本文中，我们提出了稳定价值观引导变换器（SVGT），通过一个独立的价值观模块解决了这一差距，该模块包含两个关键设计：（1）独立的价值观建模，在独立于主干网络的专用价值观空间中维护规范性表示，以及（2）显式行为引导，将这些稳定信号转化为可学习的潜在桥接令牌。这些令牌作为动态价值观锚点，显式地引导生成轨迹，确保在不同上下文中鲁棒地遵守，而不会干扰主干网络的内部表示。在多个主干网络和安全基准上的实验表明，SVGT通常将有害分数降低超过70%，同时保持生成流畅性，证明了基于架构的价值观建模的有效性。我们的代码可在https://github.com/Clervils/SVGT.git获取。

Original abstract: Aligning large language models (LLMs) with human values typically relies on post-training or inference-time steering that directly manipulates the backbone's parameters or representation space. However, a critical gap exists: the model's residual stream is highly dynamic, in which values exist as fragile, low-dimensional properties, inherently incompatible with the stability required for consistent value expression. In this paper, we propose the Stable Value Guidance Transformer (SVGT), which addresses this gap through an independent value module incorporating two key designs: (1) independent value modeling, maintaining normative representations in a dedicated value space isolated from the backbone, and (2) explicit behavioral guidance, transducing these stable signals into learnable latent Bridge Tokens. These tokens serve as dynamic value anchors to explicitly steer the generative trajectory, ensuring robust adherence across diverse contexts without disrupting the backbone's internal representations. Experiments across multiple backbones and safety benchmarks show that SVGT generally reduces harmful scores by over 70% while maintaining generation fluency, demonstrating the efficacy of architecturally grounded value modeling. Our code is available at https://github.com/Clervils/SVGT.git.

### [42] [SafeSteer: A Decoding-level Defense Mechanism for Multimodal Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11716v1)
*Xinyi Zeng,Xue Yang,Jingyuan Zhang,Huanqian Yan,Xiang Chen,Kaiwen Wei,Hankun Kang,Yu Tian*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 解码级防御机制，可迁移到 agent 安全推理。

TL;DR: 提出SafeSteer，一种无需微调的解码级防御机制，通过轻量级探测器和模态语义对齐向量提升多模态大语言模型的安全性，平衡有用性与无害性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MLLM越狱防御方法依赖昂贵的微调或低效的事后干预，难以应对新型攻击且存在性能权衡，需要一种高效、无需微调的防御策略。

Method: SafeSteer包括Decoding-Probe（解码探测器）和模态语义对齐向量。Decoding-Probe在解码时检测并纠正有害输出，迭代引导安全方向；对齐向量将文本安全对齐迁移至视觉模态。

Result: 在多个MLLMs上，SafeSteer将安全性提升高达33.40%，无需微调，且保持模型有效性，实现有用性与无害性的平衡。

中文摘要：多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）正受到越来越多的关注。由于其输入特征的异质性，它们在越狱防御方面面临重大挑战。当前的防御方法依赖于昂贵的微调或低效的事后干预，限制了它们应对新型攻击的能力，并涉及性能权衡。为了解决上述问题，我们探索了MLLMs内部固有的安全能力，并量化了它们在解码阶段辨别有害性的内在能力。我们观察到：1）MLLMs可以在解码过程中区分有害和无害输入，2）基于图像的攻击更具隐蔽性。基于这些见解，我们引入了SafeSteer，一种针对MLLMs的解码级防御机制。具体来说，它包含一个Decoding-Probe，一个轻量级的探测器，用于在解码过程中检测和纠正有害输出，迭代地将解码过程导向安全。此外，还集成了一个模态语义对齐向量，将强大的文本安全对齐转移到视觉模态。在多个MLLMs上的实验表明，SafeSteer可以在不进行微调的情况下将MLLMs的安全性提升高达33.40%。值得注意的是，它可以保持MLLMs的有效性，确保其有用性和无害性之间的平衡。

Original abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are gaining increasing attention. Due to the heterogeneity of their input features, they face significant challenges in terms of jailbreak defenses. Current defense methods rely on costly fine-tuning or inefficient post-hoc interventions, limiting their ability to address novel attacks and involving performance trade-offs. To address the above issues, we explore the inherent safety capabilities within MLLMs and quantify their intrinsic ability to discern harmfulness at decoding stage. We observe that 1) MLLMs can distinguish the harmful and harmless inputs during decoding process, 2) Image-based attacks are more stealthy. Based on these insights, we introduce SafeSteer, a decoding-level defense mechanism for MLLMs. Specifically, it includes a Decoding-Probe, a lightweight probe for detecting and correcting harmful output during decoding, which iteratively steers the decoding process toward safety. Furthermore, a modal semantic alignment vector is integrated to transfer the strong textual safety alignment to the vision modality. Experiments on multiple MLLMs demonstrate that SafeSterr can improve MLLMs' safety by up to 33.40\% without fine-tuning. Notably, it can maintain the effectiveness of MLLMs, ensuring a balance between their helpfulness and harmlessness.

### [43] [OptArgus: A Multi-Agent System to Detect Hallucinations in LLM-based Optimization Modeling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11738v1)
*Zhong Li,Zihan Guo,Xiaohan Lu,Juntao Wang,Jie Song,Chao Shen,Jiageng Wu,Mingyang Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent系统用于优化建模中的幻觉检测，提出细粒度分类和模块化审计架构，可迁移至coding agent的验证与调试。

TL;DR: 本文提出优化建模幻觉检测问题，开发了细粒度分类法和多智能体检测器OptArgus，实验表明其优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仅通过匹配参考目标值来验证LLM生成的优化工件不可靠，因为数值一致可能掩盖语义错误。

Method: 设计了细粒度幻觉分类法（目标、变量、约束、实现失败），基于该分类法构建多智能体检测器OptArgus（含指挥路由、专业审计员、证据整合），并创建了三部分基准套件进行评测。

Result: 与单智能体基线相比，OptArgus在干净工件上误报率更低，在单错误案例中定位更准确，在自然LLM生成工件上检测能力更强。

Conclusion: 将优化建模幻觉检测转化为具体实证问题，表明模块化、基于分类法的审计是提升优化建模可靠性的实用途径。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地被用于将自然语言优化问题翻译成数学公式和求解器代码，但匹配参考目标值并不可靠：一个工件可能在数值上一致，同时却改变了底层的优化语义。我们将此问题定义为“优化建模幻觉检测”，即对问题描述、符号模型和求解器实现进行结构一致性审计。据我们所知，我们开发了第一个专门针对优化建模的细粒度幻觉分类法，涵盖目标、变量、约束和实现失败。我们利用该分类法设计了OptArgus，一个具有指挥路由、专业审计员和证据整合的多智能体检测器。为了评估该设置，我们引入了一个三部分基准套件，包含484个干净工件、1266个受控注入工件和6292个自然LLM生成的工件。与匹配的单智能体基线相比，OptArgus在干净工件上产生更少的误报，在受控单错误案例上具有更准确的排名靠前的定位，并在自然模型输出上具有更强的检测能力。这些贡献共同将优化建模幻觉检测转变为具体的实证问题，并表明模块化、基于分类法的审计是实现更可靠优化建模的实用途径。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to translate natural-language optimization problems into mathematical formulations and solver code, but matching the reference objective value is not a reliable test of correctness: an artifact may agree numerically while still changing the underlying optimization semantics. We formulate this issue as \emph{optimization-modeling hallucination detection}, namely structural consistency auditing over the problem description, symbolic model, and solver implementation. We develop, to our knowledge, the first fine-grained hallucination taxonomy specifically for optimization modeling, spanning objective, variable, constraint, and implementation failures. We use this taxonomy to design OptArgus, a multi-agent detector with conductor routing, specialist auditors, and evidence consolidation. To evaluate this setting, we introduce a three-part benchmark suite with $484$ clean artifacts, $1266$ controlled injected artifacts, and $6292$ natural LLM-generated artifacts. Against a matched single-agent baseline, OptArgus produces fewer false alarms on clean artifacts, more accurate top-ranked localization on controlled single-error cases, and stronger detection on natural model outputs. Together, these contributions turn optimization-modeling hallucination detection into a concrete empirical problem and suggest that modular, taxonomy-grounded auditing is a practical route to more reliable optimization modeling.

</details>


### [44] [When Reasoning Traces Become Performative: Step-Level Evidence that Chain-of-Thought Is an Imperfect Oversight Channel](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11746v1)
*Wenkai Li,Fan Yang,Ananya Hazarika,Shaunak A. Mehta,Koichi Onoue*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 揭示CoT推理轨迹的忠实性缺陷，对依赖CoT的agent设计有潜在警示与启发。

TL;DR: 思维链轨迹与模型实际答案形成时间经常不同步，大多数失配表现为虚构延续，且后承诺文本对最终答案不重要，但CoT仍然有用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证思维链（CoT）轨迹是否与决定答案的计算过程保持同步，因为CoT轨迹被广泛用于提升性能和审计，但假设可能不成立。

Method: 提出分步检测-分类-比较框架，使用答案承诺代理（通过Patchscopes、调谐透镜探针和因果方向消融验证），在九个模型和七个基准上分析对齐性，并进行架构匹配比较、配对截断和捐赠者-污染测试。

Result: 平均仅61.9%的步骤对齐；58%的失配是虚构延续（答案已定但轨迹继续）；较低对齐与更大CoT效用相关；后承诺文本对最终答案不关键。

Conclusion: CoT虽有用，但时间上不可靠，其文本常与答案形成时刻脱节，需谨慎解释。

中文摘要：思维链（CoT）轨迹越来越多地被用于提升语言模型能力和审计模型行为，这隐含地假设可见轨迹与决定答案的计算保持同步。我们通过一个基于答案承诺代理的分步检测-分类-比较框架来检验这一假设，该代理使用Patchscopes、调谐透镜探针和因果方向消融进行交叉验证。在九个模型和七个推理基准上，潜在承诺与明确答案到达平均仅在61.9%的步骤上对齐。主要的失配模式是虚构延续：在检测到的失配事件中，58.0%发生在答案承诺代理已经稳定之后，而轨迹继续产生看似深思熟虑的文本，并且空洞分析表明在这些步骤中承诺的答案没有改变。在架构匹配的Qwen2.5/DeepSeek-R1-Distill比较中，推理流程改变失败组成的程度超过聚合对齐，最明显的是在32B规模，虚构步骤减少而矛盾状态增加。较低的分步对齐与更大的CoT效用相关，表明从CoT受益最大的设置往往在时间上最不可靠。配对截断和互补的捐赠者-污染测试进一步表明，大量承诺后文本对最终答案并不承载关键信息。这些发现表明，CoT可以保持有用，同时仍然是对答案形成时间不可靠的报告。

Original abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) traces are increasingly used both to improve language model capability and to audit model behavior, implicitly assuming that the visible trace remains synchronized with the computation that determines the answer. We test this assumption with a step-level Detect-Classify-Compare framework built around an answer-commitment proxy that is cross-validated with Patchscopes, tuned-lens probes, and causal direction ablation. Across nine models and seven reasoning benchmarks, latent commitment and explicit answer arrival align on only 61.9% of steps on average. The dominant mismatch pattern is confabulated continuation: 58.0% of detected mismatch events occur after the answer-commitment proxy has already stabilized while the trace continues producing deliberative-looking text, and a vacuousness analysis shows that the committed answer does not change during these steps. In architecture-matched Qwen2.5/DeepSeek-R1-Distill comparisons, the reasoning pipeline changes failure composition more than aggregate alignment, most clearly at 32B where confabulated steps decrease as contradictory states increase. Lower step-level alignment is also associated with larger CoT utility, suggesting that the settings that benefit most from CoT are often the least temporally faithful. Paired truncation and a complementary donor-corruption test further indicate that much post-commitment text is not load-bearing for the final answer. These findings suggest that CoT can remain useful while still being an unreliable report of when the answer was formed.

</details>


### [45] [Beyond Inefficiency: Systemic Costs of Incivility in Multi-Agent Monte Carlo Simulations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11789v1)
*Alison Moldovan-Mauer,Benedikt Mangold*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent蒙特卡洛模拟研究不文明沟通对效率的影响，虽非软件工程，但揭示了多agent协作动力学。

TL;DR: 本研究利用基于LLM的多智能体系统作为可控社会学沙盒，通过蒙特卡洛模拟生成对抗性辩论，发现有毒行为导致收敛延迟，且小模型延迟更大，同时存在显著的首动优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统人类受试者研究受伦理、可重复性和自然场景不可预测性限制，难以隔离沟通行为对效率的影响，故需要一种可控、可规模化的方法。

Method: 使用基于大语言模型的多智能体系统，结合蒙特卡洛模拟框架，生成不同毒性条件下的结构化1对1对抗性辩论，测量收敛时间（轮数）作为效率指标。

Result: 确认先前研究25%的收敛延迟，且参数较少的模型延迟显著更大；发现显著的首动优势，即先手智能体获胜率高于随机。

Conclusion: LLM多智能体系统可作为研究沟通行为的社会学沙盒，有毒行为对效率的影响跨模型规模泛化，且首动优势为新的发现。

中文摘要：非建设性辩论和不文明沟通对生产力和凝聚力带来的成本已有充分记录，但隔离它们对运营效率的影响已被证明是困难的。该领域的人类受试者研究受到伦理监督、有限的可重复性以及自然环境中固有的不可预测性的限制。我们通过利用基于大语言模型的多智能体系统作为受控的社会学沙盒来填补这一空白，使得能够在规模上系统性地操纵沟通行为。使用蒙特卡洛模拟框架，我们在不同毒性条件下生成了数千场结构化的1对1对抗性辩论，测量收敛时间（定义为达成结论所需的轮数）作为交互效率的代理指标。基于先前的研究，我们在两个额外不同参数规模的LLM智能体上复制并扩展了其发现，从而能够评估有毒行为对辩论动态的影响是否跨模型规模泛化。先前研究报告的25%的收敛延迟得到了确认。发现对于参数较少的模型，这个延迟显著更大。我们进一步识别出显著的首动优势，即发起讨论的智能体无论毒性条件如何，其获胜率显著高于随机水平。

Original abstract: Unconstructive debate and uncivil communication carry well-documented costs for productivity and cohesion, yet isolating their effect on operational efficiency has proven difficult. Human subject research in this domain is constrained by ethical oversight, limited reproducibility, and the inherent unpredictability of naturalistic settings. We address this gap by leveraging Large Language Model (LLM) based Multi-Agent Systems as a controlled sociological sandbox, enabling systematic manipulation of communicative behavior at scale. Using a Monte Carlo simulation framework, we generate thousands of structured 1-on-1 adversarial debates across varying toxicity conditions, measuring convergence time, defined as the number of rounds required to reach a conclusion, as a proxy for interactional efficiency. Building on a prior study, we replicate and extend its findings across two additional LLM agents of varying parameter size, allowing us to assess whether the effects of toxic behavior on debate dynamics generalize across model scale. The convergence latency of 25% reported in the previous study was confirmed. It was found that this latency is significantly bigger for models with fewer parameters. We further identify a significant first-mover advantage, whereby the agent initiating the discussion wins significantly above chance regardless of toxicity condition.

### [46] [Why Users Go There: World Knowledge-Augmented Generative Next POI Recommendation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11807v1)
*Qiuyu Ding,Heng-Da Xu,Wei Zhang,Dongyi Lv,Changda Xia,Feng Xiong,Mu Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent生成上下文叙事增强推荐，虽领域不同，但agent利用外部知识的方式有迁移潜力。

TL;DR: 提出AWARE模型，利用LLM代理生成时空感知的上下文叙述，将外部世界知识融入个性化推荐，显著提升POI推荐性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成式POI推荐模型知识固定，无法感知动态现实世界条件（如本地事件、文化趋势）对用户移动决策的影响。

Method: 采用LLM代理为每个用户生成位置和时间感知的上下文叙述，捕捉区域文化、季节趋势和当前事件，并将其锚定在用户行为上下文中。

Result: 在三个真实数据集上，AWARE始终优于基线，相对改进最高达12.4%。

Conclusion: AWARE通过整合外部世界知识并个性化叙事，有效提升了LLM在POI推荐中的适应性和准确性。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型（LLM）的生成式兴趣点（POI）推荐模型通过将下一个POI预测公式化为序列生成任务，已显示出有希望的结果。然而，这些模型中编码的知识在训练后保持不变，使得它们无法感知不断变化的现实世界条件，这些条件塑造了用户的移动决策，例如本地事件和文化趋势。为弥合这一差距，我们提出了AWARE（基于Agent的世界知识增强推荐），它采用LLM代理生成位置和时间感知的上下文叙述，捕捉与每个用户相关的区域文化特征、季节趋势和当前事件。AWARE并非引入通用或噪声信息，而是进一步将这些叙述锚定在每个用户的行为上下文中，将外部世界知识扎根于个性化的时空模式中。在三个真实世界数据集上的大量实验表明，AWARE始终优于竞争性基线，实现了高达12.4%的相对改进。

Original abstract: Generative point-of-interest (POI) recommendation models based on large language models (LLMs) have shown promising results by formulating next POI prediction as a sequence generation task. However, the knowledge encoded in these models remains fixed after training, making them unable to perceive evolving real-world conditions that shape user mobility decisions, such as local events and cultural trends. To bridge this gap, we propose AWARE (Agent-based World knowledge Augmented REcommendation), which employs an LLM agent to generate location- and time-aware contextual narratives that capture regional cultural characteristics, seasonal trends, and ongoing events relevant to each user. Rather than introducing generic or noisy information, AWARE further anchors these narratives in each user's behavioral context, grounding external world knowledge in personalized spatial-temporal patterns. Extensive experiments on three real-world datasets demonstrate that AWARE consistently outperforms competitive baselines, achieving up to 12.4% relative improvement.

### [47] [Automated Reformulation of Robust Optimization via Memory-Augmented Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11813v1)
*Jinbiao Chen,Shuang Jin,Guoyun Zhang,Junyu Zhang,Guanyi Wang,Hanzhang Qin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 记忆增强的LLM自动化鲁棒优化重构，直接相关自动代码优化与agent经验复用，可迁移性强。

TL;DR: 提出了AutoREM，一种无需调优的记忆增强框架，利用离线学习从失败轨迹中积累经验，显著提升了LLM在鲁棒优化重新表述任务上的准确性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在自动进行鲁棒优化重新表述时仍面临挑战，且缺乏专门的基准测试来评估这类方法。

Method: 提出AutoREM，通过构建结构化文本经验记忆，利用离线适应过程从过去的失败中学习，无需专家知识或参数更新即可提升LLM的重新表述能力。

Result: 实验表明AutoREM在分布内、分布外数据集及多种基础LLM上均能持续提升RO重新表述的准确性和效率。

Conclusion: AutoREM是一种有效的、可迁移的框架，能够增强LLM在鲁棒优化重新表述任务上的性能，且无需额外调优或专家输入。

中文摘要：鲁棒优化（RO）为不确定性下的决策制定提供了一个原则性框架，但其实际应用通常受限于需要手动将不确定优化模型重新表述为易于处理的确定性对应模型。最近的大型语言模型（LLM）已显示出自动化优化表述的前景，但RO重新表述仍然具有挑战性，因为它需要精确的多步推理和数学上一致的转换。为了促进基于LLM的重新表述的系统评估（目前尚无专门的基准测试），我们开发了AutoRO-Bench，这是一个基准测试，具有针对核心RO重新表述任务的自动化数据生成流水线，以及针对RO应用任务的精选数据集。为了解决重新表述的挑战，我们提出了带有经验记忆的自动化重新表述（AutoREM），这是一个无需调优的记忆增强框架，通过定制的离线适应过程反思过去的失败轨迹，自主构建结构化的文本经验记忆。AutoREM既不需要领域特定的专家知识，也不需要参数更新，并且所得记忆可以轻松在不同基础LLM之间迁移。实验结果表明，AutoREM在分布内数据集、分布外数据集以及多样化的基础LLM上，一致地提高了RO重新表述的准确性和效率。

Original abstract: Robust optimization (RO) provides a principled framework for decision-making under uncertainty, but its practical use is often limited by the need to manually reformulate uncertain optimization models into tractable deterministic counterparts. Recent large language models (LLMs) have been shown promising for automating optimization formulation, yet RO reformulation remains challenging because it requires precise multi-step reasoning and mathematically consistent transformations. To facilitate systematic evaluation of LLM-based reformulation, for which no dedicated benchmark currently exists, we develop AutoRO-Bench, a benchmark featuring an automated data generation pipeline for the core RO reformulation task and a curated dataset for the RO application task. To address the reformulation challenge, we propose Automated Reformulation with Experience Memory (AutoREM), a tuning-free memory-augmented framework that autonomously builds a structured textual experience memory by reflecting on past failed trajectories through a tailored offline adaptation procedure. AutoREM requires neither domain-specific expert knowledge nor parameter updates, and the resulting memory readily transfers across different base LLMs. Experimental results show that AutoREM consistently improves the accuracy and efficiency of RO reformulation across in-distribution datasets, out-of-distribution datasets, and diverse base LLMs.

### [48] [MedMemoryBench: Benchmarking Agent Memory in Personalized Healthcare](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11814v1)
*Yihao Wang,Haoran Xu,Renjie Gu,Yixuan Ye,Xinyi Chen,Xinyu Mu,Yuan Gao,Chunxiao Guo,Peng Wei,Jinjie Gu,Huan Li,Ke Chen,Lidan Shou*

TL;DR: MedMemoryBench是一个针对医疗健康代理的高保真、长程记忆基准测试，通过“边构建边评估”协议和记忆饱和研究，揭示了主流架构在复杂医疗推理和噪声鲁棒性上的严重瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用人机协作流水线，基于临床合成的患者原型生成高真实感医疗轨迹，并开创“边构建边评估”的流式评估协议，同时形式化记忆饱和现象。

Result: 构建了包含约2000会话和16000交互轮次的数据集，基准测试显示主流架构在复杂医疗推理和噪声鲁棒性上存在严重瓶颈。

Conclusion: MedMemoryBench暴露了现有记忆机制的根本缺陷，为开发鲁棒、生产就绪的医疗代理奠定了重要基础。

中文摘要：大规模部署个性化医疗健康代理需要极其精确、安全且能够进行长期临床跟踪的记忆机制。然而，现有基准测试主要关注日常开放域对话，未能捕捉现实医疗应用中高风险复杂性。受服务于数千万活跃用户的行业领先健康管理代理的严格生产需求驱动，我们提出MedMemoryBench。我们开发了一个人机协作流水线，基于临床合成的患者原型合成高度真实的长程医疗轨迹。该过程产生了一个大规模、经过专家验证的数据集，包含约2000个会话和16000次交互轮次。关键的是，MedMemoryBench摒弃了传统的静态评估，开创了一种“边构建边评估”的流式评估协议，精确模拟生产环境中的动态记忆积累。此外，我们形式化并系统研究了记忆饱和这一关键现象，即持续的信息输入会主动降低检索和推理的鲁棒性。全面基准测试揭示了主流架构中的严重瓶颈，特别是在复杂医疗推理和噪声鲁棒性方面。通过暴露这些根本缺陷，MedMemoryBench为开发鲁棒、生产就绪的医疗代理奠定了重要基础。

Original abstract: The large-scale deployment of personalized healthcare agents demands memory mechanisms that are exceptionally precise, safe, and capable of long-term clinical tracking. However, existing benchmarks primarily focus on daily open-domain conversations, failing to capture the high-stakes complexity of real-world medical applications. Motivated by the stringent production requirements of an industry-leading health management agent serving tens of millions of active users, we introduce MedMemoryBench. We develop a human-agent collaborative pipeline to synthesize highly realistic, long-horizon medical trajectories based on clinically grounded, synthetic patient archetypes. This process yields a massive, expertly validated dataset comprising approximately 2,000 sessions and 16,000 interaction turns. Crucially, MedMemoryBench departs from traditional static evaluations by pioneering an "evaluate-while-constructing" streaming assessment protocol, which precisely mirrors dynamic memory accumulation in production environments. Furthermore, we formalize and systematically investigate the critical phenomenon of memory saturation, where sustained information influx actively degrades retrieval and reasoning robustness. Comprehensive benchmarking reveals severe bottlenecks in mainstream architectures, particularly concerning complex medical reasoning and noise resilience. By exposing these fundamental flaws, MedMemoryBench establishes a vital foundation for developing robust, production-ready medical agents.

### [49] [SkillSmith: Compiling Agent Skills into Boundary-Guided Runtime Interfaces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15215v1)
*Duling Xu,Zheng Chen,Zaifeng Pan,Jiawei Guan,Dong Dong,Jialin Li,Bangzheng Pu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: SkillSmith 是一个边界优先的编译器-运行时框架，通过离线编译技能为最小可执行接口，动态访问相关组件，显著减少LLM Agent系统中的冗余推理开销和令牌使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能执行范式存在不相关的上下文注入和重复的技能特定推理与规划两类冗余，导致效率低下。

Method: 提出边界优先的编译器-运行时框架SkillSmith，离线提取技能的操作边界并编译为最小可执行接口，运行时仅动态执行相关组件。

Result: 在SkillsBench上，相较原始技能，令牌使用减少57.44%，思考迭代减少42.99%，时间减少50.57%，成本降低57.44%；强模型编译产物可被小模型重用并提升准确率。

Conclusion: SkillSmith通过边界编译有效消除冗余，提升LLM Agent系统的效率和可迁移性。

中文摘要：最近，技能已在基于大型语言模型（LLM）的智能体系统中被广泛采用，涉及各个领域。在现有框架中，技能通常作为上下文指导被注入到智能体推理循环中，一旦匹配到运行时任务，就能实现专门的任务解决能力。我们发现这种执行范式引入了两个主要的冗余来源：不相关的上下文注入和重复的技能特定推理与规划。为此，我们提出了SkillSmith，一种边界优先的编译器-运行时框架，它将技能包离线编译为最小的可执行接口。通过从技能中提取细粒度的操作边界，SkillSmith使智能体能够在运行时动态访问和执行仅相关的组件，从而最大限度地减少不必要的上下文注入和冗余推理开销。在SkillsBench基准上的评估中，与使用原始技能相比，SkillSmith减少了57.44%的解决阶段令牌使用量、42.99%的思考迭代次数、50.57%的解决时间（快2.02倍），以及57.44%的令牌比例货币成本。此外，由更强大模型生成的编译产物可以被更小或更高效的运行时模型重用，在原始技能解释失败的情况下提高任务准确性。源代码和数据可在https://github.com/AetherHeart-AI/Aeloon获取。

Original abstract: Recently, skills have been widely adopted in large language model (LLM)-based agent systems across various domains. In existing frameworks, skills are typically injected into the agent reasoning loop as contextual guidance once matched to a runtime task, enabling specialized task-solving capabilities. We find that this execution paradigm introduces two major sources of redundancy: irrelevant context injection and repeated skill-specific reasoning and planning. To this end, we propose SkillSmith, a boundary-first compiler-runtime framework that compiles skill packages offline into minimal executable interfaces. By extracting fine-grained operational boundaries from skills, SkillSmith enables agents to dynamically access and execute only the relevant components at runtime, thereby minimizing unnecessary context injection and redundant reasoning overhead. In the evaluation on SkillsBench benchmark, SkillSmith reduces solve-stage token usage by 57.44%, thinking iterations by 42.99%, solve time by 50.57% (2.02x faster), and token-proportional monetary cost by 57.44% compared with using raw-skills. Moreover, compiled artifacts produced by a stronger model can be reused by a smaller or more efficient runtime model, improving task accuracy in cases where raw skill interpretation fails. The source code and data are available at https://github.com/AetherHeart-AI/Aeloon.

</details>


### [50] [On-Policy Self-Evolution via Failure Trajectories for Agentic Safety Alignment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11882v1)
*Bo Yin,Qi Li,Xinchao Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 基于失败轨迹的在线自进化框架，提升agent安全对齐，方法论可迁移到coding agent安全与自我改进

TL;DR: 提出FATE框架，通过将失败轨迹转化为修复监督并采用帕累托前沿策略优化，实现了安全与效用的平衡，显著提升了LLM代理的安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全对齐方法存在安全-效用权衡，且信号稀疏（响应级或离策略），限制了实际部署。

Method: 提出FATE，一个在策略自演化框架，利用验证器评分的失败轨迹生成修复候选，经多维度过滤后作为密集轨迹级监督信号；并引入PFPO，结合监督热身和帕累托感知优化以兼顾安全与效用。

Result: 在AgentDojo、AgentHarm和ATBench上，FATE使攻击成功率降低33.5%，有害顺从降低82.6%，外部轨迹安全诊断提升6.5%。

Conclusion: 失败的轨迹可以提供结构化的修复监督，用于自演化代理的安全提升，同时保持任务效用。

中文摘要：使用工具的LLM代理在轨迹层面而非仅最终响应上失败，因为它们可能执行不安全的工具调用、遵循注入指令、顺从有害请求，或对良性任务过度拒绝，尽管产生了看似安全的答案。现有的安全对齐信号大多是响应级或离策略的，并且常常导致安全-效用权衡：提高代理安全性会以降低任务性能为代价。这种稀疏且单目标的奖励严重限制了实际可用性。为弥补这一差距，我们提出了FATE，一个在策略的自演化框架，它将验证器评分的失败转化为修复监督，无需专家示范。对于每个失败，同一策略提出修复候选，然后由验证器重新评分，并在安全性、效用、过度拒绝控制和轨迹有效性方面进行过滤。这一密集的轨迹级信息随后被用作代理自演化的监督信号。在此过程中，我们进一步引入了帕累托前沿策略优化（PFPO），结合监督热身和帕累托感知策略优化以维护安全-效用权衡。在AgentDojo、AgentHarm和ATBench上的实验表明，FATE在不同模型和规模上提高了安全性，同时保留了有用行为。与强基线相比，FATE将攻击成功率降低了33.5%，有害顺从降低了82.6%，并将外部轨迹安全诊断提升了6.5%。这些结果表明，失败的轨迹可以为更安全的自演化代理提供结构化的修复监督。

Original abstract: Tool-using LLM agents fail through trajectories rather than only final responses, as they may execute unsafe tool calls, follow injected instructions, comply with harmful requests, or over-refuse benign tasks despite producing a seemingly safe answer. Existing safety-alignment signals are largely response-level or off-policy, and often incur a safety-utility trade-off: improving agent safety comes at the cost of degraded task performance. Such sparse and single-objective rewards severely limit real-world usability. To bridge this gap, we propose FATE, an on-policy self-evolving framework that transforms verifier-scored failures into repair supervision without expert demonstrations. For each failure, the same policy proposes repair candidates, which are then re-scored by verifiers and filtered across security, utility, over-refusal control, and trajectory validity. This dense trajectory-level information is then used as a supervision signal for agent self-evolution. During this process, we further introduce Pareto-Front Policy Optimization (PFPO), combining supervised warmup with Pareto-aware policy optimization to preserve safety-utility trade-offs. Experiments on AgentDojo, AgentHarm, and ATBench show that FATE improves safety across different models and scales while preserving useful behavior. Compared with strong baselines, FATE reduces attack success rate by 33.5%, harmful compliance by 82.6%, and improves external trajectory-safety diagnosis by 6.5%. These results suggest that failed trajectories can provide structured repair supervision for safer self-evolving agents.

</details>


### [51] [Rethinking Supervision Granularity: Segment-Level Learning for LLM-Based Theorem Proving](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11905v1)
*Shuo Xu,Jiakun Zhang,Junyu Lai,Chun Cao,Jingwei Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出段级监督用于LLM定理证明agent，证明搜索与代码优化agent共享推理需求，可启发训练策略

TL;DR: 提出段级监督方法，从证明轨迹中提取局部连贯段训练策略模型，在多个数据集上优于步级和整体基线，并提升现有步级证明器性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 步级监督提供密集局部信号但可能碎片化证明过程，整体监督保留全局结构但生成复杂，需要更合适的监督粒度来平衡局部和全局信息。

Method: 提出段级监督，从证明轨迹中提取局部连贯的证明段作为训练数据，并在推理时重用该策略触发短rollout；同时引入目标感知rollout。

Result: 在miniF2F上，段级监督模型分别达到64.84%、60.90%、66.31%的成功率，优于基线；目标感知rollout提升BFS-Prover-V2-7B从68.77%到70.74%，InternLM2.5-StepProver从59.59%到60.33%。

Conclusion: 适当的监督粒度能更好地对齐模型学习与证明结构和搜索，段级监督是一种有效的训练数据构建策略。

中文摘要：在Lean 4中使用大型语言模型进行自动定理证明通常通过两种范式实现：步级策略预测与树搜索，或整体证明生成。这两种范式代表了构建监督训练数据的两种相反粒度：前者提供密集的局部信号，但可能破坏连贯的证明过程；后者保留全局结构，但需要复杂的端到端生成。在本文中，我们重新审视监督粒度作为证明轨迹上的训练集构建问题，并提出段级监督——一种从证明轨迹中提取局部连贯证明段以训练策略模型的训练数据构建策略。我们在推理时重用相同的策略，为现有步级模型触发短rollout。在STP、LeanWorkbook和NuminaMath-LEAN上使用段级监督训练的策略模型在miniF2F上分别实现了64.84%、60.90%和66.31%的证明成功率，始终优于步级和整体证明基线。目标感知rollout进一步改进了现有步级证明器，同时降低了推理成本。它将BFS-Prover-V2-7B的证明成功率从68.77%提升至70.74%，将InternLM2.5-StepProver从59.59%提升至60.33%，表明适当的监督粒度能更好地使模型学习与证明结构和搜索对齐。代码和模型可在https://github.com/NJUDeepEngine/SEG-ATP获取。

Original abstract: Automated theorem proving with large language models in Lean 4 is commonly approached through either step-level tactic prediction with tree search or whole-proof generation. These two paradigms represent opposite granularities for constructing supervised training data: the former provides dense local signals but may fragment coherent proof processes, while the latter preserves global structure but requires complex end-to-end generation. In this paper, we revisit supervision granularity as a training set construction problem over proof trajectories and propose segment-level supervision, a training data construction strategy that extracts locally coherent proof segments for training policy models. We further reuse the same strategy at inference time to trigger short rollouts for existing step-level models. When trained with segment-level supervision on STP, LeanWorkbook, and NuminaMath-LEAN, the resulting policy models achieve proof success rates of 64.84%, 60.90%, and 66.31% on miniF2F, respectively, consistently outperforming both step-level and whole-proof baselines. Goal-aware rollout further improves existing step-level provers while reducing inference costs. It increases the proof success rate of BFS-Prover-V2-7B from 68.77% to 70.74% and that of InternLM2.5-StepProver from 59.59% to 60.33%, showing that appropriate supervision granularity better aligns model learning with proof structure and search. Code and models are available at https://github.com/NJUDeepEngine/SEG-ATP.

</details>


### [52] [When Simulation Lies: A Sim-to-Real Benchmark and Domain-Randomized RL Recipe for Tool-Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11928v1)
*Xiaolin Zhou,Aojie Yuan,Zheng Luo,Zipeng Ling,Xixiao Pan,Yicheng Gao,Haiyue Zhang,Jiate Li,Shuli Jiang,Prince Zizhuang Wang,Zixuan Zhu,Jinbo Liu,Ryan A. Rossi,Hua Wei,Xiyang Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 工具使用agent的鲁棒性benchmark和域随机化RL训练方法，直接相关agent工具使用与鲁棒性。

TL;DR: 提出RobustBench-TC基准测试和ToolRL-DR域随机化强化学习方法，揭示了工具使用语言代理在部署噪声下鲁棒性不均匀，并通过训练显著提升鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际部署中工具使用语言代理面临输入噪声、工具注册表模糊和API不可靠等问题，而现有基准测试未考虑这些sim-to-real差距，导致代理性能大幅下降，亟需系统性的鲁棒性评估和训练方法。

Method: 构建了包含22种扰动类型的基准RobustBench-TC（按POMDP的观测、动作空间、奖励相关元数据和转换动力学分类），并提出ToolRL-DR域随机化强化学习框架，在扰动增强轨迹上训练工具使用代理。

Result: 在21个模型上，观测扰动影响小（<5%准确率下降），奖励和转换扰动影响大（约40%和30%下降）；ToolRL-DR-Full在3B骨干上保持约75%干净准确率，综合扰动准确率与14B开源基线相当，并弥合了27%的转换差距。

Conclusion: 域随机化RL能有效提升工具使用代理在部署噪声下的鲁棒性，且训练中未见过的扰动类型（如转换扰动）也能通过泛化的重试策略获得一定缓解，表明该方法具有迁移能力。

中文摘要：工具使用的语言代理在基准测试中被评估，这些基准测试假设干净的输入、明确的工具注册表和可靠的API。实际部署违反了所有这些假设：用户拼写错误会传播到幻觉工具名称，配置错误的请求超时可能导致代理无限期停滞，跨服务器的重复工具名称可能会冻结SDK。我们将这些失败研究为工具使用部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）中的模拟到现实差距，其中部署噪声通过观测、动作空间、奖励相关元数据或转换动态进入。我们引入了RobustBench-TC，一个包含22种扰动类型的基准测试，这些扰动按这四个POMDP组件组织，每个扰动都基于已验证的GitHub问题或记录在案的工具调用失败。在21个从1.5B到32B参数的模型（包括闭源的o4-mini）中，鲁棒性分布极不均匀：观测扰动使准确率下降不到5%，而奖励相关和转换扰动分别使准确率下降约40%和30%；仅靠规模不能弥合这些差距。然后我们提出了ToolRL-DR，一种域随机化强化学习（RL）方法，该方法在跨越三个静态可编码POMDP组件的扰动增强轨迹上训练工具使用代理。在3B骨干上，ToolRL-DR-Full保留了大约四分之三的干净准确率，并达到与开源14B函数调用基线相当的综合扰动准确率，同时显著缩小了与o4-mini的差距。它尽管在训练中从未见过转换扰动，却弥合了大约27%的转换差距，这表明在对抗性静态工具使用输入上进行RL会诱导一种更持久的重试策略，该策略可转移到未见过的运行时故障。数据集、代码和基准排行榜公开可用。

Original abstract: Tool-use language agents are evaluated on benchmarks that assume clean inputs, unambiguous tool registries, and reliable APIs. Real deployments violate all these assumptions: user typos propagate into hallucinated tool names, a misconfigured request timeout can stall an agent indefinitely, and duplicate tool names across servers can freeze an SDK. We study these failures as a sim-to-real gap in the tool-use partially observable Markov decision process (POMDP), where deployment noise enters through the observation, action space, reward-relevant metadata, or transition dynamics. We introduce RobustBench-TC, a benchmark with 22 perturbation types organized by these four POMDP components, each grounded in a verified GitHub issue or documented tool-calling failure. Across 21 models from 1.5B to 32B parameters (including the closed-source o4-mini), the robustness profile is sharply uneven: observation perturbations reduce accuracy by less than 5%, while reward-relevant and transition perturbations reduce accuracy by roughly 40% and 30%, respectively; scale alone does not close these gaps. We then propose ToolRL-DR, a domain-randomization reinforcement learning (RL) recipe that trains a tool-use agent on perturbation-augmented trajectories spanning the three statically encodable POMDP components. On a 3B backbone, ToolRL-DR-Full retains roughly three-quarters of clean accuracy and reaches an aggregate perturbed accuracy comparable to open-source 14B function-calling baselines while substantially narrowing the gap to o4-mini. It closes approximately 27% of the Transition gap despite never seeing transition perturbations in training, suggesting that RL on adversarial static tool-use inputs induces a more persistent retry policy that transfers to unseen runtime failures. The dataset, code and benchmark leaderboard are publicly available.

</details>


### [53] [Counterfactual Trace Auditing of LLM Agent Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11946v2)
*Xiaolin Zhou,Jinbo Liu,Li Li,Ryan A. Rossi,Xiyang Hu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出反事实追踪审计框架评估agent技能，直接测量agent行为变化，对agent评估方法有启发。

TL;DR: 提出反事实追踪审计（CTA）框架，用于评估技能对智能体行为的影响，实验表明CTA能揭示通过率无法捕捉的行为变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前技能评估方法有限，仅靠通过率无法反映技能的真实行为影响。

Method: 提出CTA框架，配对有/无技能追踪，分割对齐阶段，输出SIP标注。

Result: 在49个软件工程任务上应用CTA，发现通过率仅变化0.3%，但识别出522个SIP实例，揭示多种行为影响，并总结三个发现。

Conclusion: CTA将非正式失败模式转化为可重复行为测量，弥补了评估差距。

中文摘要：大语言模型智能体越来越多地配备智能体技能。当前对技能的评估方法仍然有限。大多数已部署的基准测试仅报告技能附加前后的通过率，将技能视为对智能体行为的黑箱改变。我们引入了反事实追踪审计（CTA），这是一个衡量技能如何改变智能体行为的框架。CTA将每个有技能的智能体追踪与同一任务上无技能的对应追踪配对，将两个追踪分割成目标导向的阶段，对齐这些阶段，并输出结构化的技能影响模式（SIP）标注。这些标注描述了技能的行为效果，而不仅仅是任务结果。我们在SWE-Skills-Bench上使用Claude对49个软件工程任务实例化了CTA。由此产生的审计揭示了一个明显的评估差距。通过率平均仅变化+0.3个百分点，表明总体影响很小。然而，CTA在相同的配对追踪中识别出522个SIP实例，表明即使在通过率几乎不变的情况下，技能也显著重塑了智能体行为。审计还分离了通过率无法检测到的几个重复出现的影响，包括字面模板复制、任务外工件创建、过度规划和任务恢复。得出了三个发现。首先，高基线任务包含了大多数观察到的技能影响，尽管它们的通过率已经饱和，因此无法反映这些影响。其次，中等基线性能的任务显示出最大的可恢复增益，但通常以显著更高的token成本为代价。第三，主导的SIP类型可以通过基线桶来识别：表面锚定在天花板任务中最常见，而边缘情况提示在中档和底层任务中最常见。这些规律将非正式的失败模式观察转化为可复现的行为测量。

Original abstract: Large Language Model agents are increasingly augmented with agent skills. Current evaluation methods for skills remain limited. Most deployed benchmarks report only pass rate before and after a skill is attached, treating the skill as a black box change to agent behavior. We introduce Counterfactual Trace Auditing (CTA), a framework for measuring how a skill changes agent behavior. CTA pairs each with skill agent trace with a without skill counterpart on the same task, segments both traces into goal directed phases, aligns the phases, and emits structured Skill Influence Pattern (SIP) annotations. These annotations describe the behavioral effect of a skill rather than only its task outcome. We instantiate CTA on SWE-Skills-Bench with Claude across 49 software engineering tasks. The resulting audit reveals a clear evaluation gap. Pass rate changes by only +0.3 percentage points on average, suggesting little aggregate effect. Yet CTA identifies 522 SIP instances across the same paired traces, showing that the skills substantially reshape agent behavior even when pass rate is nearly unchanged. The audit also separates several recurring effects that pass rate cannot detect, including literal template copying, off task artifact creation, excess planning, and task recovery. Three findings emerge. First, high baseline tasks contain most of the observed skill effects, although their pass rate is already saturated and therefore cannot reflect those effects. Second, tasks with moderate baseline performance show the most recoverable gain, but often at substantially higher token cost. Third, the dominant SIP type can be identified by baseline bucket: surface anchoring is most common on ceiling tasks and edge-case prompting is most common on mid-range and floor tasks. These regularities turn informal failure mode observations into reproducible behavioral measurements.

</details>


### [54] [SAGE: A Self-Evolving Agentic Graph-Memory Engine for Structure-Aware Associative Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12061v1)
*Juntong Wang,Haoyue Zhao,guanghui Pan,Xiyuan Wang,Yanbo Wang,Qiyan Deng,Muhan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出自进化图记忆引擎SAGE，用于长时记忆agent，属于agent记忆与自我改进方法。

TL;DR: SAGE是一个自演进图记忆引擎，通过记忆写入器和基于图基础模型的读取器之间的反馈循环，动态构建和优化图记忆，从而在多种长时记忆任务中提升证据恢复、答案依据和检索效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG和GraphRAG系统将记忆图视为静态检索中间件，限制了从部分线索恢复完整证据链、利用图结构角色以及通过下游反馈改进记忆的能力。

Method: SAGE包含两个角色：记忆写入器（从交互历史逐步构建结构化图记忆）和基于图基础模型的记忆读取器（执行检索并提供反馈），通过自演进机制迭代优化记忆。

Result: 在多跳QA、开放域检索等任务中，SAGE经两轮自演进后达到最佳平均排名；在NQ零样本开放域转移中Recall@2/5为82.5/91.6；在LongMemEval和HaluMem上，训练与读写反馈改善了长时记忆和幻觉诊断指标。

Conclusion: 自演进、结构感知的图记忆是实现鲁棒长时域语言智能体的有前景基础。

中文摘要：长时记忆正在成为语言智能体的核心瓶颈。现有的RAG和GraphRAG系统大多将记忆图视为静态检索中间件，这限制了它们从部分线索中恢复完整证据链、利用可复用的图结构角色以及通过下游反馈改进记忆本身的能力。我们提出了SAGE，一种自演进智能体图记忆引擎，它将图记忆建模为动态的长时记忆基质。SAGE耦合了两个角色：一个记忆写入器，它从交互历史中逐步构建结构化的图记忆；以及一个基于图基础模型的记忆读取器，用于执行检索并向记忆写入器提供反馈。我们提供了严格的理论分析来支持该框架。在多跳问答、开放域检索、领域特定评论问答以及长时智能体记忆基准测试中，SAGE改善了证据恢复、答案依据和检索效率：经过两轮自演进后，它在多跳问答上取得了最佳平均排名；在零样本开放域迁移中，它在NQ上达到了82.5/91.6的Recall@2/5。进一步的LongMemEval和HaluMem结果表明，训练和读写反馈改善了多项长时记忆和幻觉诊断指标，表明自演进、结构感知的图记忆是实现鲁棒的长时域语言智能体的有前景的基础。

Original abstract: Long-term memory is becoming a central bottleneck for language agents. Exsting RAG and GraphRAG systems largely treat memory graphs as static retrieval middleware, which limits their ability to recover complete evidence chains from partial cues, exploit reusable graph-structrual roles, and improve the memory itself through downstream feedback. We introduce SAGE, a Self-evolving Agentic Graph-memory Engine that models graph memory as a dynamic long-term memory substrate. SAGE couples two roles: a memory writer that incrementally constucts structured graph memory from interaction histories, and a Graph Foundation Model-based memory reader to perform retrieval and provide feedback to the memory writer. We provide rigorooous theoretical annalyses supporting the framework. Across multi-hop QA, open-domain retireval, domain-specific review QA, and long-term agent-memory benchmarks, SAGE improves evidence recovery, answer grounding, and retrieval efficiency: after two self-evolution rounds, it achieves the best average rank on multi-hop QA; in zero-shot open-domain transfer, it reaches 82.5/91.6 Recall@2/5 on NQ. Further results on LongMemEval and HaluMem show that traning and reader-writer feedback improve multiple long-term memory and hallucination-diagnostic metrics, suggesting that self-evolving, structure-aware graph memory is a promising foundation for robust long-horizon language agents.

</details>


### [55] [Operationalizing Document AI: A Microservice Architecture for OCR and LLM Pipelines in Production](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18818v1)
*Yao Fehlis,Benjamin Bengfort,Zhangzhang Si,Vahid Eyorokon,Prema Roman,Patrick Deziel,Devon Slonaker,Steve Veldman,Ben Johnson,Joyce Rigelo,Michael Wharton,Steve Kramer*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出微服务架构封装多种模型流水线，实现每小时处理数千份多页文档，发现OCR是延迟瓶颈，系统受GPU容量限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缩小文档理解模型定义与生产部署之间的差距。

Method: 微服务架构，混合分类，分离GPU/CPU，异步处理，水平扩展。

Result: 系统每小时处理数千份多页文档，OCR主导端到端延迟，系统在共享GPU推理容量决定的并发度下饱和。

Conclusion: 提供具体架构模式，帮助实践者构建生产级文档理解系统。

中文摘要：学术研究往往关注文档理解的新模型，导致文献中模型定义与生产规模运行之间的巨大差距。为缩小这一差距，我们提出了一种微服务架构，该架构封装了多个模型的流水线，包括分类、光学字符识别（OCR）和大语言模型结构化字段提取，并介绍了我们在每小时处理数千份多页文档的流水线上运行的经验。我们描述了我们的主要设计决策，包括混合分类、将GPU绑定的推理与CPU绑定的编排分离、使用异步处理处理流水线中许多IO绑定的操作，以及独立的水平扩展策略。通过批处理分析，我们发现了两个影响生产部署的令人惊讶的定性发现：OCR（而非语言模型解析）主导了端到端延迟，并且系统在由共享GPU推理容量（而非工作进程数）确定的并发度下饱和。我们的目标是为从业者提供具体的架构模式，以构建在基准之外也能正常工作的文档理解系统，有效地将模型应用于生产。

Original abstract: Academic research tends to focus on new models for document understanding creating a wide gap in the literature between model definition and running models at production scale. To close that gap, we present a microservice architecture that encapsulates pipelines of multiple models for classification, optical character recognition (OCR), and large language model structured field extraction as well as our experience running this pipeline on thousands of multi-page documents per hour. We describe our primary design decisions, including a hybrid classification, separation of GPU-bound inference from CPU-bound orchestration, use of asynchronous processing for the many IO-bound operations in the pipeline, and an independent, horizontal scaling strategy. Using batch profiling, we identified two surprising qualitative findings that shape production deployments: OCR, not language-model parsing, dominates end-to-end latency, and the system saturates at a concurrency determined by shared GPU-inference capacity rather than worker count. Our goal is to provide practitioners with concrete architectural patterns for building document understanding systems that work beyond the benchmark; effectively operationalizing models in production.

### [56] [Intermediate Artifacts as First-Class Citizens: A Data Model for Durable Intermediate Artifacts in Agentic Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12087v1)
*Josh Rosen,Seth Rosen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent系统中中间工件的数据模型，对agent记忆与工作流管理有启发

TL;DR: 提出持久、可检查的中间工件数据模型，使AI工作更可检查、可修改和可维护。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI系统在多步骤任务中产生的中间工作是短暂的，最终产物是上游状态的损失性投影，导致工作难以检查、修改和维护。

Method: 提出系统级数据模型，定义中间工件的属性（类型化、结构化、可寻址、版本化、依赖感知、权威、可消费），并形式化添加和替代更新语义，以及工件谱系支持持久中间状态。

Result: 该数据模型使得中间工件可被区分、可版本化、可依赖追踪，并支持评估维护状态质量。

Conclusion: 持久中间工件不是让模型更聪明，而是使AI生成的工作更可检查、可修改和可维护。

中文摘要：许多AI系统围绕循环组织，其中模型进行推理、调用工具、观察结果并继续直到任务完成。这些系统通常产生最终产物，如备忘录、计划、建议和分析，而塑造这些输出的中间工作仍然短暂。对于多步骤、可修改的AI工作，最终产物通常是上游状态的损失性投影。我们认为，此类系统应保留持久、可检查的中间工件：类型化、结构化、可寻址、版本化、依赖感知、权威且可被下游计算使用。这些工件不是模型的私有思维链。它们是维护的工作产品，如证据图、声明结构、标准、假设、计划、转换规则、合成程序、未解决的紧张关系和部分产品，后续人类和代理可以检查、修改、替代和改进。贡献是一个系统级数据模型。我们将中间工件与聊天记录、记忆、隐藏思维链、叙述、思考和最终答案区分开来；形式化添加和替代更新语义，并明确当前状态解析；描述工件谱系如何支持跨修订的持久中间状态；并论证评估必须针对维护状态质量，而不仅仅是最终输出质量。主张并非工件使模型更智能，而是持久中间工件使AI生成的工作随时间推移更可检查、可修改和可维护。

Original abstract: Many AI systems are organized around loops in which models reason, call tools, observe results, and continue until a task is complete. These systems often produce final artifacts such as memos, plans, recommendations, and analyses, while the intermediate work that shaped those outputs remains ephemeral. For multi-step, revisable AI work, final artifacts are often lossy projections over upstream state.
  We argue that such systems should preserve durable, inspectable intermediate artifacts: typed, structured, addressable, versioned, dependency-aware, authoritative, and consumable by downstream computation. These artifacts are not the model's private chain-of-thought. They are maintained work products such as evidence maps, claim structures, criteria, assumptions, plans, transformation rules, synthesis procedures, unresolved tensions, and partial products that later humans and agents can inspect, revise, supersede, and improve.
  The contribution is a systems-level data model. We distinguish intermediate artifacts from chat transcripts, memory, hidden chain-of-thought, narration, thinking, and final answers; formalize additive and superseding update semantics with explicit current-state resolution; describe how artifact lineage supports durable intermediate state across revisions; and argue that evaluation must target maintained-state quality, not only final-output quality. The claim is not that artifacts make models smarter. It is that durable intermediate artifacts make AI-generated work more inspectable, revisable, and maintainable over time.

</details>


### [57] [Autonomy and Agency in Agentic AI: Architectural Tactics for Regulated Contexts](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12105v1)
*Damir Safin,Dian Balta*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent自治与agency维度及架构策略，可迁移至coding agent的安全控制设计

TL;DR: 提出一个二维设计空间（代理能力与自主性各分五级）及六种架构策略，以在受监管环境中进行合规感知的代理型AI设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法未能联合处理代理能力和自主性的耦合，导致缺乏对监督、行动后果和错误纠正的原则性推理基础。

Method: 引入二维设计空间（各分五级），提出六种架构策略（检查点、升级、多智能体委托、工具供应、工具围栏、写入暂存），并考察五个部署参数（模型能力、智能体架构、工具保真度、工作流瓶颈、评估）。

Result: 通过两个公共部门工作示例验证策略在现实合规约束下的应用，提供了共享词汇表。

Conclusion: 该框架使责任性、可审计性和可逆性成为显式设计考虑，而非事后改造的属性。

中文摘要：在受监管的环境中部署具有代理能力的人工智能需要对其两个设计维度进行原则性推理：代理能力（系统能做什么）和自主性（系统在无人参与的情况下能采取多少行动）。虽然这两个维度通常被单独处理，但它们是耦合的：在更高的自主性下，人类错误纠正的可获得性更低，因此可靠运行需要相应约束代理能力；合规性要求通过随着行动后果的增加而强制要求人类参与来强化这一点。然而，没有既定的方法能够同时处理这两个维度，这使得从业者缺乏对监督、行动后果和错误纠正进行原则性推理的基础。这项工作引入了一个二维设计空间，其中两个维度都被组织为五个操作级别，使耦合性变得明确且可导航。自主性范围从人类指挥的操作（L1）到完全自主的监控（L5）；代理能力范围从对提供的上下文进行推理（L1）到对权威记录进行提交写入（L5）。在此空间基础上，我们提出了六种架构策略——检查点、升级、多智能体委托、工具供应、工具围栏和写入暂存——用于调整部署在该空间中的位置。这些策略基于公共部门背景下的两个工作示例进行说明，展示了它们如何在现实合规约束下应用。我们进一步考察了五个部署参数——模型能力、智能体架构、工具保真度、工作流瓶颈和评估——这些参数独立于代理能力和自主性，决定了在任何配置下可实现的内容。总之，设计空间、策略和部署参数提供了一个共享词汇表，用于进行原则性、合规感知的代理型AI设计，其中责任性、可审计性和可逆性被明确作为设计考虑因素，而不是必须在部署后改造的属性。

Original abstract: Deploying agentic AI in regulated contexts requires principled reasoning about two design dimensions: agency (what the system can do) and autonomy (how much it acts without human involvement). Though often treated independently, they are coupled: at higher autonomy, human error correction is less available, so reliable operation requires constraining agency accordingly; compliance requirements reinforce this by mandating human involvement as action consequences grow. Yet no established approach addresses them jointly, leaving practitioners without a principled basis for reasoning about oversight, action consequences, and error correction.
  This work introduces a two-dimensional design space in which both dimensions are organised into five operational levels, making the coupling explicit and navigable. Autonomy ranges from human-commanded operation (L1) to fully autonomous monitoring (L5); agency ranges from reasoning over supplied context (L1) to committed writes to authoritative records (L5). Building on this space, we propose six architectural tactics--checkpoints, escalation, multi-agent delegation, tool provisioning, tool fencing, and write staging--for adjusting a deployment's position within it. The tactics are grounded in two worked examples from public-sector contexts, illustrating how they apply under realistic compliance constraints. We further examine five deployment parameters--model capability, agent architecture, tool fidelity, workflow bottlenecks, and evaluation--that shape what is achievable at any configuration independently of agency and autonomy. Together, the design space, tactics, and deployment parameters provide a shared vocabulary for principled, compliance-aware agentic AI design in which responsibility, auditability, and reversibility are explicit design considerations rather than properties that must be retrofitted after deployment.

</details>


### [58] [Rollout Cards: A Reproducibility Standard for Agent Research](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12131v1)
*Charlie Masters,Ziyuan Liu,Stefano V. Albrecht*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent研究可重复性标准rollout cards，直接适用于coding agent评测

TL;DR: 为解决智能体研究中的可重复性问题，论文引入回放卡来保存和报告完整的回放记录，并揭示了当前报告规则对分数的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能体研究中广泛存在的可重复性问题：论文通常只报告分数而不提供回放记录，导致相同行为在不同评估规则下可能得到不同分数，且许多开源仓库未报告运行失败、出错或跳过的情况，影响结果的可信度和比较的公平性。

Method: 通过对50个流行仓库进行结构化审计，记录了37种报告规则导致分数变化的情况，并提出了回放卡（Rollout Cards）——一种包含完整回放记录、声明视图和报告规则的数据包。在工具安全、多智能体等四个领域验证了其有效性，并通过重新评分展示了报告规则对分数和排名的影响。

Result: 仅改变报告规则可使报告分数变化高达20.9个绝对百分点，甚至反转模型排名。所有审计的仓库均未报告失败或错误运行。回放卡支持重新分析和多角度评估。

Conclusion: 回放卡能够有效提升智能体研究的可重复性和透明度，建议研究者采用回放卡报告方式，并公开了集成到Ergon的参考实现以供社区使用。

中文摘要：长期影响机器学习和强化学习的可重复性问题现在开始出现在智能体研究中：论文通过报告分数比较系统，而留下这些分数背后的回放记录难以检查。对于智能体任务，这一点很重要，因为当评估选择回放的不同部分或应用不同的报告规则时，相同的行为可能获得不同的报告分数。在对50个流行的训练和评估仓库进行结构化审计时，我们发现没有任何一个仓库在报告主要分数的同时报告有多少次运行失败、出错或被跳过。我们还记录了37种情况，其中报告规则可能会改变任务成功率、成本/令牌计数或固定证据的时间测量，有时甚至剧烈改变。我们将回放记录（而非报告分数）视为智能体研究可重复性的单位。我们引入了回放卡：一种出版物包，它保存回放记录，并声明报告分数背后的视图、报告规则和丢弃清单。我们在两个设置中验证了回放卡。首先，在工具安全、多智能体系统、定理证明和搜索方面的四个部分公开发布让我们能够计算其原始报告未包含的分析。其次，对保留的基准输出进行重新评分涉及短回答、代码生成和工具使用任务，结果表明仅改变报告规则就可以使报告分数改变20.9个绝对百分点，并且在某些情况下会颠覆前沿模型的排名。我们发布了一个参考实现，集成到Ergon（一个开源强化学习环境）中，并公开发布了由Ergon生成的回放卡导出，涵盖工具使用、软件工程、网页交互、多智能体协调、安全性和搜索等基准测试，以支持未来的研究。

Original abstract: Reproducibility problems that have long affected machine learning and reinforcement learning are now surfacing in agent research: papers compare systems by reported scores while leaving the rollout records behind those scores difficult to inspect. For agentic tasks, this matters because the same behaviour can receive different reported scores when evaluations select different parts of a rollout or apply different reporting rules. In a structured audit of 50 popular training and evaluation repositories, we find that none report how many runs failed, errored, or were skipped alongside headline scores. We also document 37 cases where reporting rules can change task-success rates, cost/token accounting, or timing measurements for fixed evidence, sometimes dramatically. We treat rollout records, not reported scores, as the unit of reproducibility for agent research. We introduce rollout cards: publication bundles that preserve the rollout record and declare the views, reporting rules, and drops manifests behind reported scores. We validate rollout cards in two settings. First, four partial public releases in tool safety, multi-agent systems, theorem proving, and search let us compute analyses their original reports did not include. Second, re-grading preserved benchmark outputs across short-answer, code-generation, and tool-use tasks shows that changing only the reporting rule can change reported scores by 20.9 absolute percentage points and, in some cases, invert rankings of frontier models. We release a reference implementation integrated into Ergon, an open-source reinforcement learning gym, and publicly publish Ergon-produced rollout-card exports for benchmarks spanning tool use, software engineering, web interaction, multi-agent coordination, safety, and search to support future research.

</details>


### [59] [ALGOGEN: Tool-Generated Verifiable Traces for Reliable Algorithm Visualization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12159v1)
*Kunpeng Liao,Yuexiao Ma,Yisheng Lin,Hualin Zeng,Xiawu Zheng,Rongrong Ji*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出解耦LLM执行与渲染的agent范式，生成可验证轨迹，对一般agent设计有启发

TL;DR: ALGOGEN通过将算法执行与渲染解耦，利用VTA和RSL生成可靠的算法可视化视频，在LeetCode基准上成功率达99.8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端LLM系统（如CODE2VIDEO）在生成AV视频时需同时模拟算法流程和满足渲染约束，导致LLM产生幻觉，出现执行失败、元素重叠和帧间不一致等问题。

Method: 提出ALGOGEN范式，引入可视化轨迹代数（VTA）和渲染风格语言（RSL），LLM生成Python跟踪器输出VTA-JSON轨迹，再由确定性渲染器编译为不同目标输出（Manim、LaTeX/TikZ、Three.js）。

Result: 在200个LeetCode任务上，ALGOGEN的平均成功率为99.8%，比端到端方法（82.5%）提升17.3%。

Conclusion: 解耦算法执行与渲染可有效减少LLM在复杂AV任务中的幻觉，提供更可靠的算法可视化自动生成方案。

中文摘要：算法可视化（AV）通过动画化算法执行状态帮助学生建立心智模型。最近基于LLM的系统（如CODE2VIDEO）以端到端方式生成AV视频。然而，这种范式要求系统同时模拟算法流程并满足视频渲染约束（如元素布局和配色方案）。这一复杂任务导致LLM产生幻觉，造成执行成功率降低、元素重叠以及帧间不一致。为解决这些挑战，我们提出ALGOGEN，一种将算法执行与渲染解耦的新范式。首先引入可视化轨迹代数（VTA），这是一个关于算法视觉状态和操作的幺半群。然后LLM生成一个Python跟踪器，模拟算法流程并输出VTA-JSON轨迹（VTA的JSON编码）。对于渲染，我们定义渲染风格语言（RSL）来模板化算法布局。确定性渲染器将算法轨迹与RSL编译为Manim、LaTeX/TikZ或Three.js输出。在包含200个任务的LeetCode AV基准测试上评估，ALGOGEN相比端到端方法的平均成功率提高了17.3%，达到99.8%对82.5%。这些结果表明，我们的解耦范式有效缓解了复杂AV任务中LLM的幻觉，为自动生成高质量算法可视化提供了更可靠的解决方案。演示视频和代码可在项目仓库中找到。

Original abstract: Algorithm Visualization (AV) helps students build mental models by animating algorithm execution states. Recent LLM-based systems such as CODE2VIDEO generate AV videos in an end-to-end manner. However, this paradigm requires the system to simultaneously simulate algorithm flow and satisfy video rendering constraints, such as element layout and color schemes. This complex task induces LLM hallucinations, resulting in reduced execution success rates, element overlap, and inter-frame inconsistencies.
  To address these challenges, we propose ALGOGEN, a novel paradigm that decouples algorithm execution from rendering. We first introduce Visualization Trace Algebra (VTA), a monoid over algorithm visual states and operations. The LLM then generates a Python tracker that simulates algorithm flow and outputs VTA-JSON traces, a JSON encoding of VTA. For rendering, we define a Rendering Style Language (RSL) to templatize algorithm layouts. A deterministic renderer then compiles algorithm traces with RSL into Manim, LaTeX/TikZ, or Three.js outputs.
  Evaluated on a LeetCode AV benchmark of 200 tasks, ALGOGEN achieves an average success rate improvement of 17.3% compared to end-to-end methods, with 99.8% versus 82.5%. These results demonstrate that our decoupling paradigm effectively mitigates LLM hallucinations in complex AV tasks, providing a more reliable solution for automated generation of high-quality algorithm visualizations. Demo videos and code are available in the project repository.

</details>


### [60] [Do Enterprise Systems Need Learned World Models? The Importance of Context to Infer Dynamics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12178v1)
*Jishnu Sethumadhavan Nair,Patrice Bechard,Rishabh Maheshwary,Surajit Dasgupta,Sravan Ramachandran,Aakash Bhagat,Shruthan Radhakrishna,Pulkit Pattnaik,Johan Obando-Ceron,Shiva Krishna Reddy Malay,Sagar Davasam,Seganrasan Subramanian,Vipul Mittal,Sridhar Krishna Nemala,Christopher Pal,Srinivas Sunkara,Sai Rajeswar*

TL;DR: 提出企业发现代理，通过运行时读取配置来发现转换动态，比仅靠离线训练的世界模型在部署偏移下更鲁棒。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出企业发现代理，在运行时通过读取系统配置来恢复相关转换动态；并引入CascadeBench基准测试用于评估。

Result: 离线训练的世界模型在分布内表现良好，但在动态变化时性能下降；而基于发现的代理在部署偏移下更鲁棒。

Conclusion: 在可配置的企业环境中，智能体不应仅依赖固定的内化动态，而应结合运行时发现相关转换逻辑的机制。

中文摘要：世界模型使智能体能够通过内化环境动态来预判其行动的影响。然而，在企业系统中，这些动态通常由特定于租户的业务逻辑定义，这些逻辑在不同部署间变化并随时间演化，导致基于历史转换训练的模型在部署偏移下变得脆弱。我们提出了一个世界模型文献尚未解决的问题：当规则可以在推理时读取时，智能体是否仍然需要学习它们？我们论证并通过实验证明，在转换动态可配置且可读取的环境中，运行时发现通过将预测建立在活动系统实例上，补充了离线训练。我们提出了企业发现代理，它通过在运行时读取系统配置而不是仅依赖内化表示来恢复相关的转换动态。我们引入了CascadeBench，一个面向推理的企业级级联预测基准，采用了World of Workflows在多样化合成环境上的评估方法，并结合部署偏移评估表明，离线训练的世界模型在分布内表现良好，但随着动态变化而退化，而基于发现的代理通过在当前实例中建立预测基础，在偏移下更加鲁棒。我们的发现表明，在可配置的企业环境中，智能体不应仅依赖固定的内化动态，而应结合在运行时发现相关转换逻辑的机制。

Original abstract: World models enable agents to anticipate the effects of their actions by internalizing environment dynamics. In enterprise systems, however, these dynamics are often defined by tenant-specific business logic that varies across deployments and evolves over time, making models trained on historical transitions brittle under deployment shift. We ask a question the world-models literature has not addressed: when the rules can be read at inference time, does an agent still need to learn them? We argue, and demonstrate empirically, that in settings where transition dynamics are configurable and readable, runtime discovery complements offline training by grounding predictions in the active system instance. We propose enterprise discovery agents, which recover relevant transition dynamics at runtime by reading the system's configuration rather than relying solely on internalized representations. We introduce CascadeBench, a reasoning-focused benchmark for enterprise cascade prediction that adopts the evaluation methodology of World of Workflows on diverse synthetic environments, and use it together with deployment-shift evaluation to show that offline-trained world models can perform well in-distribution but degrade as dynamics change, whereas discovery-based agents are more robust under shift by grounding their predictions in the current instance. Our findings suggest that, in configurable enterprise environments, agents should not rely solely on fixed internalized dynamics, but should incorporate mechanisms for discovering relevant transition logic at runtime.

### [61] [CAX-Agent: A Lightweight Agent Harness for Reliable APDL Automation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15218v1)
*Chenying Lin,Yichen Hai,Yi He,Ran Wang,Haiyan Qiang,Liang Yu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出轻量级agent harness架构用于APDL自动化，包含结构化执行控制、工具封装和故障恢复策略，可迁移至coding agent设计。

TL;DR: CAX-Agent通过在LLM和求解器之间插入编排中间件（含恢复阶梯）提升MAPDL仿真可靠性，实验表明模型驱动恢复策略显著优于无恢复或仅规则恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型直接用于MAPDL仿真时缺乏结构化控制和故障恢复，导致输出不一致和任务失败，需要一种可靠的自动化框架。

Method: 提出CAX-Agent三层架构（LLM服务、代理工具包、求解器后端），设计了恢复阶梯并实验对比三种恢复策略（无恢复、仅规则、仅模型）在50个基准上的表现。

Result: 模型驱动恢复策略（model_only）在完成率（0.9267）、任务得分（3.59/4）、总分（9.16/10）和零干预率（0.84）上均最优，效果显著优于其他策略（Cliff's delta=0.81-0.87）。

Conclusion: CAX-Agent的模型驱动恢复能有效提升任务可靠性和自动化程度，但当前验证基于简单几何，需在更复杂场景中进一步验证。

中文摘要：部署用于MAPDL有限元仿真的大型语言模型面临实际可靠性挑战：如果没有结构化的执行控制、工具封装和故障恢复，输出可能不一致且任务失败很常见。Agent Harness范式通过插入特定领域的编排中间件来解决这一问题，该中间件管理工具生命周期、工作流状态和恢复升级。本文介绍了CAX-Agent的架构，这是一个专为MAPDL自动化设计的轻量级代理工具包，并实证评估了其核心组件之一——恢复策略。CAX-Agent将执行组织为三个层次——LLM服务、代理工具包和求解器后端——并配备一个恢复阶梯，从确定性规则修补，经模型驱动的重新生成，到上下文丰富化和人工干预。我们在50个标准结构基准上评估了三种恢复策略（no_recovery、rule_only和model_only），每种策略重复运行三次（共450个案例运行）。两名独立人工评分者在盲测条件下对任务完成度进行评分；评分者间一致性较强（二次加权Cohen's kappa = 0.84，96%的评分对相差不超过1分）。Model_only实现了最高的完成率（0.9267）、任务得分（3.59/4）、总分（9.16/10）和零干预率（0.84），优于rule_only（0.7733、3.17/4、7.03/10、0.00）和no_recovery（0.6933、2.74/4、5.60/10、0.00），效应量较大（Cliff's delta = 0.81-0.87）。该基准使用故意简化的几何形状来隔离恢复策略的影响；我们讨论了这些发现的范围以及更广泛验证的方向。

Original abstract: Large language models deployed for MAPDL finite-element simulation face practical reliability challenges: without structured execution control, tool encapsulation, and fault recovery, outputs may be inconsistent and task failures are common. The Agent Harness paradigm addresses this by inserting domain-specific orchestration middleware that manages tool lifecycles, workflow state, and recovery escalation. This paper presents the architecture of CAX-Agent, a lightweight agent harness purpose-built for MAPDL automation, and empirically evaluates one of its core components -- the recovery policy.CAX-Agent organizes execution into three layers -- LLM service, agent harness, and solver backend -- with a recovery ladder that escalates from deterministic rule patching through model-driven regeneration to context enrichment and human intervention. We evaluate three recovery strategies (no_recovery, rule_only, and model_only) on 50 standard structural benchmarks with three repeated runs per strategy (450 case-runs total). Two independent human raters score task completion under blind conditions; inter-rater agreement is strong (quadratic weighted Cohen's kappa = 0.84, 96 percent of score pairs within one point). Model_only achieves the best completion rate (0.9267), task score (3.59/4), total score (9.16/10), and zero-intervention rate (0.84), outperforming rule_only (0.7733, 3.17/4, 7.03/10, 0.00) and no_recovery (0.6933, 2.74/4, 5.60/10, 0.00) with large effect sizes (Cliff's delta = 0.81-0.87). The benchmark uses deliberately simple geometries to isolate recovery-policy effects; we discuss the scope of these findings and directions for broader validation.
