### [89] [Deep Reasoning in General Purpose Agents via Structured Meta-Cognition](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11388v1)
*Dean Light,Michael Theologitis,Kshitish Ghate,Shuyue Stella Li,Benjamin Newman,Chirag Shah,Aylin Caliskan,Pang Wei Koh,Dan Suciu,Yulia Tsvetkov*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 通用agent深度推理方法，结构化元认知构建任务scaffold，直接相关且高效。

TL;DR: 提出深度推理方法，通过结构化元推理构建任务特定脚手架，智能体DOLORES在多个基准上显著优于现有脚手架方法，8B模型甚至超越32B模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体的脚手架硬编码推理决策，缺乏灵活适应任务结构变化的能力。

Method: 引入深度推理，使用形式语言表示元推理为可执行分解，通过上下文示例指导推理时脚手架构建，并实例化为DOLORES智能体。

Result: DOLORES在四个硬性基准上平均比最强基线提高24.8%，8B版本超越同族32B模型。

Conclusion: 未来智能体系统应将脚手架视为自适应推理，根据任务需求即时构建结构。

中文摘要：人类通过在不同推理模式之间灵活切换来直观地解决复杂问题：他们规划、执行、修改中间目标、通过关联判断解决歧义，并对明确指定的子问题应用形式化程序。当前的LLM智能体缺乏这种灵活性，因为其脚手架预先硬编码了此类推理决策。这些脚手架在预设结构与任务匹配时有效，但在解决需要调整推理结构本身的任务时则显得脆弱。我们引入了深度推理（Deep Reasoning）——一种通过结构化元推理在推理时构建任务特定脚手架的推理方法。深度推理使用一种形式语言，将元推理表示为关联推理、形式计算和递归子问题求解上的可执行分解，使得分解原则能被编码为上下文示例，指导测试时的脚手架构建。我们将此方法实例化到一个通用智能体（DOLORES）中，该智能体将复杂任务分配到更受控制的推理线程中。我们在四个硬性基准（多跳推理、长链问答、长上下文聚合和深度研究式信息搜索）上评估了它的性能，并与最先进的脚手架方法进行了比较。DOLORES在三个模型大小和两个模型家族中优于所有评估的脚手架，平均比最强的评估脚手架基线提高24.8%。DOLORES将认知分布到结构化、低负载的推理线程中，从而减少了过早终止和幻觉。这一优势甚至可以弥合规模差距，8B版本在超过一半的设置中超越了同一家族的所有评估的32B基线。这些结果表明，未来的智能体系统应将脚手架视为自适应推理，即用即构每个任务所需的结构。

Original abstract: Humans intuitively solve complex problems by flexibly shifting among reasoning modes: they plan, execute, revise intermediate goals, resolve ambiguity through associative judgment, and apply formal procedures to well-specified subproblems. Current LLM agents lack this flexibility, as their scaffolds hard-code such reasoning decisions in advance. These scaffolds are effective when their prescribed structure matches the task, but brittle when solving the task requires adapting the structure of reasoning itself. We introduce Deep Reasoning -- an inference-time approach for constructing task-specific scaffolds through structured meta-reasoning. Deep Reasoning uses a formal language that represents meta-reasoning as executable decompositions over associative inference, formal computation, and recursive subproblem solving, enabling decomposition principles to be encoded as in-context examples that guide test-time scaffold construction. We instantiate this approach in a general-purpose agent (DOLORES) that distributes complex tasks across more controlled reasoning threads. We evaluate it against state-of-the-art scaffolding methods across four hard benchmarks: multi-hop reasoning, long-chain question answering, long-context aggregation, and deep research-style information seeking. DOLORES outperforms all evaluated scaffolds across three model sizes and two model families, improving over the strongest evaluated scaffold baseline by 24.8% on average. DOLORES distributes cognition across structured, lower-load reasoning threads, thereby reducing premature termination and hallucinations. This advantage can even bridge the scaling gap, with an 8B version surpassing all evaluated 32B baselines from the same family in more than half the settings. These results point toward future agentic systems that treat scaffolding as adaptive reasoning, constructing the structure each task requires just-in-time.

</details>


### [90] [Agent-BRACE: Decoupling Beliefs from Actions in Long-Horizon Tasks via Verbalized State Uncertainty](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11436v1)
*Joykirat Singh,Zaid Khan,Archiki Prasad,Justin Chih-Yao Chen,Akshay Nambi,Hyunji Lee,Elias Stengel-Eskin,Mohit Bansal*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出信念状态表示解耦agent行为，适用于长程部分可观测任务，可迁移

TL;DR: Agent-BRACE通过将LLM智能体解耦为信念状态模型和策略模型，并利用结构化近似信念（原子声明+置信度标签）进行决策，在长时部分可观测任务中显著提升性能并保持恒定上下文窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在部分可观测长时任务中面临两个挑战：维护对未观测状态的不确定性以及历史上下文无限增长。现有方法缺乏对信念状态的有效表示，因此需要一种紧凑且结构化的信念表示方法来支持决策。

Method: 将LLM智能体解耦为信念状态模型和策略模型，通过强化学习联合优化。信念状态模型生成一组原子自然语言声明，每个声明带有序数的言语化确定性标签（从确定到未知），形成结构化近似信念。策略模型基于该近似信念（而非完整历史）选择动作。

Result: 在长期部分可观测的具身语言环境中，Agent-BRACE在Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct上平均绝对提升14.5%，在Qwen3-4B-Instruct上提升5.3%，优于强RL基线，且上下文窗口大小与情节长度无关。

Conclusion: Agent-BRACE通过结构化信念表示有效解决了部分可观测性和历史增长问题，提升了LLM智能体在长时任务中的性能，且信念校准度随证据积累而提高。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被部署在部分可观测环境中的长时任务上，在这些任务中，模型必须在多个步骤中推断并跟踪复杂的环境状态，同时采取行动。这带来了两个挑战：部分可观测性要求对未观测到的世界属性保持不确定性，而长期的交互历史会导致上下文无限增长，稀释任务相关信息。这两个挑战的一个原则性解决方案是信念状态：给定过去观测和行动的环境状态后验分布，它能紧凑地编码历史信息以进行决策，无论情节长度如何。然而，在LLM智能体中，文本的开放性质使得如何表示这样的分布变得不明确。因此，我们引入了Agent-BRACE：通过抽象和置信度估计的智能体信念状态表示，一种将LLM智能体解耦为信念状态模型和策略模型的方法，并通过强化学习联合优化。信念状态模型产生信念分布的结构化近似：一组关于环境的原子自然语言声明，每个声明都带有一个有序的言语化确定性标签，范围从确定到未知。策略模型基于这种紧凑、结构化的近似信念（而非完整历史）进行条件化，学习在显式不确定性下选择行动。在长期、部分可观测的具身语言环境中，Agent-BRACE实现了平均绝对提升14.5%（Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct）和5.3%（Qwen3-4B-Instruct），优于强大的强化学习基线，同时保持与情节长度无关的近乎恒定的上下文窗口。进一步分析表明，随着证据的积累，学到的信念在情节过程中变得越来越校准。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed on long-horizon tasks in partially observable environments, where they must act while inferring and tracking a complex environment state over many steps. This leads to two challenges: partial observability requires maintaining uncertainty over unobserved world attributes, and long interaction history causes context to grow without bound, diluting task-relevant information. A principled solution to both challenges is a belief state: a posterior distribution over environment states given past observations and actions, which compactly encodes history for decision making regardless of episode length. In LLM agents, however, the open-ended nature of text makes it unclear how to represent such a distribution. Therefore, we introduce Agent-BRACE: Agent Belief state Representation via Abstraction and Confidence Estimation, a method that decouples an LLM agent into a belief state model and a policy model, jointly optimized via reinforcement learning. The belief state model produces a structured approximation of the belief distribution: a set of atomic natural language claims about the environment, each annotated with an ordinal verbalized certainty label ranging from certain to unknown. The policy model conditions on this compact, structured approximate belief rather than the full history, learning to select actions under explicit uncertainty. Across long-horizon, partially observable embodied language environments, Agent-BRACE achieves an average absolute improvement of +14.5% (Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct) and +5.3% (Qwen3-4B-Instruct), outperforming strong RL baselines while maintaining a near-constant context window independent of episode length. Further analysis shows that the learned belief becomes increasingly calibrated over the course of an episode as evidence accumulates.

</details>


### [91] [Three Regimes of Context-Parametric Conflict: A Predictive Framework and Empirical Validation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11574v1)
*Pruthvinath Jeripity Venkata*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出LLM处理上下文与参数化记忆冲突的三机制框架，对agent设计中的记忆与上下文权衡有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出三机制框架解释大模型在训练知识与文档冲突时的行为差异，并通过实验验证了参数确定性和任务框架的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决现有文献中大模型在处理训练知识与矛盾文档时行为不一致的实证矛盾。

Method: 提出三机制框架（单源更新、竞争整合、任务适当选择），区分参数强度和唯一性，并在5个模型上通过9,970次API调用进行三个实验阶段的验证。

Result: GEE逻辑回归确认了所有模型的机制2确定性梯度（beta=-0.38~-0.50, p≤.013），机制3消融实验显示任务框架将上下文遵循率从近100%翻转为6-71%。

Conclusion: 三机制框架能统一解释大模型在知识冲突情境下的行为，参数确定性和任务知识需求是关键预测因子。

中文摘要：关于大型语言模型如何处理其训练知识与矛盾文档之间冲突的文献中存在一个持久的实证矛盾：一些研究发现模型固执地保留其训练得到的答案，几乎有一半时间忽略提供的文档，而其他研究发现模型很容易遵从文档，大约96%的情况下遵循上下文。我们认为一旦认识到先前的实验研究了三种性质不同的处理情境而未加以区分，这些矛盾就会消散。我们提出了一个三机制框架：机制1（单源更新，主导预测因子：证据连贯性），机制2（竞争整合，主导预测因子：参数确定性），机制3（任务适当选择，主导预测因子：任务知识需求）。我们形式化了参数强度（暴露频率）和参数唯一性（编码一致性）之间的区别，并实证表明这些是正交维度（r = -0.002, p = .97），其中强度是稳定事实领域中的操作性预测因子。我们通过在三个实验阶段中使用9,970次API调用，在Claude Sonnet 4.6、GPT-5.5、Gemini 2.5 Flash、Llama 4 Maverick和DeepSeek V3上验证了该框架。GEE逻辑回归确认了所有五个模型预测的机制2确定性梯度（beta = -0.38到-0.50，所有p <= .013，BH-FDR校正）。机制3的消融实验表明，仅任务框架就将上下文遵循从近100%（上下文知识条件）翻转至6-71%（参数知识条件），所有五个模型均显著（p < .001）。确定性梯度对多项结果建模、对冲反应的敏感性分析和FDR校正是稳健的。

Original abstract: The literature on how large language models handle conflict between their training knowledge and a contradicting document presents a persistent empirical contradiction: some studies find models stubbornly retain their trained answers, ignoring provided documents nearly half the time, while others find models readily defer to the document, following context approximately 96% of the time. We argue these contradictions dissolve once one recognises that prior experiments have studied three qualitatively distinct processing situations without distinguishing them. We propose a three-regime framework: Regime 1 (single-source updating, dominant predictor: evidence coherence), Regime 2 (competitive integration, dominant predictor: parametric certainty), and Regime 3 (task-appropriate selection, dominant predictor: task knowledge requirement). We formalise a distinction between parametric strength (exposure frequency) and parametric uniqueness (encoding consistency), showing empirically that these are orthogonal dimensions (r = -0.002, p = .97) with strength as the operative predictor in stable factual domains. We validate the framework across Claude Sonnet 4.6, GPT-5.5, Gemini 2.5 Flash, Llama 4 Maverick, and DeepSeek V3 using 9,970 API calls in three experimental phases. GEE logistic regression confirms the predicted Regime 2 certainty gradient for all five models (beta = -0.38 to -0.50, all p <= .013, BH-FDR corrected). A Regime 3 ablation shows task framing alone flips context-following from near-100% (contextual knowledge condition) to 6-71% (parametric knowledge condition), with all five models significant (p < .001). The certainty gradient is robust to multinomial outcome modeling, sensitivity analyses for hedging responses, and FDR correction.

</details>


### [92] [Scalable Token-Level Hallucination Detection in Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12384v1)
*Rui Min,Tianyu Pang,Chao Du,Minhao Cheng,Yi R. Fung*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: token级幻觉检测，可用于提升agent输出可靠性。

TL;DR: 提出TokenHD，一种训练令牌级幻觉检测器的整体流程，通过可扩展数据引擎和重要性加权训练，使小型检测器（0.6B）超越大型推理模型（QwQ-32B），并具有良好的跨领域泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有步骤级幻觉检测方法依赖步骤分割，导致粒度有限和可扩展性差，难以有效检测推理密集型任务中的微妙幻觉。

Method: TokenHD包含一个可扩展的数据引擎，用于大规模合成幻觉注释；一个基于重要性加权的训练策略；以及一个严格的评估协议。检测器直接对自由文本操作，无需步骤划分。

Result: 小型检测器（0.6B）训练后显著超越大型推理模型（QwQ-32B），检测性能随模型规模（0.6B至8B）一致提升，且跨领域泛化良好。

Conclusion: TokenHD可有效训练令牌级幻觉检测器，性能优异且泛化能力强，为进一步增强跨域泛化提供了策略探索。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）展现了卓越的能力，但仍然频繁产生幻觉。这些幻觉在推理密集型任务中难以检测，因为内容看似连贯但包含逻辑缺陷和不可靠的中间结果等错误。虽然步骤级分析常用于检测内部幻觉，但由于依赖步骤分割，其粒度有限且可扩展性差。为了解决这些限制，我们提出了TokenHD，一个用于训练令牌级幻觉检测器的整体流程。具体来说，TokenHD包括一个可扩展的数据引擎，用于合成大规模幻觉注释，以及一个包含重要性加权策略的训练方案，以实现稳健的模型训练。为了系统地评估检测性能，我们还提供了一个严格的评估协议。通过TokenHD内的训练，我们的检测器直接对自由文本进行操作来识别幻觉，无需预定义的步骤分割或额外的文本重格式化。我们的实验表明，即使是一个小型检测器（0.6B）在训练后也能取得显著的性能提升，超过更大的推理模型（例如QwQ-32B），并且检测性能在0.6B到8B的模型规模上持续扩展。最后，我们展示了我们的检测器能够在各种实际场景中很好地泛化，并探索了进一步增强其跨领域泛化能力的策略。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities, but they still frequently produce hallucinations. These hallucinations are difficult to detect in reasoning-intensive tasks, where the content appears coherent but contains errors like logical flaws and unreliable intermediate results. While step-level analysis is commonly used to detect internal hallucinations, it suffers from limited granularity and poor scalability due to its reliance on step segmentation. To address these limitations, we propose TokenHD, a holistic pipeline for training token-level hallucination detectors. Specifically, TokenHD consists of a scalable data engine for synthesizing large-scale hallucination annotations along with a training recipe featuring an importance-weighted strategy for robust model training. To systematically assess the detection performance, we also provide a rigorous evaluation protocol. Through training within TokenHD, our detector operates directly on free-form text to identify hallucinations, eliminating the need for predefined step segmentation or additional text reformatting. Our experiments show that even a small detector (0.6B) achieves substantial performance gains after training, surpassing much larger reasoning models (e.g., QwQ-32B), and detection performance scales consistently with model size from 0.6B to 8B. Finally, we show that our detector can generalize well across diverse practical scenarios and explore strategies to further enhance its cross-domain generalization capability.

</details>


### [93] [Stories in Space: In-Context Learning Trajectories in Conceptual Belief Space](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12412v1)
*Eric Bigelow,Raphaël Sarfati,Daniel Wurgaft,Owen Lewis,Thomas McGrath,Jack Merullo,Atticus Geiger,Ekdeep Singh Lubana*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 探究LLM上下文学习中的信念空间轨迹，利于理解agent动态更新机制。

TL;DR: LLM的上下文学习可视为贝叶斯推理，其信念在低维几何空间中更新，通过故事理解实验验证了该空间的流形结构、行为与表征的一致性，以及通过干预因果控制信念轨迹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究将LLM的上下文学习视为贝叶斯推理，但潜在假设空间的结构未知。本文旨在探索该空间的结构及其与信念更新的关系。

Method: 结合行为分析和表征分析，利用故事理解任务进行动态信念更新实验，通过线性探针解码内部表征预测行为，并施加因果干预。

Result: 信念更新形成低维结构化流形上的轨迹；模型行为与内部表征一致反映该结构；干预表征能因果地改变信念轨迹。

Conclusion: LLM的信念动力学可用几何空间解释，为上下文学习的贝叶斯观点提供了结构化基础。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）通过上下文更新其行为，这可以被视为一种贝叶斯推理形式。然而，这种推理所依据的潜在假设空间的结构仍不清楚。在这项工作中，我们提出LLM在低维几何空间——一个概念信念空间——上分配信念，而上下文学习对应于信念随时间更新时在该空间中的轨迹。以故事理解为自然情境下的动态信念更新，我们结合行为分析和表征分析来研究这些轨迹。我们发现：（1）信念更新可以很好地描述为低维结构化流形上的轨迹；（2）这种结构在模型行为和内部表示中一致反映，并且可以通过简单的线性探针解码以预测行为；（3）对这些表示的干预因果地引导信念轨迹，其影响可以从概念空间的几何结构预测。总之，我们的结果提供了LLM中信念动力学的几何解释，将上下文学习的贝叶斯解释建立在结构化概念表示的基础上。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) update their behavior in context, which can be viewed as a form of Bayesian inference. However, the structure of the latent hypothesis space over which this inference operates remains unclear. In this work, we propose that LLMs assign beliefs over a low-dimensional geometric space - a conceptual belief space - and that in-context learning corresponds to a trajectory through this space as beliefs are updated over time. Using story understanding as a natural setting for dynamic belief updating, we combine behavioral and representational analyses to study these trajectories. We find that (1) belief updates are well-described as trajectories on low-dimensional, structured manifolds; (2) this structure is reflected consistently in both model behavior and internal representations and can be decoded with simple linear probes to predict behavior; and (3) interventions on these representations causally steer belief trajectories, with effects that can be predicted from the geometry of the conceptual space. Together, our results provide a geometric account of belief dynamics in LLMs, grounding Bayesian interpretations of in-context learning in structured conceptual representations.

</details>


### [94] [Simulating Students or Sycophantic Problem Solving? On Misconception Faithfulness of LLM Simulators](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12748v1)
*Heejin Do,Shashank Sonkar,Mrinmaya Sachan*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM模拟学生信念忠实度，对agent交互与反馈设计有启发

TL;DR: 提出误解忠实性评估框架和选择性翻转分数（SFS），发现当前LLM模拟学生普遍缺乏误解忠实性，通过后训练可有效提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模拟学生评估仅关注输出相似性，忽略交互中是否保持连贯误解，需评估误解忠实性。

Method: 提出误解对比反馈协议和选择性翻转分数（SFS），并在多个LLM上测试；开发后训练流程（SFT、偏好优化、带SFS奖励的RL）以提升误解忠实性。

Result: 当前LLM在SFS上接近零，表现出谄媚失败模式；后训练中SFT显著提升，SFS对齐RL改进更一致。

Conclusion: 误解忠实性是具挑战性但可训练的特性，应转向交互式信念感知的学生建模。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）能够流畅地生成类似学生的回答，使其成为训练和评估AI导师及人类教育者的有吸引力的模拟学生。然而，这类模拟器通常通过输出与真实学生的相似性来评估，而非通过它们在交互中是否像拥有连贯误解的学生那样表现。我们引入了一个受控框架来评估误解忠实性，即模拟器是否维持由误解驱动的信念状态，并在反馈针对根本误解时有选择性地更新。我们框架的核心是一个误解对比反馈协议，将针对性反馈与两个对照进行比较：错位反馈（针对另一个不同但合理的误解）和通用反馈（仅指出答案错误）。我们提出了选择性翻转分数（SFS），量化模拟器在针对性反馈下比在对照反馈下翻转答案的频率高出多少。在七个LLM（4B-120B）、多个数据集和提示策略中，模拟器表现出接近零的SFS，无论反馈相关性如何，都以同样高的概率纠正答案。进一步分析揭示了一种谄媚失败模式：模型的行为更像问题解决者，而非拥有误解的学生，它们将任何纠正信号视为放弃模拟信念并从内部知识重新求解的线索。为了解决这个问题，我们开发了一个后训练流程，包括监督微调（SFT）、偏好优化和基于SFS对齐奖励的强化学习（RL）；SFT取得了高达+0.56的显著提升，而SFS对齐的RL比偏好优化提供了更一致的改进。我们的结果确立了误解忠实性是一个具有挑战性但可训练的特性，激励从静态输出匹配转向交互式、信念感知的学生建模。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can fluently generate student-like responses, making them attractive as simulated students for training and evaluating AI tutors and human educators. Yet such simulators are typically evaluated by output similarity to real students, not by whether they behave like students with coherent misconceptions during interaction. We introduce a controlled framework for evaluating misconception faithfulness, whether a simulator maintains a misconception-driven belief state and updates selectively when feedback addresses the underlying misconception. Central to our framework is a misconception-contrastive feedback protocol that compares targeted feedback against two controls: misaligned feedback (targeting a different but plausible misconception) and generic feedback (only identifying answer is wrong). We propose Selective Flip Score (SFS), which quantifies how much more often a simulator flips its answer under targeted feedback than under contrastive controls. Across seven LLMs (4B-120B), multiple datasets, and prompting strategies, simulators exhibit near-zero SFS, correcting their answers at similarly high rates regardless of feedback relevance. Further analyses reveal a sycophantic failure mode: models behave less like students with misconceptions but more like problem-solvers who treat any corrective signal as a cue to abandon the simulated belief and re-solve from internal knowledge. To address this, we develop a post-training pipeline spanning supervised fine-tuning (SFT), preference optimization, and reinforcement learning (RL) with an SFS-aligned reward; SFT yields notable gains up to +0.56, and SFS-aligned RL provides more consistent improvements than preference optimization. Our results establish misconception faithfulness as a challenging yet trainable property, motivating a shift from static output matching toward interactive, belief-aware student modeling.

</details>


### [95] [TriVAL: A Tri-Validation Framework for Faithful Automatic Optimization Modeling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.23966v1)
*Ziyang Fang,JinXi Wang,Jinghui Zhong,Yew-Soon Ong*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 三阶段验证框架用于自动优化建模，含construct-validate-revise循环，对coding agent有启发

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种三重验证框架TriVAL，用于自动优化建模，通过分阶段验证和修正来减少错误累积，并在新基准NL4COP上证明了其优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动优化建模方法缺乏明确验证，导致错误累积降低准确性。

Method: 提出了TriVAL三重验证框架，在语义规范、数学公式和代码生成三个阶段执行构建-验证-修订循环，并引入更难的基准NL4COP。

Result: 在NL4COP和已有基准上，TriVAL一致优于现有方法，在最具挑战性问题上提升最大。

Conclusion: TriVAL通过分阶段验证和修正有效提升了自动优化建模的准确性，减少了错误传播。

中文摘要：优化建模充当了自然语言问题描述与优化求解器之间的关键桥梁，并且始终是将运筹学（OR）引入实际决策的基石。大语言模型（LLM）的最新进展推动了自动优化建模的重大进步。然而，现有方法在建模过程中仍然缺乏明确的验证，导致早期阶段引入的错误会沿流程传递，最终降低最终建模的准确性。为了应对这一挑战，我们提出了TriVAL，一个三重验证框架，它在自动优化建模的三个阶段执行明确的验证：语义规范、数学公式和代码生成。在每个阶段，TriVAL遵循构建-验证-修订循环，根据阶段特定标准评估当前结果，并在必要时进行修订。这种设计有助于在错误跨阶段积累之前识别并纠正它们，从而在整个建模过程中保持忠实性。为了在更具挑战性的组合问题上评估自动优化建模，我们进一步引入了NL4COP，一个包含50种不同问题类型、150个实例的基准测试，其决策逻辑更复杂、约束更紧密耦合、建模要求比现有基准更苛刻。在NL4COP和既有基准上的实验表明，TriVAL始终优于最先进的方法，在最具挑战性的问题上取得了最大的提升。

Original abstract: Optimization modeling serves as the pivotal bridge between natural-language problem descriptions and optimization solvers, and remains a cornerstone for bringing operations research (OR) into real-world decision making. Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have driven significant progress in automatic optimization modeling. However, existing methods still lack explicit validation during the modeling process, allowing errors introduced in earlier stages to carry through the pipeline and ultimately reduce final modeling accuracy. To address this challenge, we introduce TriVAL, a tri-validation framework that performs explicit validation at three stages of automatic optimization modeling: semantic specification, mathematical formulation, and code generation. At each stage, TriVAL follows a construct-validate-revise loop that assesses the current result against stage-specific criteria and revises it when needed. This design helps identify and correct errors before they accumulate across stages, helping preserve faithfulness throughout the modeling process. To evaluate automatic optimization modeling on more challenging combinatorial problems, we further introduce NL4COP, a benchmark of 150 instances across 50 diverse problem types with more complex decision logic, more tightly coupled constraints, and more demanding modeling requirements than existing benchmarks. Experiments on NL4COP and established benchmarks show that TriVAL consistently outperforms state-ofthe-art methods, with the largest gains on the most challenging problems.

</details>

### [96] [Emergent Communication between Heterogeneous Visual Agents through Decentralized Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11695v1)
*Mikako Ochiai,Masatoshi Nagano,Tadahiro Taniguchi*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 异构 agent 涌现通信，通用多 agent 方法。

TL;DR: 本文研究异质视觉智能体通过仅交换离散令牌的局部感知评估来涌现共享符号，发现即使在没有共享感知的情况下，共同符号也能出现，且视觉表示相似性影响语言内容和对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索当智能体具有不同视觉表示时，共享符号如何从局部感知评估中涌现，而不依赖外部通信目标。

Method: 提出Metropolis-Hastings标题游戏（MHCG），智能体交换令牌序列，监听器基于自身视觉特征使用MH准则接受或拒绝，使用不同视觉编码器对在MS-COCO上实验。

Result: MHCG产生视觉信息共享序列，优于基线；编码器异质性降低共享序列数量和质量，但保留特异性；MH接受避免退化。

Conclusion: 共享符号可从局部感知评估中涌现，视觉表示相似性塑造语言内容和对称性。

中文摘要：符号是共享的，但感知是私有的。我们通过分散学习研究异质视觉智能体之间的涌现通信，询问当智能体具有不同视觉表示时，哪些视觉信息可以变得可共享。我们的智能体不通过共享的外部通信目标来优化消息，而是仅交换离散的令牌序列，并使用局部感知证据更新自己的模型。这一设置关注涌现通信中一个未被充分探索的方面，考察没有共享感知访问时共同符号是否能够出现，以及私有视觉空间之间的相似性如何约束所产生语言的内容和对称性。我们在Metropolis-Hastings标题游戏（MHCG）中实例化这一设置，其中两个智能体通过交换提出的令牌序列协作形成共享标题，监听器使用基于自身视觉特征评估的MH风格标准接受或拒绝该序列。我们比较了三对冻结的视觉编码器，智能体从随机初始化的文本模块开始。在MS-COCO上的实验表明，MHCG产生的视觉信息共享令牌序列在跨智能体对齐、视觉特征预测和图像-文本检索方面优于无通信基线；所有跨智能体指标随着编码器不匹配的增加而下降。适度的编码器异质性减少了共享序列的数量，同时保留了每个序列的视觉特异性，而更强的编码器异质性产生更少、更粗糙且更不对称的序列。消融实验表明，监听器端的MH接受对于避免退化的令牌形成至关重要。这些结果表明，共享符号可以仅从局部感知评估中产生，编码器之间的视觉表示相似性塑造了所产生语言的内容和对称性。

Original abstract: Symbols are shared, but perception is private. We study emergent communication between heterogeneous visual agents through decentralized learning, asking what visual information can become shareable when agents have different visual representations. Instead of optimizing messages through a shared external communicative objective, our agents exchange only discrete token sequences and update their own models using local perceptual evidence. This setting focuses on an underexplored aspect of emergent communication, examining whether common symbols can arise without shared perceptual access, and how the similarity between private visual spaces constrains the content and symmetry of the resulting language. We instantiate this setting in the Metropolis-Hastings Captioning Game (MHCG), where two agents collaboratively form shared captions by exchanging proposed token sequences that a listener accepts or rejects using an MH-style criterion evaluated against its own visual features. We compare three pairings of frozen visual encoders, with agents starting from randomly initialized text modules. Experiments on MS-COCO show that MHCG produces visually informative shared token sequences that outperform a no-communication baseline in cross-agent alignment, visual-feature prediction, and image-text retrieval; all cross-agent metrics decline as encoder mismatch increases. Moderate encoder heterogeneity reduces the number of shared sequences while preserving per-sequence visual specificity, whereas stronger encoder heterogeneity yields fewer, coarser, and more asymmetric sequences. Ablations show that listener-side MH acceptance is critical for avoiding degenerate token formation. These results suggest that shared symbols can arise from local perceptual evaluation alone, with visual representational similarity across encoders shaping both the content and symmetry of the resulting language.

</details>


### [97] [VideoSEAL: Mitigating Evidence Misalignment in Agentic Long Video Understanding by Decoupling Answer Authority](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12571v1)
*Chenhao Qiu,Yechao Zhang,Xin Luo,Shien Song,Xusheng Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 长视频问答agent，提出解耦规划器-检查器框架，涉及agent规划与验证，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 本文提出解耦的规划器-检查器框架，解决长视频问答中证据错位问题，在多个基准上提升准确性和证据对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长视频理解智能体存在证据错位问题，即答案正确但缺乏检索证据支持，源于提示压力和奖励压力，根本原因是耦合的智能体范式混淆了长期规划与答案权威性。

Method: 提出解耦的规划器-检查器框架，将规划与答案权威性分离，通过像素级验证门控最终答案，并引入时间基础性和语义基础性两个诊断指标。

Result: 在LVBench上达到55.1%，在LongVideoBench上达到62.0%，提升准确性和证据对齐，生成可解释搜索轨迹，且架构可扩展、支持主干即插即用。

Conclusion: 解耦框架有效解决证据错位，实现更好的长视频问答性能，且具有可扩展性和灵活性。

中文摘要：长视频问答需要在高度冗余的内容中定位稀疏、时间分散的视觉证据。尽管当前的多模态大语言模型在短视频上表现良好，但长视频引入了长期搜索和验证，这通常需要多轮、智能体的交互。我们表明现有的长视频理解智能体可能表现出“证据错位”：它们产生正确的答案，但这些答案不被检索或检查的证据所支持。为了表征这种失败，我们引入两个诊断指标（时间基础性和语义基础性），并用它们揭示两种加剧错位的压力：推理时共享上下文饱和导致的提示压力，以及训练时仅基于结果的优化导致的奖励压力。这些发现指向一个结构性根本原因：耦合的智能体范式混淆了长期规划与答案权威性。因此，我们提出了解耦的规划器-检查器框架，该框架将规划与答案权威性分离，并在像素级验证上进行最终答案的门控。在四个长视频基准上，我们的框架提高了答案准确性和证据对齐性，在LVBench上达到55.1%，在LongVideoBench上达到62.0%，同时生成可解释的搜索轨迹。此外，解耦架构随搜索预算增加而一致扩展，并支持即插即用地升级MLLM主干，而无需重新训练规划器。代码和模型可在 https://github.com/Echochef/VideoSEAL 获取。

Original abstract: Long video question answering requires locating sparse, time-scattered visual evidence within highly redundant content. Although current MLLMs perform well on short videos, long videos introduce long-horizon search and verification, which often necessitates multi-turn, agentic interaction. We show that existing LVU agents can exhibit "evidence misalignment": they produce correct answers that are not supported by the retrieved or inspected evidence. To characterize this failure, we introduce two diagnostics (temporal groundedness and semantic groundedness) and use them to reveal two pressures that amplify misalignment: prompt pressure from shared-context saturation at inference time and reward pressure from outcome-only optimization during training. These findings point to a structural root cause: the coupled agent paradigm conflates long-horizon planning with answer authority. We therefore propose the decoupled planner-inspector framework, which separates planning from answer authority and gates final answering on pixel-level verification. Across four long-video benchmarks, our framework improves both answer accuracy and evidence alignment, achieving 55.1% on LVBench and 62.0% on LongVideoBench while producing interpretable search trajectories. Moreover, the decoupled architecture scales consistently with increased search budgets and supports plug-and-play upgrades of the MLLM backbone without retraining the planner. Code and models are available at https://github.com/Echochef/VideoSEAL.

</details>

### [98] [What Do You Think I Think? Accounting for Human Beliefs Using Second-Order Theory of Mind](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12745v1)
*Patrick Callaghan,Reid Simmons,Henny Admoni*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 二阶心智理论用于agent建模人类信念，对交互式agent有启发

TL;DR: 基于二阶心智理论，智能体通过I-POMDP建模人的错误信念和认知偏见，检测并适应性地生成反馈，用户研究表明能显著提升交互信息量和有用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能体实际知识与人对其所知的理解之间的差异会阻碍交互，而智能体检测到这些差异后可以提供反馈改善交互。

Method: 使用I-POMDP作为二阶心智理论框架，建模人的错误信念及认知偏见和启发式的演化，使智能体能检测认知偏见并自适应生成反馈。

Result: 面对面用户研究表明，ToM-2学习者能考虑教师的认知偏见，显著提升教师行为的信息量，且主观上认为其反馈更有用。

Conclusion: 基于二阶心智理论的方法能有效利用认知偏见检测来改善人机交互，提升智能体反馈的效用。

中文摘要：智能体实际知识与人对其所知的理解之间的差异可能会阻碍交互。如果智能体能够检测到这种差异，它就可以提供反馈以解释这些差异，并改善当前和未来的交互。本文以I-POMDP作为二阶心智理论（ToM-2）的框架，赋予智能体建模人对智能体错误信念的演化过程以及产生这些信念的认知偏见和启发式（CBH）的能力。通过这种方式，智能体可以在交互过程中检测到CBH可能发挥作用的情况，并自适应地生成考虑到这些因素的反馈。一项面对面的用户研究表明，ToM-2学习者能够考虑到教师的CBH影响，显著提高教师行为的信息量，主观结果也表明人们认为ToM-2学习者的反馈更有用。

Original abstract: Discrepancies between an agent's actual knowledge and what a person thinks the agent knows can hinder interactions. If an agent could detect such discrepancies, it could provide feedback to account for them and improve current and future interactions. Using the I-POMDP as a framework for a second-order Theory of Mind (ToM-2), this work endows an agent with the ability to model the evolution of a person's erroneous beliefs about an agent and the cognitive biases and heuristics (CBH) from which they arise. In doing so, the agent can detect when CBH might be at play during an interaction and adaptively generate feedback that accounts for them. An in-person user study shows how a ToM-2 learner can account for the effects of a teacher's CBH to significantly improve the informativeness of teacher actions, and subjective results suggest people find the ToM-2 learner's feedback more useful.

</details>

### [99] [Predictive Maps of Multi-Agent Reasoning: A Successor-Representation Spectrum for LLM Communication Topologies](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11453v2)
*Ethan Parks,Dalal Alharthi*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 多agent通信拓扑的预测图谱分析，可用于agent系统诊断

TL;DR: 提出基于后继表示谱量的结构诊断方法，可预推理多智能体LLM通信拓扑的失效模式，实验验证谱量预测鲁棒性和共识的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估仅能在事后且针对特定任务回答拓扑对漂移、共识和鲁棒性的影响，缺乏预推理诊断工具。

Method: 利用行随机通信算子的后继表示，提取三个谱量（谱半径、谱隙、条件数）作为结构诊断，推导链、星、网格的闭式谱，并通过12步状态跟踪任务验证。

Result: 条件数是扰动鲁棒性的完美秩预测器（r_s=1.0），谱隙部分预测共识（r_s=0.5），谱半径与累积误差完美反向（r_s=-1.0），反向归因于线性谱对非收缩偏差漂移不敏感，仿射噪声扩展恢复排序。

Conclusion: 该工作为多智能体LLM系统提供了表示感知、漂移感知的结构诊断，是迈向预推理评估的一步。

中文摘要：部署多智能体大语言模型（LLM）系统的从业者目前必须在链、星、网格及更丰富的变体等通信拓扑之间做出选择，而没有任何预推理诊断可以判断哪种拓扑会放大漂移、收敛为共识或在扰动下保持鲁棒。现有评估仅能在事后且仅针对所测量的任务回答这些问题。我们引入了一种基于行随机通信算子的后继表示 $M = (I - γP)^{-1}$ 的多智能体LLM通信图结构诊断方法，并将其三个谱量——谱半径 $ρ(M)$、谱隙 $Δ(M)$ 和条件数 $κ(M)$——与三种不同的失效模式联系起来。我们推导了在行随机归一化下链、星和网格的闭式谱，并在一个12步结构化状态跟踪任务上使用Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct在100次独立试验中验证了预测。条件数是经验扰动鲁棒性的完美秩阶预测器（$r_s = 1.0$）；谱隙部分预测了共识动力学（$r_s = 0.5$）；而谱半径与累积误差完美反向相关（$r_s = -1.0$）。我们将这种反向关系归因于线性谱对非收缩偏差漂移视而不见的机制，并提出了一种仿射噪声扩展预测图，恢复了经验排序。我们认为这是迈向表示感知、漂移感知的多智能体LLM系统结构诊断的第一步，与经典谱理论和共识理论并驾齐驱。

Original abstract: Practitioners deploying multi-agent large language model (LLM) systems must currently choose between communication topologies such as chain, star, mesh, and richer variants without any pre-inference diagnostic for which topology will amplify drift, converge to consensus, or remain robust under perturbation. Existing evaluation answers these questions only post hoc and only for the task measured. We introduce a structural diagnostic for multi-agent LLM communication graphs based on the successor representation $M = (I - γP)^{-1}$ of the row-stochastic communication operator, and we connect three of its spectral quantities, the spectral radius $ρ(M)$, the spectral gap $Δ(M)$, and the condition number $κ(M)$, to three distinct failure modes. We derive closed-form spectra for the chain, star, and mesh under row-stochastic normalization, and validate the predictions on a 12-step structured state-tracking task with Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct over 100 independent trials. The condition number is a perfect rank-order predictor of empirical perturbation robustness ($r_s = 1.0$); the spectral gap partially predicts consensus dynamics ($r_s = 0.5$); and the spectral radius is perfectly \emph{inverted} with respect to cumulative error ($r_s = -1.0$). We trace this inversion to a regime in which linear spectra are blind to non-contracting bias drift, and we propose an affine-noise extension of the predictive map that recovers the empirical ordering. We read this as a first step toward representational, drift-aware structural diagnostics for multi-agent LLM systems, sitting alongside classical spectral and consensus theory.

</details>


### [100] [Mechanism Plausibility in Generative Agent-Based Modeling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12824v2)
*Patrick Zhao,David Huu Pham,Nicholas Vincent*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 生成式agent建模机制合理性评估，提出量表，对agent评估有参考

TL;DR: 该研究整合了LLM-ABM与科学哲学，提出了一个四级的机制合理性量表，以区分模型的生成充分性和机制合理性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前研究混淆了LLM在ABM中的能力、预测和解释，缺乏区分模型生成现象能力与机制解释合理性的标准。

Method: 通过结合近期LLM-ABM工作与科学哲学文献，可操作化定义“合理性”，开发了四级量表。

Result: 提出的量表能够分离模型生成充分性和机制合理性的评估，明确预测模型与解释模型的不同角色。

Conclusion: 机制合理性量表为评估LLM-ABM模拟提供了框架，有助于建模者区分能力进展与解释性进展。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）能够在没有显式编程规则的情况下生成高级多样的现象。这一能力使其被应用于不同的基于智能体的模型（ABMs）和社会模拟中。最近的研究探讨了它们生成不同感兴趣现象的能力，例如社交媒体平台上的人类行为或博弈论场景中的外星行为。然而，能力、预测和解释是不同的——借鉴科学哲学和机制文献，解释需要在一定程度上展示现象是如何由相关的组织实体和活动产生的。对于建模者来说，描述实验的特征或模拟是否在能力（或解释）方面取得了进展，如果没有基于可能相距较远的研究领域，可能会很困难。我们将近期关于LLM-ABMs的工作与当代科学哲学文献相结合，并以此可操作化地定义了“合理性”（plausibility）的四级量表。我们的量表将模型生成充分性（再现现象的能力）与机制合理性（现象如何产生）的评估分开，并阐明了不同模型（如预测模型和解释模型）的不同角色。我们将其称为机制合理性量表。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can generate high-level diverse phenomena without explicitly programmed rules. This capability has led to their adoption within different agent-based models (ABMs) and social simulations. Recent studies investigate their ability to generate different phenomena of interest, for example, human behavior on social media platforms or alien behavior in game-theoretic scenarios. However, capability, prediction, and explanation are different--drawing from the philosophy of science and mechanisms literature, explanation requires showing, to some degree, how a phenomenon is produced by related organized entities and activities. For modelers, describing the characteristics of an experiment or whether a simulation provides progress in capability (or explanation), can be difficult without being grounded in potentially distant research areas. We integrate recent work on LLM-ABMs with contemporary philosophy of science literature and use it to operationalize a definition of 'plausibility' in a four-level scale. Our scale separates the evaluation of a model's generative sufficiency (ability to reproduce a phenomenon) from its mechanistic plausibility (how the phenomenon could be produced), and clarifies the distinct roles of different models, such as predictive and explanatory ones. We introduce this as the Mechanism Plausibility Scale.

</details>

### [101] [Trade-offs in Decentralized Agentic AI Discovery Across the Compute Continuum](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11839v1)
*Patrizio Dazzi,Emanuele Carlini,Matteo Mordacchini,Saul Urso*

Main category: cs.DC

Selection reason: 去中心化agent发现机制研究，涉及多agent协调与分布式架构，对agent系统设计有参考价值。

TL;DR: 本文在4096节点基准测试下比较了Chord、Pastry和Kademlia三种结构化覆盖网络在代理发现中的性能权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代理系统需要跨云、边缘和间歇性连接域的有效发现机制，而去中心化DHT是实现代理目录的有前途方向。

Method: 在共享控制平面框架内，通过4096节点静态和动态基准测试，对比Chord、Pastry和Kademlia在发现可靠性、启动行为和控制平面开销方面的表现。

Result: 三种覆盖网络在发现可靠性、启动行为和控制平面开销上表现出不同的权衡特性。

Conclusion: 研究阐明了不同结构化覆盖网络在边缘到云环境中用于代理发现的操作点，为设计选择提供依据。

中文摘要：部署在计算连续体中的代理系统需要发现机制，这些机制在云、边缘和间歇性连接域中保持有效。在一些新兴的代理架构中，去中心化发现已经是一个活跃的设计方向，将基于DHT的查找置于代理目录的路径上。本文研究了用于代理发现的主要结构化覆盖网络族之间的权衡，比较了Chord、Pastry和Kademlia作为共享控制平面框架内的候选索引基板。使用以4096节点静态比较和代表性4096节点动态变化基准为中心的基准测试子集，本文描述了发现可靠性、启动行为和控制平面开销在这些覆盖网络中的变化。目标是阐明它们在边缘到云环境中为代理发现暴露的操作点。

Original abstract: Agentic systems deployed across the compute continuum need discovery mechanisms that remain effective across cloud, edge, and intermittently connected domains. In some emerging agentic architectures, decentralized discovery is already an active design direction, placing DHT-based lookup on the path toward agent directories. This paper studies the trade-offs among major structured-overlay families for agent discovery, comparing Chord, Pastry, and Kademlia as candidate indexing substrates within a shared control-plane framework. Using a benchmark subset centered on a 4096-node stationary comparison and a representative 4096-node churn benchmark, the paper characterizes how discovery reliability, startup behavior, and control-plane overhead vary across these overlays. The goal is to clarify the operating points they expose for agent discovery across edge-to-cloud environments.

</details>

### [102] [Metric-Gradient Projection for Stable Multi-Agent Policy Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18809v1)
*Zuyuan Zhang,Sizhe Tang,Mahdi Imani,Tian Lan*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 多智能体策略学习稳定投影方法，可迁移至多agent协作。

TL;DR: 提出HPML方法，通过Hodge投影将多智能体联合更新场分解为度量梯度部分，提高学习稳定性和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体学习中联合更新场的耦合导致缓慢或不稳定学习，现有方法难以解决。

Method: 将联合更新场投影到度量梯度分量，通过变分定义、泊松方程，使用图和神经网络实现。

Result: 受控实验验证几何机制，CTDE基准测试显示稳定性和归一化回报提升。

Conclusion: HPML作为插件可改善MARL管线。

中文摘要：通用和的多智能体学习通常受堆叠更新场支配，其中每个智能体的策略更新改变了其他智能体面临的优化景观。这种耦合可能将集体改进的可积分量与循环交互动力学纠缠在一起，导致多智能体学习缓慢或不稳定。现有的方法，如正则化、信用分配和共识方法，通过局部或算法修改来稳定MARL；HPML通过将联合更新场投影到度量梯度分量上对它们进行补充。我们引入HPML（Hodge投影多智能体学习），它将多智能体系统的联合更新场视为向量场的L^2空间中的一个元素，并计算一个Hodge型投影到最近的度量梯度势流。HPML跟随投影分量作为更新方向，产生在所选度量和采样度量下最近的度量梯度场。该投影是变分定义的，由泊松型方程表征，并通过基于图和摊销神经实现来从样本中恢复投影方向。我们证明了投影动力学允许一个Lyapunov势，并产生具有显式加性非势项的平衡间隙界。受控实验验证了几何机制，CTDE基准测试表明，当HPML作为MARL流水线中的插件投影层使用时，稳定性和归一化回报均有提高。

Original abstract: General-sum multi-agent learning is often governed by a stacked update field in which each agent's policy update changes the optimization landscape faced by the others. This coupling can entangle an integrable component of collective improvement with cyclic interaction dynamics, leading to slow or unstable multi-agent learning. Existing approaches, such as regularization, credit assignment, and consensus methods, stabilize MARL through local or algorithmic modifications; HPML complements them by projecting the joint update field onto a metric-gradient component. We introduce \textbf{HPML} (\textbf{H}odge-\textbf{P}rojected \textbf{M}ulti-agent \textbf{L}earning), which views the joint update field of a multi-agent system as an element of an $L^2$ space of vector fields and computes a Hodge-type projection onto the closest metric-gradient potential flow. HPML follows the projected component as the update direction, yielding the closest metric-gradient field under the chosen metric and sampling measure. The projection is defined variationally, characterized by a Poisson-type equation, and implemented through graph-based and amortized neural realizations that recover projected directions from samples. We show that the projected dynamics admit a Lyapunov potential and yield equilibrium-gap bounds with an explicit additive non-potentiality term. Controlled experiments validate the geometric mechanism, and CTDE benchmarks show improved stability and normalized return when HPML is used as a plug-in projection layer in MARL pipelines.

</details>


### [103] [Drop the Act: Probe-Filtered RL for Faithful Chain-of-Thought Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11467v1)
*Swapnil Parekh*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 探针过滤RL实现忠实思维链，可提升agent推理可信度

TL;DR: ProFIL通过探头滤波减少推理模型的“推理戏剧”，提高忠实度并缩短链长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推理模型产生无用的“推理戏剧”步骤，浪费资源并污染可解释性，需要一种方法在保持准确性的同时减少这种无效推理。

Method: 在冻结基础模型上训练多头注意力探头，从内部激活中检测事后承诺步骤；在GRPO训练中，探头得分超过阈值的rollout的优势被归零，从而抑制戏剧步骤。

Result: 在GSM8K、LiveCodeBench、ToolUse、MMLU-Redux四个领域和Llama-8B、Qwen-7B两个模型上，戏剧减少11-100%，忠实比例提升（如LiveCodeBench +24pp），链长缩短4-19%，准确率保持或提升，且优于长度惩罚基线。

Conclusion: ProFIL能有效减少推理戏剧、提高思维链忠实度并缩短链长，增益来源于语义承诺检测而非简单的链压缩，且方法稳定可靠。

中文摘要：推理模型在事后将它们在内部已经承诺的答案合理化，产生了一系列*推理戏剧*：看似经过深思熟虑的步骤，但对正确性毫无贡献。这浪费了推理令牌，污染了可解释性，并掩盖了模型实际计算的内容。我们引入了**ProFIL**（**探**头-**滤**波强化学习），作为分组相对策略优化（GRPO）的一个即插即用扩展，以减少戏剧、增加思维链忠实度并缩短链长。一个多头注意力探头在冻结的基础模型上训练*一次*，仅从内部激活中检测事后承诺步骤；在GRPO期间，探头得分超过阈值的展开序列的优势被归零。*我们的核心发现是，在冻结基础上训练的探头，使用验证器派生的标签且无需人工标注，提供了一个稳定的信号，抑制了戏剧，同时抵制了先前工作预测的RL混淆故障模式。*在四个推理领域（GSM8K、LiveCodeBench、ToolUse、MMLU-Redux）和两种模型架构（Llama-8B、Qwen-7B）上，ProFIL将事后承诺戏剧减少了**11%到100%**，提高了忠实比例（例如，在LiveCodeBench上使用独立的Claude 3.7 Sonnet评判器时提高了24个百分点），并缩短了4%到19%的链长，同时保持或提高了任务准确性。ProFIL还击败了匹配的长度惩罚GRPO基线，将增益隔离为语义承诺检测而非链压缩。探头权重、训练配置和展开序列在所有四个领域都发布。

Original abstract: Reasoning models post-hoc rationalize answers they have already committed to internally, producing chains of *reasoning theater*: deliberative-looking steps that contribute nothing to correctness. This wastes inference tokens, pollutes interpretability, and obscures what the model actually computed. We introduce **ProFIL** (**Pro**be-**Fil**tered Reinforcement Learning) to *reduce theater, increase chain-of-thought faithfulness, and shrink chain length* in a single, drop-in extension to Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). A multi-head attention probe is trained *once* on the *frozen* base model to detect post-commitment steps from internal activations alone; during GRPO, rollouts whose probe score exceeds a threshold have their advantage zeroed. *Our central finding is that a probe trained on a frozen base, with verifier-derived labels and no human annotation, provides a stable signal that suppresses theater while resisting the RL-obfuscation failure mode predicted by prior work.* Across four reasoning domains (GSM8K, LiveCodeBench, ToolUse, MMLU-Redux) and two model architectures (Llama-8B, Qwen-7B), ProFIL reduces post-commitment theater by **11--100%**, raises faithful-fraction (e.g., +24pp on LiveCodeBench under an independent Claude 3.7 Sonnet judge), and shortens chains by 4--19%, all while preserving or improving task accuracy. ProFIL also beats a matched length-penalty GRPO baseline, isolating the gain as semantic commitment-detection rather than chain compression. Probe weights, training configurations, and rollouts are released across all four domains.

</details>


### [104] [Evolutionary Task Discovery: Advancing Reasoning Frontiers via Skill Composition and Complexity Scaling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11666v1)
*Liqin Ye,Yanbin Yin,Michael Galarnyk,Yuzhao Heng,Sudheer Chava,Chao Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 进化任务发现合成训练数据，可启发 agent 训练数据生成。

TL;DR: 提出EvoTD框架，通过结构化演化算子（交叉和参数变异）在算法技能和复杂度双轴流形上定向搜索数据合成，结合最近发展区过滤，显著提升LLM推理能力并跨模型泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据合成方法（如无结构变异或探索）导致同质性崩溃，无法系统扩展LLM推理前沿，限制了后训练范式的有效性。

Method: 提出EvoTD框架，将数据合成视为在算法技能和复杂度属性的双轴流形上的定向搜索，使用交叉算子合成新颖技能组合增强多样性，参数变异算子扩展结构约束驱动鲁棒泛化，并集成动态最近发展区过滤器确保任务可学习。

Result: EvoTD在多个模型架构、预训练范式和规模上一致带来显著的推理提升，证明结构化演化课程有效支持推理改进。

Conclusion: 结构化演化课程（EvoTD）能够系统性地扩展推理前沿，有效提升LLM的推理能力，并具有良好的泛化性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）的推理前沿通过现代后训练范式（例如，基于可验证奖励的强化学习，RLVR）取得了显著进步。然而，这些方法的有效性仍然受到训练数据多样性和复杂性的根本限制。一种实用的解决方案是数据合成；然而，现有依赖于无结构变异或探索的方法遭受同质性崩溃，未能系统性地扩展推理前沿。为了克服这一问题，我们提出演化式任务发现（EvoTD），这是一个将数据合成视为在算法技能和复杂度属性的双轴流形上的定向搜索的框架。我们引入结构化的演化算子来导航该空间：一个交叉算子，通过合成新颖的技能组合来增强多样性；以及一个参数变异算子，通过扩展结构约束（例如，输入大小、树深度）来驱动鲁棒的泛化。关键的是，我们集成了一个动态的最近发展区过滤器，确保任务处于模型可学习的区域内。实验结果表明，EvoTD带来了显著的推理提升，并且这些提升在模型架构、预训练范式和规模上一致地泛化，证明了结构化演化课程可以有效支持推理改进。我们在https://github.com/liqinye/EvoTD上发布了代码。

Original abstract: The reasoning frontier of Large Language Models (LLMs) has advanced significantly through modern post-training paradigms (e.g., Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR)). However, the efficacy of these methods remains fundamentally constrained by the diversity and complexity of the training data. One practical solution is data synthesis; yet, prevalent methods relying on unstructured mutation or exploration suffer from homogeneity collapse, failing to systematically expand the reasoning frontier. To overcome this, we propose Evoutionary Task Discovery (EvoTD), a framework that treats data synthesis as a directed search over a dual-axis manifold of Algorithmic Skills and Complexity Attributes. We introduce structured evolutionary operators to navigate this space: a Crossover operator that synthesizes novel skill compositions to enhance diversity, and a Parametric Mutation operator that scales structural constraints (e.g., input size, tree depth) to drive robust generalization. Crucially, we integrate a dynamic Zone of Proximal Development filter, ensuring tasks lie within the learnable region of the model. Empirically, EvoTD delivers substantial reasoning gains that generalize consistently across model architectures, pretraining regimes, and scales, demonstrating that structured evolutionary curricula can effectively support reasoning improvement. We release our code on https://github.com/liqinye/EvoTD.

</details>


### [105] [Shaping Zero-Shot Coordination via State Blocking](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11688v1)
*Mingu Kang,Sunwoo Lee,Yonghyeon Jo,Seungyul Han*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 零样本协调多智能体方法，可迁移到 agent 协作。

TL;DR: SBC通过状态阻塞创建虚拟环境，使智能体接触多样的次优伙伴策略，提升零样本协调的泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通过增加伙伴多样性难以实现对未见伙伴的可靠泛化，需要新的框架改善零样本协调。

Method: SBC通过状态阻塞生成一系列虚拟环境，无需直接修改环境，使智能体在训练中经历多样的次优伙伴策略。

中文摘要：零样本协调（ZSC）旨在使智能体能够与独立训练的伙伴合作而无需事先交互，这是现实世界多智能体系统和人类-人工智能协作的关键要求。现有方法大多强调在训练期间增加伙伴多样性，然而这类策略往往无法实现对未见伙伴的可靠泛化。我们引入了状态阻塞协调（SBC），一个简单而有效的框架，通过诱导多样化的交互场景来改进ZSC，而无需直接修改环境。具体地，SBC通过状态阻塞生成一系列虚拟环境，允许智能体体验广泛的次优伙伴策略。在多个基准测试中，SBC在零样本协调方面展示了优越的性能，包括对人类伙伴的强泛化能力。

Original abstract: Zero-shot coordination (ZSC) aims to enable agents to cooperate with independently trained partners without prior interaction, a key requirement for real-world multi-agent systems and human-AI collaboration. Existing approaches have largely emphasized increasing partner diversity during training, yet such strategies often fall short of achieving reliable generalization to unseen partners. We introduce State-Blocked Coordination (SBC), a simple yet effective framework that improves ZSC by inducing diverse interaction scenarios without direct environment modification. Specifically, SBC generates a family of virtual environments through state blocking, allowing agents to experience a wide range of suboptimal partner policies. Across multiple benchmarks, SBC demonstrates superior performance in zero-shot coordination, including strong generalization to human partners.

### [106] [GEAR: Granularity-Adaptive Advantage Reweighting for LLM Agents via Self-Distillation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11853v2)
*Sijia Li,Yuchen Huang,Zifan Liu,Yanping Li,Jingjing Fu,Li Zhao,Jiang Bian,Ling Zhang,Jun Zhang,Rui Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出自适应粒度信用分配框架GEAR，提升LLM agent工具使用和推理性能，可直接迁移到coding agent训练

TL;DR: 提出GEAR框架，通过自蒸馏获取token和片段级信号，自适应重加权优势，显著提升LLM在长程任务中的强化学习性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结果级奖励监督粗糙，细粒度信用分配在长程轨迹中难以获取可靠局部信用并正确分配。

Method: 比较在线学生与条件教师的散度，以散度峰值作为自适应片段边界，对齐部分保留token级分辨率，偏离部分分组为片段并用散度调制优势。

Result: 在8个数学推理和工具使用基准上，GEAR均优于GRPO、自蒸馏基线及token/turn级方法，低准确率任务上提升达20%。

Conclusion: 自适应重加权方案在挑战性长程设置中有效，尤其对困难任务提升显著。

中文摘要：强化学习已成为LLM智能体广泛使用的后训练方法，其中训练通常依赖于提供粗糙监督的结果级奖励。虽然细粒度的信用分配对于有效的策略更新很有前景，但获取可靠的局部信用并将其分配给长程轨迹的正确部分仍是一个开放挑战。在本文中，我们提出粒度自适应优势重加权（GEAR），一种自适应粒度的信用分配框架，该框架利用从自蒸馏中获得的token级和片段级信号重塑轨迹级GRPO优势。GEAR将在线策略学生与真实条件教师进行比较，以获得参考引导的散度信号，用于识别自适应片段边界和调制局部优势权重。这种散度通常在语义偏差开始时出现峰值，而同一自回归延续中的后续token可能回到低散度。因此，GEAR将这些峰值视为自适应信用区域的锚点：在学生与教师保持对齐的地方，保留token级分辨率；在学生偏离的地方，GEAR将相应的延续分组为一个自适应片段，并使用偏离点的散度调制该片段的优势。在Qwen3 4B和8B模型上的八个数学推理和智能工具使用基准测试中，实验表明GEAR始终优于标准GRPO、仅自蒸馏基线以及token级或turn级信用分配方法。在GRPO基线准确率较低的基准上，增益尤其显著，相对于GRPO提升高达约20%，这表明所提出的自适应重加权方案在更具挑战性的长程设置中特别有用。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning has become a widely used post-training approach for LLM agents, where training commonly relies on outcome-level rewards that provide only coarse supervision. While finer-grained credit assignment is promising for effective policy updates, obtaining reliable local credit and assigning it to the right parts of the long-horizon trajectory remains an open challenge. In this paper, we propose Granularity-adaptivE Advantage Reweighting (GEAR), an adaptive-granularity credit assignment framework that reshapes the trajectory-level GRPO advantage using token- and segment-level signals derived from self-distillation. GEAR compares an on-policy student with a ground-truth-conditioned teacher to obtain a reference-guided divergence signal for identifying adaptive segment boundaries and modulating local advantage weights. This divergence often spikes at the onset of a semantic deviation, while later tokens in the same autoregressive continuation may return to low divergence. GEAR therefore treats such spikes as anchors for adaptive credit regions: where the student remains aligned with the teacher, token-level resolution is preserved; where it departs, GEAR groups the corresponding continuation into an adaptive segment and uses the divergence at the departure point to modulate the segment' s advantage. Experiments across eight mathematical reasoning and agentic tool-use benchmarks with Qwen3 4B and 8B models show that GEAR consistently outperforms standard GRPO, self-distillation-only baselines, and token- or turn-level credit-assignment methods. The gains are especially strong on benchmarks with lower GRPO baseline accuracy, reaching up to around 20\% over GRPO, suggesting that the proposed adaptive reweighting scheme is especially useful in more challenging long-horizon settings.

### [107] [Composition of Memory Experts for Diffusion World Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18813v1)
*Sebastian Stapf,Pablo Acuaviva Huertos,Aram Davtyan,Paolo Favaro*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 组合记忆专家的扩散世界模型，为agent规划提供记忆架构启发

TL;DR: 提出一种基于扩散的专家乘积框架，通过解耦短期、长期和空间记忆专家，克服世界模型中记忆保真度和扩展性之间的权衡，提升时间一致性和导航性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型架构（如Transformer、循环和状态空间模型）在记忆保真度和计算扩展性之间存在根本性权衡，难以同时捕捉局部细节和长程历史，且存在模式坍塌问题。

Method: 采用扩散模型框架，通过对比专家乘积集成三个异构记忆专家：短期记忆专家（局部动态）、长期记忆专家（外部权重存储情景历史，通过测试时微调更新）和空间长期记忆专家（几何空间一致性），避免单一架构的局限性。

Result: 在模拟和真实世界基准测试中，该方法在时间一致性、过去观察回忆和导航性能上均优于现有方法，且能扩展到长上下文而不产生二次计算成本。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种新的记忆增强扩散世界模型范式，通过组合专家解耦记忆与架构，有效解决了历史保真度和扩展性的矛盾，为强化学习中的规划和决策提供了更可靠的未来预测能力。

中文摘要：世界模型旨在预测与过去观察一致的可能未来，这是强化学习中规划和决策的核心能力。然而，现有架构面临一个根本性的记忆权衡：变换器保留了局部细节，但受限于二次注意力；而循环模型和状态空间模型扩展性更好，但以保真度为代价压缩历史。为克服这一权衡，我们建议将未来-过去一致性与任何单一架构解耦，转而利用一组专门的专家。我们引入一个基于扩散的框架，通过对比专家乘积公式整合异构记忆模型。我们的方法实例化了三个互补角色：捕获精细局部动态的短期记忆专家、通过轻量测试时微调将情景历史存储在外部扩散权重中的长期记忆专家，以及强制几何和空间一致性的空间长期记忆专家。这种组合设计避免了模式坍塌，并在不产生二次成本的情况下扩展到长上下文。在模拟和真实世界基准测试中，我们的方法提高了时间一致性、过去观察的回忆以及导航性能，为构建和操作记忆增强的扩散世界模型建立了一个新的范式。

Original abstract: World models aim to predict plausible futures consistent with past observations, a capability central to planning and decision-making in reinforcement learning. Yet, existing architectures face a fundamental memory trade-off: transformers preserve local detail but are bottlenecked by quadratic attention, while recurrent and state-space models scale more efficiently but compress history at the cost of fidelity. To overcome this trade-off, we suggest decoupling future-past consistency from any single architecture and instead leveraging a set of specialized experts. We introduce a diffusion-based framework that integrates heterogeneous memory models through a contrastive product-of-experts formulation. Our approach instantiates three complementary roles: a short-term memory expert that captures fine local dynamics, a long-term memory expert that stores episodic history in external diffusion weights via lightweight test-time finetuning, and a spatial long-term memory expert that enforces geometric and spatial coherence. This compositional design avoids mode collapse and scales to long contexts without incurring a quadratic cost. Across simulated and real-world benchmarks, our method improves temporal consistency, recall of past observations, and navigation performance, establishing a novel paradigm for building and operating memory-augmented diffusion world models.

### [108] [Holder Policy Optimisation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12058v2)
*Yuxiang Chen,Dingli Liang,Yihang Chen,Ziqin Gong,Chenyang Le,Zhaokai Wang,Jiachen Zhu,Lingyu Yang,Jianghao Lin,Weinan Zhang,Jun Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 改进GRPO的通用强化学习方法（HölderPO），可迁移到agent训练。

TL;DR: 用Hölder均值统一令牌级概率聚合，通过动态退火调节参数p，解决GRPO中固定聚合的适应性问题，提升稳定性和收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决GRPO依赖固定聚合机制导致的适应性受限和训练崩溃/性能不佳的权衡问题。

Method: 提出HölderPO框架，用Hölder均值聚合令牌级概率，通过动态退火算法在训练中调节参数p。

Result: 在数学基准上平均准确率54.9%，相对提升7.2%；ALFWorld成功率93.8%。

Conclusion: HölderPO通过动态调节p实现更好的稳定性和收敛性，性能优于现有基线。

中文摘要：组相对策略优化（GRPO）通过估计一组采样轨迹的优势来增强大型语言模型。然而，将这些轨迹级优势映射到策略更新需要聚合每个序列内的令牌级概率。对此步骤依赖固定聚合机制从根本上限制了算法的适应性。经验上，我们观察到一个关键的权衡：某些固定聚合经常遭受训练崩溃，而其他聚合则无法产生令人满意的性能。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了\textbf{HölderPO}，一个通用的策略优化框架，通过Hölder均值统一令牌级概率聚合。通过明确调节参数$p$，我们的框架提供了对梯度集中度和方差边界之间权衡的连续控制。理论上，我们证明较大的$p$会集中梯度以放大稀疏学习信号，而较小的$p$则严格限制梯度方差。由于没有静态配置能普遍解决这种集中-稳定性权衡，我们通过一个动态退火算法实例化该框架，该算法在训练生命周期中逐步调度$p$。大量评估表明，该方法在稳定性和收敛性上优于现有基线。具体而言，我们的方法在多个数学基准测试中实现了最先进的平均准确率$54.9\%$，相对于标准GRPO产生了$7.2\%$的相对提升，并在ALFWorld上取得了$93.8\%$的出色成功率。

Original abstract: Group Relative Policy Optimisation (GRPO) enhances large language models by estimating advantages across a group of sampled trajectories. However, mapping these trajectory-level advantages to policy updates requires aggregating token-level probabilities within each sequence. Relying on a fixed aggregation mechanism for this step fundamentally limits the algorithm's adaptability. Empirically, we observe a critical trade-off: certain fixed aggregations frequently suffer from training collapse, while others fail to yield satisfactory performance. To resolve this, we propose \textbf{HölderPO}, a generalised policy optimisation framework unifying token-level probability aggregation via the Hölder mean. By explicitly modulating the parameter $p$, our framework provides continuous control over the trade-off between gradient concentration and variance bounds. Theoretically, we prove that a larger $p$ concentrates the gradient to amplify sparse learning signals, whereas a smaller $p$ strictly bounds gradient variance. Because no static configuration can universally resolve this concentration-stability trade-off, we instantiate the framework with a dynamic annealing algorithm that progressively schedules $p$ across the training lifecycle. Extensive evaluations demonstrate superior stability and convergence over existing baselines. Specifically, our approach achieves a state-of-the-art average accuracy of $54.9\%$ across multiple mathematical benchmarks, yielding a substantial $7.2\%$ relative gain over standard GRPO and secures an exceptional $93.8\%$ success rate on ALFWorld.

</details>


### [109] [Missing Old Logits in Asynchronous Agentic RL: Semantic Mismatch and Repair Methods for Off-Policy Correction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12070v2)
*Zhong Guan,Yongjian Guo,Haoran Sun,Wen Huang,Shuai Di,Likang Wu,Xiong Jun Wu,Hongke Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 异步agentic RL中缺失旧logits问题的修复方法，直接相关agent训练。

TL;DR: 针对异步强化学习训练中缺失旧logits的问题，本文研究了精确和近似修正策略，并采用改进的PPO-EWMA方法，显著提升了训练速度和优化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 异步流水线中缺失历史训练侧logits导致PPO解耦修正语义被破坏，裁剪和掩蔽阈值交互不良，因此需要解决此问题以实现有效的异步训练。

Method: 提出了三种精确获取旧logits的策略（快照版本跟踪、专用旧logits模型、部分推演中断同步），并比较了系统权衡；同时从近似修正角度采用改进的PPO-EWMA方法以保留解耦修正优势。

Result: 改进的PPO-EWMA方法在训练速度和优化性能上取得了显著提升。

Conclusion: 本文通过解决缺失旧logits问题，实现了更好的异步强化学习训练，验证了精确与近似修正路径的有效性。

中文摘要：异步强化学习通过将样本生成与策略优化解耦，提高了大型语言模型智能体的推演吞吐量，但也为PPO风格的离线修正引入了一种关键失效模式。在异构训练系统中，总重要性比率理想上应分解为两个语义不同的因子：一个“训练-推理差异项”，用于对齐同一行为策略版本下推理侧和训练侧的分布；以及一个“策略陈旧项”，用于约束从历史策略到当前策略的更新。我们表明，具有延迟更新和部分推演的实际异步流水线常常丢失所需的历史训练侧logits，即旧的logits。这种缺失旧logits的问题将差异修复与陈旧性修正纠缠在一起，破坏了解耦修正的预期语义，并使裁剪和掩蔽阈值产生不良交互。为解决此问题，我们研究了精确和近似修正两条路径。我们提出了三种精确获取旧logits的策略：基于快照的版本跟踪、专用的旧logits模型以及通过部分推演中断进行同步，并比较了它们的系统权衡。从近似修正的角度，我们专注于在无法低成本恢复精确旧logits时，通过更合适的近似策略保留解耦修正的优势，而不增加额外系统开销。基于此分析，我们采用了一种改进的PPO-EWMA方法，在训练速度和优化性能方面都取得了显著提升。

Original abstract: Asynchronous reinforcement learning improves rollout throughput for large language model agents by decoupling sample generation from policy optimization, but it also introduces a critical failure mode for PPO-style off-policy correction. In heterogeneous training systems, the total importance ratio should ideally be decomposed into two semantically distinct factors: a \emph{training--inference discrepancy term} that aligns inference-side and training-side distributions at the same behavior-policy version, and a \emph{policy-staleness term} that constrains the update from the historical policy to the current policy. We show that practical asynchronous pipelines with delayed updates and partial rollouts often lose the required historical training-side logits, or old logits. This missing-old-logit problem entangles discrepancy repair with staleness correction, breaks the intended semantics of decoupled correction, and makes clipping and masking thresholds interact undesirably. To address this issue, we study both exact and approximate correction routes. We propose three exact old-logit acquisition strategies: snapshot-based version tracking, a dedicated old-logit model, and synchronization via partial rollout interruption, and compare their system trade-offs. From the perspective of approximate correction, we focus on preserving the benefits of decoupled correction through a more appropriate approximate policy when exact old logits cannot be recovered at low cost, without incurring extra system overhead. Following this analysis, we adopt a revised PPO-EWMA method, which achieves significant gains in both training speed and optimization performance.

### [110] [No More, No Less: Task Alignment in Terminal Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12233v1)
*Sina Mavali,David Pape,Jonathan Evertz,Samira Abedini,Devansh Srivastav,Thorsten Eisenhofer,Sahar Abdelnabi,Lea Schönherr*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 研究terminal agent的任务对齐能力，提出TAB benchmark，涉及选择性使用环境指令，对coding agent可靠性与评测有直接启发。

TL;DR: 提出了TAB基准，用于评估智能体选择性遵循环境指令的能力，发现前沿智能体在任务对齐上存在显著不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准无法衡量智能体在复杂任务中区分相关指令与干扰项的能力，导致智能体可能通过盲目遵循或完全忽略指令而表现虚假的鲁棒性。

Method: 从Terminal-Bench 2.1中构建89个任务，每个任务缺失关键信息，该信息嵌入在环境工件中作为必要线索，同时加入合理但无关的干扰项，评估智能体选择性使用线索的能力。

Result: 十个前沿智能体在TAB上任务对齐得分低，最强智能体任务完成度高但对齐度低；提示注入防御方法同时抑制了干扰项和必要线索的执行。

Conclusion: 任务对齐的智能体需要选择性使用环境指令，而非全盘接受或拒绝，当前智能体存在系统性任务对齐差距。

中文摘要：终端智能体越来越能够从单一用户提示中自主执行复杂、长期的任务。为此，它们必须解释环境中遇到的指令（例如README文件、代码注释、堆栈跟踪）并确定其与任务的相关性。这产生了一个基本挑战：必须遵循相关线索以完成任务，而必须忽略不相关或误导性的线索。现有基准未捕捉这一能力。一个智能体可能通过盲目地遵循所有指令显得有能力，或者通过完全忽略指令显得稳健。我们引入了TAB（任务对齐基准），这是一套来自Terminal-Bench 2.1的89个终端任务。每个任务都故意未完全指定，缺失的信息作为必要线索嵌入在自然的工件中，同时附有看似合理但不相关的干扰项。解决这些任务需要选择性使用线索并忽略干扰项。将TAB应用于十个前沿智能体揭示了任务能力与任务对齐之间的系统性差距。最强的Terminal-Bench智能体在TAB上实现了高任务完成度但低任务对齐度。评估六种提示注入防御进一步表明，抑制干扰项执行也会抑制完成任务所需的线索。这些结果表明，任务对齐的智能体需要选择性使用环境指令，而不是全盘接受或拒绝。

Original abstract: Terminal agents are increasingly capable of executing complex, long-horizon tasks autonomously from a single user prompt. To do so, they must interpret instructions encountered in the environment (e.g., README files, code comments, stack traces) and determine their relevance to the task. This creates a fundamental challenge: relevant cues must be followed to complete a task, whereas irrelevant or misleading ones must be ignored. Existing benchmarks do not capture this ability. An agent may appear capable by blindly following all instructions, or appear robust by ignoring them altogether. We introduce TAB (Task Alignment Benchmark), a suite of 89 terminal tasks derived from Terminal-Bench 2.1. Each task is intentionally underspecified, with missing information provided as a necessary cue embedded in a natural environmental artifact, alongside a plausible but irrelevant distractor. Solving these tasks requires selectively using the cue while ignoring the distractor. Applying TAB to ten frontier agents reveals a systematic gap between task capability and task alignment. The strongest Terminal-Bench agent achieves high task completion but low task alignment on TAB. Evaluating six prompt-injection defenses further shows that suppressing distractor execution also suppresses the cues required for task completion. These results demonstrate that task-aligned agents require selective use of environmental instructions rather than blanket acceptance or rejection.

</details>


### [111] [PriorZero: Bridging Language Priors and World Models for Decision Making](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12289v1)
*Junyu Xiong,Yuan Pu,Jia Tang,Yazhe Niu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: PriorZero框架结合LLM先验与世界模型，通过MCTS实现规划，可迁移至coding agent中利用语言知识进行决策。

TL;DR: PriorZero通过解耦的推出-训练设计，将LLM先验注入世界模型规划中，有效解决了先验-动态不匹配问题，在文本冒险和网格世界任务中提升了探索效率和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法中，静态LLM知识无法适应长时域任务的复杂动态，固定策略限制探索多样性，端到端微调存在优化不稳定和信用分配问题，亟需一种能有效融合LLM先验与RL的方法。

Method: PriorZero提出解耦的推出-训练设计：推出时，仅在MCTS根节点注入LLM先验（根先验注入），引导搜索；训练时，交替优化世界模型（联合学习动态、策略、值）和LLM（利用世界模型的值估计提供信用分配信号）。

Result: 在Jericho文本冒险游戏和BabyAI指令遵循网格世界任务中，PriorZero一致提高了探索效率和渐近性能。

Conclusion: PriorZero建立了LLM赋能决策制定的统一框架，有效弥合了LLM先验与RL动态之间的差距，展示了在复杂任务中提升性能的潜力。

中文摘要：利用大型语言模型（LLM）丰富的世界知识来增强强化学习（RL）智能体，为实现通用智能提供了一条有希望的路径。然而，一个根本的先验-动态不匹配阻碍了现有方法：静态的LLM知识无法直接适应长时域任务的复杂转移动态。将LLM先验用作固定策略会限制探索多样性，因为先验对环境特定的动态视而不见；而端到端微调则面临优化不稳定性和信用分配问题。为了弥合这一差距，我们提出了PriorZero，一个统一的框架，通过解耦的推出-训练设计将LLM派生的概念先验整合到基于世界模型的规划中。在推出过程中，一种新颖的根先验注入机制仅在蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）的根节点处注入LLM先验，将搜索集中在语义上有希望的动作上，同时保留世界模型的深度前瞻能力。在训练过程中，PriorZero将世界模型学习与LLM适应解耦：世界模型在交互数据上持续精炼，以联合改进其动态、策略和值预测，然后利用其值估计为稳定的LLM微调提供细粒度的信用分配信号，通过交替优化实现。在多种基准测试上的实验，包括Jericho中的文本冒险游戏和BabyAI中的指令遵循网格世界任务，表明PriorZero一致地提高了探索效率和渐近性能，为LLM赋能的决策制定建立了一个有希望的框架。我们的代码可在https://github.com/opendilab/LightZero获取。

Original abstract: Leveraging the rich world knowledge of Large Language Models (LLMs) to enhance Reinforcement Learning (RL) agents offers a promising path toward general intelligence. However, a fundamental prior-dynamics mismatch hinders existing approaches: static LLM knowledge cannot directly adapt to the complex transition dynamics of long-horizon tasks. Using LLM priors as fixed policies limits exploration diversity, as the prior is blind to environment-specific dynamics; while end-to-end fine-tuning suffers from optimization instability and credit assignment issues. To bridge this gap, we propose PriorZero, a unified framework that integrates LLM-derived conceptual priors into world-model-based planning through a decoupled rollout-training design. During rollout, a novel root-prior injection mechanism incorporates LLM priors exclusively at the root node of Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS), focusing search on semantically promising actions while preserving the world model's deep lookahead capability. During training, PriorZero decouples world-model learning from LLM adaptation: the world model is continuously refined on interaction data to jointly improve its dynamics, policy, and value predictions, its value estimates are then leveraged to provide fine-grained credit assignment signals for stable LLM fine-tuning via alternating optimization. Experiments across diverse benchmarks, including text-based adventure games in Jericho and instruction-following gridworld tasks in BabyAI, demonstrate that PriorZero consistently improves both exploration efficiency and asymptotic performance, establishing a promising framework for LLM-empowered decision-making. Our code is available at https://github.com/opendilab/LightZero.

</details>

*Matthew Beddows,Aiden Durrant,Georgios Leontidis*

Original abstract: Accurate crop yield forecasting in commercial soft fruit production is constrained by the data available in typical commercial farm records, which lack the sensor networks, satellite imagery, and high-resolution meteorological inputs that most state-of-the-art approaches assume. We propose a structured LLM agent framework that performs post-hoc correction of existing model predictions, encoding agricultural domain knowledge across tools for phase detection, bias learning, and range validation. Evaluated on a proprietary strawberry yield dataset and a public USDA corn harvest dataset, agent refinement of XGBoost reduced MAE by 20% and MASE by 56% on strawberry, with consistent improvements across Moirai2 (MAE 24%, MASE 22%) and Random Forest (MAE 28%, MASE 66%) baselines. Using Llama 3.1 8B as the agent produced the strongest corrections across all configurations; LLaVA 13B showed inconsistent gains, highlighting sensitivity to the choice of refinement model.

### [113] [OGLS-SD: On-Policy Self-Distillation with Outcome-Guided Logit Steering for LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12400v2)
*Yuxiao Yang,Xiaoyun Wang,Weitong Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 基于结果的logit steering自蒸馏方法，可增强agent推理能力。

TL;DR: 提出OGLS-SD框架，通过对比成功和失败轨迹的教师逻辑分数来稳定在线自蒸馏，提升数学推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决OPSD中由于教师和学生响应模式不匹配导致的训练不稳定问题，以及自我反射响应带来的偏差。

Method: 利用可验证的结果奖励，对比成功和失败轨迹的教师逻辑分数，构建结果判别性的引导方向进行令牌级校准。

Result: 在数学推理基准上，OGLS-SD稳定了自蒸馏并提升了性能，优于标准OPSD和其他变体。

Conclusion: OGLS-SD通过结果引导的逻辑分数校准，有效缓解了OPSD的不稳定性，提高了推理能力。

中文摘要：我们研究了在线自蒸馏（OPSD），其中语言模型通过沿着自己的在线轨迹蒸馏特权教师分布来改进其推理能力。尽管有前景，但OPSD可能因教师和学生响应之间的模式不匹配而遭受训练不稳定性。自我反射的教师响应可能会引入反射引起的偏差和响应模板，这些模板会错误地校准令牌级监督，最终损害学生的推理能力。为了缓解这个问题，我们提出了OGLS-SD，一个结果引导的逻辑分数引导框架，该框架利用可验证的结果奖励来校准特权教师逻辑分数。具体地，OGLS-SD对比由成功和失败的在线轨迹诱导的教师逻辑分数，构建一个结果判别性的引导方向用于令牌级指导。在数学推理基准上的实验表明，OGLS-SD稳定了自蒸馏并提高了性能，优于标准OPSD和其他变体。

Original abstract: We study on-policy self-distillation (OPSD), where a language model improves its reasoning ability by distilling privileged teacher distributions along its own on-policy trajectories. Despite its promise, OPSD can suffer from training instability due to a pattern mismatch between teacher and student responses. Self-reflected teacher responses may introduce reflection-induced biases and response templates that miscalibrate token-level supervision, ultimately harming the student's reasoning ability. To mitigate this issue, we propose OGLS-SD, an outcome-guided logit-steering framework that leverages verifiable outcome rewards to calibrate privileged teacher logits. Specifically, OGLS-SD contrasts teacher logits induced by successful and failed on-policy trajectories, constructing an outcome-discriminative steering direction for token-level guidance. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that OGLS-SD stabilizes self-distillation and improves performance over standard OPSD and other variants.

Original abstract: Evaluation of foundation models often rely on aggregate scores from benchmarks that lack comprehensive coverage and metadata for a fine-grained evaluation. We introduce a framework for automated benchmark generation. Our framework generates evaluation problems grounded in reference material, such as textbooks, producing benchmarks with broad coverage, rich metadata, and robustness to contamination. The pipeline employs a multi-agent architecture for problem generation and a solution-graph-driven strategy that significantly improves the reliability of ground truth solutions. Using the framework, we generate three benchmarks in Machine Learning, Corporate Finance, and Personal Finance. Expert review finds a significantly lower ground-truth error rate than previous benchmarks such as MMLU and GSM8K. Evaluation of 12 commercial and open-source models shows that our benchmarks achieve near-uniform competency coverage and surface performance differences across models that existing benchmarks fail to capture. We will open-source the framework and our curated benchmarks soon.
