### [115] [Predicting Decisions of AI Agents from Limited Interaction through Text-Tabular Modeling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12411v1)
*Eilam Shapira,Moshe Tennenholtz,Roi Reichart*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 从有限交互预测AI agent决策，提供agent建模与行为分析工具。

TL;DR: 本文提出目标自适应文本-表格预测方法，利用LLM隐藏状态作为观察者特征，在谈判游戏中有效预测不熟悉对手的决策，显著提升AUC并降低误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI代理在与不熟悉的对手进行自然语言谈判时，对手的LLM、提示、控制逻辑等细节未知，且决策有金钱后果，因此需要从少量交互中预测对手的下一步决策。

Method: 在受控博弈中构建目标自适应文本-表格预测模型，基于表格基础模型结合游戏状态特征和LLM文本表示，并引入LLM-as-Observer编码器（小冻结LLM读取决策时状态和对话，用其隐藏状态作为决策导向特征），利用目标代理之前的K个游戏作为适应示例。

Result: 在13个前沿LLM代理上训练、91个留出代理上测试，完整模型优于直接LLM预测提示和游戏+文本特征基线；在K=16时，Observer特征在响应预测AUC上提升约4点，在讨价还价报价预测误差上降低14%。

Conclusion: 将对手预测表述为目标自适应文本-表格任务能够实现有效适应，并且隐藏的LLM表示能暴露直接提示无法获得的决策相关信号。

中文摘要：AI代理以自然语言与不熟悉的对手进行谈判和交易：例如，一个买家机器人面对未知的卖家，或一个采购助理与供应商谈判。在这些交互中，对手的大语言模型（LLM）、提示词、控制逻辑和基于规则的备选方案都是隐藏的，而每个决策都可能带来金钱上的后果。我们探究一个代理是否能够通过少量交互预测不熟悉对手的下一步决策。为了避免真实世界中的日志混淆，我们在受控讨价还价和谈判游戏中研究这一问题，并将其表述为目标自适应的文本-表格预测：每个决策点是一个表格行，结合了结构化的游戏状态、报价历史和对话，同时将同一目标代理（即被建模的对手）之前的K个游戏作为标记的适应示例提供在提示中。我们的模型基于一个表格基础模型，该模型使用游戏状态特征和基于LLM的文本表示来表示行，并添加了LLM作为观察者作为额外表示：一个小的冻结LLM读取决策时的状态和对话；它的答案被丢弃，其隐藏状态成为决策导向的特征，使LLM成为编码器而不是直接的少样本预测器。在13个前沿LLM代理上训练，并在91个留出的结构化代理上测试，完整模型优于直接使用LLM作为预测器的提示和游戏+文本特征基线。在这个表格模型中，观察者特征对其他特征方案有额外贡献：在K=16时，它们在两个任务上将响应预测AUC提高了约4点，并将讨价还价报价预测误差降低了14%。这些结果表明，将对手预测表述为目标自适应的文本-表格任务能够实现有效的适应，并且隐藏的LLM表示暴露了直接提示无法展现的决策相关信号。

Original abstract: AI agents negotiate and transact in natural language with unfamiliar counterparts: a buyer bot facing an unknown seller, or a procurement assistant negotiating with a supplier. In such interactions, the counterpart's LLM, prompts, control logic, and rule-based fallbacks are hidden, while each decision can have monetary consequences. We ask whether an agent can predict an unfamiliar counterpart's next decision from a few interactions. To avoid real-world logging confounds, we study this problem in controlled bargaining and negotiation games, formulating it as target-adaptive text-tabular prediction: each decision point is a table row combining structured game state, offer history, and dialogue, while $K$ previous games of the same target agent, i.e., the counterpart being modeled, are provided in the prompt as labeled adaptation examples. Our model is built on a tabular foundation model that represents rows using game-state features and LLM-based text representations, and adds LLM-as-Observer as an additional representation: a small frozen LLM reads the decision-time state and dialogue; its answer is discarded, and its hidden state becomes a decision-oriented feature, making the LLM an encoder rather than a direct few-shot predictor. Training on 13 frontier-LLM agents and testing on 91 held-out scaffolded agents, the full model outperforms direct LLM-as-Predictor prompting and game+text features baselines. Within this tabular model, Observer features contribute beyond the other feature schemes: at $K=16$, they improve response-prediction AUC by about 4 points across both tasks and reduce bargaining offer-prediction error by 14%. These results show that formulating counterpart prediction as a target-adaptive text-tabular task enables effective adaptation, and that hidden LLM representations expose decision-relevant signals that direct prompting does not surface.

</details>


### [116] [Solve the Loop: Attractor Models for Language and Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12466v1)
*Jacob Fein-Ashley,Paria Rashidinejad*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 吸引子模型实现可内化迭代推理，可迁移至agent推理模块。

TL;DR: 提出吸引子模型，通过隐式微分求解不动点实现稳定高效的迭代精炼，在语言建模和推理上超越现有模型，并展现平衡内化现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有循环Transformer训练不稳定、成本高、深度固定，需要一种可扩展的迭代精炼方法。

Method: 骨干模块提出输出嵌入，吸引子模块通过求解不动点精炼，梯度由隐式微分获得，训练内存不随深度增加，迭代次数自适应。

Result: 在语言建模上困惑度降低46.6%，准确率提升19.7%，770M模型优于1.3B标准Transformer；推理任务上小模型取得高准确率，超越前沿模型；发现平衡内化现象。

Conclusion: 吸引子模型通过将循环内化为计算，使迭代精炼变得可扩展。

中文摘要：循环Transformer通过迭代精炼潜在表示，为纯前馈计算提供了一种有前景的替代方案，改善了语言建模和推理。然而，循环架构在训练上仍然不稳定，优化和部署成本高，并且局限于小的固定循环深度。我们引入了吸引子模型（Attractor Models），其中骨干模块首先提出输出嵌入，然后吸引子模块通过求解不动点来精炼它们，梯度通过隐式微分获得。因此，训练内存在有效深度上保持恒定，并且迭代次数通过收敛自适应地选择。实验上，吸引子模型在两个场景中优于现有模型：大规模语言模型预训练和基于小模型的推理。在语言建模中，吸引子模型在不同规模上实现了对标准Transformer和稳定循环模型的帕累托改进，困惑度最多降低46.6%，下游准确率最多提升19.7%，同时降低了训练成本。值得注意的是，一个770M参数的吸引子模型在训练数据减半的情况下优于一个1.3B参数的Transformer。在具有挑战性的推理任务上，我们展示了仅2700万参数和大约1000个例子的模型在Sudoku-Extreme上达到了91.4%的准确率，在Maze-Hard上达到了93.1%，其扩展性优于完全失败的Claude和GPT o3等前沿模型，而专门的递归推理器在更大规模上崩溃。最后，我们展示了吸引子模型表现出一种新现象，我们称之为平衡内化：固定点训练使模型的初始输出嵌入接近平衡，从而允许在推理时移除求解器而性能几乎没有下降。总之，这些结果表明，吸引子模型通过将循环转变为模型可以学习内化的计算，使得迭代精炼变得可扩展。

Original abstract: Looped Transformers offer a promising alternative to purely feed-forward computation by iteratively refining latent representations, improving language modeling and reasoning. Yet recurrent architectures remain unstable to train, costly to optimize and deploy, and constrained to small, fixed recurrence depths. We introduce Attractor Models, in which a backbone module first proposes output embeddings, then an attractor module refines them by solving for the fixed point, with gradients obtained through implicit differentiation. Thus, training memory remains constant in effective depth, and iterations are chosen adaptively by convergence. Empirically, Attractor Models outperform existing models across two regimes, large-scale language-model pretraining and reasoning with tiny models. In language modeling, Attractor Models deliver a Pareto improvement over standard Transformers and stable looped models across sizes, improving perplexity by up to 46.6% and downstream accuracy by up to 19.7% while reducing training cost. Notably, a 770M Attractor Model outperforms a 1.3B Transformer trained on twice as many tokens. On challenging reasoning tasks, we show that our model with only 27M parameters and approximately 1000 examples achieves 91.4% accuracy on Sudoku-Extreme and 93.1% on Maze-Hard, scaling favorably where frontier models like Claude and GPT o3, fail completely, and specialized recursive reasoners collapse at larger sizes. Lastly, we show that Attractor Models exhibit a novel phenomenon, which we call equilibrium internalization: fixed-point training places the model's initial output embedding near equilibrium, allowing the solver to be removed at inference time with little degradation. Together, these results suggest that Attractor Models make iterative refinement scalable by turning recurrence into a computation the model can learn to internalize.

</details>


### [117] [Learning, Fast and Slow: Towards LLMs That Adapt Continually](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12484v2)
*Rishabh Tiwari,Kusha Sareen,Lakshya A Agrawal,Joseph E. Gonzalez,Matei Zaharia,Kurt Keutzer,Inderjit S Dhillon,Rishabh Agarwal,Devvrit Khatri*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 快速慢速学习框架，用于LLM持续适应，可启发agent的适应性学习

TL;DR: 提出快慢训练（FST）框架，将模型参数作为慢权重、优化上下文作为快权重，在推理任务上比RL样本效率高3倍，且减少灾难性遗忘和保持可塑性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 参数更新导致灾难性遗忘和可塑性丧失，而上下文学习性能有限；人类在不同时间尺度学习，因此需要结合两者优势。

Method: 引入快慢学习框架，模型参数作为慢权重，优化上下文作为快权重，从文本反馈中学习任务特定信息。

Result: FST比RL样本效率高3倍，性能渐近线更高；模型KL散度降低70%，减少遗忘；持续学习场景中能继续获取新任务而RL停滞。

Conclusion: 快慢训练在样本效率、性能、遗忘和持续学习方面优于仅参数更新方法。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）通过更新其参数（例如，通过强化学习）来针对下游任务进行训练。然而，更新参数迫使它们吸收特定任务的信息，这可能导致灾难性遗忘和可塑性丧失。相比之下，使用固定LLM参数的上下文学习可以廉价且快速地适应特定任务的要求（例如，提示优化），但其本身通常无法达到通过更新LLM参数所能获得的性能提升。没有充分的理由将学习限制在上下文中或权重中。此外，人类也可能在不同的时间尺度上学习（例如，系统1与系统2）。为此，我们为LLM引入了一个快慢学习框架，其中模型参数作为“慢”权重，优化后的上下文作为“快”权重。这些快“权重”可以从文本反馈中学习，吸收特定任务的信息，同时允许慢权重保持更接近基础模型并维持通用推理行为。快慢训练（FST）在推理任务上比仅慢学习（RL）样本效率高达3倍，同时始终达到更高的性能渐近线。此外，FST训练的模型保持更接近基础LLM（KL散度降低高达70%），导致比RL训练更少的灾难性遗忘。这种漂移的减少也保持了可塑性：在一个任务上训练后，FST训练的模型比仅参数训练的模型更有效地适应后续任务。在持续学习场景中，任务领域动态变化，FST继续获取每个新任务，而仅参数RL停滞不前。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are trained for downstream tasks by updating their parameters (e.g., via RL). However, updating parameters forces them to absorb task-specific information, which can result in catastrophic forgetting and loss of plasticity. In contrast, in-context learning with fixed LLM parameters can cheaply and rapidly adapt to task-specific requirements (e.g., prompt optimization), but cannot by itself typically match the performance gains available through updating LLM parameters. There is no good reason for restricting learning to being in-context or in-weights. Moreover, humans also likely learn at different time scales (e.g., System 1 vs 2). To this end, we introduce a fast-slow learning framework for LLMs, with model parameters as "slow" weights and optimized context as "fast" weights. These fast "weights" can learn from textual feedback to absorb the task-specific information, while allowing slow weights to stay closer to the base model and persist general reasoning behaviors. Fast-Slow Training (FST) is up to 3x more sample-efficient than only slow learning (RL) across reasoning tasks, while consistently reaching a higher performance asymptote. Moreover, FST-trained models remain closer to the base LLM (up to 70% less KL divergence), resulting in less catastrophic forgetting than RL-training. This reduced drift also preserves plasticity: after training on one task, FST trained models adapt more effectively to a subsequent task than parameter-only trained models. In continual learning scenarios, where task domains change on the fly, FST continues to acquire each new task while parameter-only RL stalls.

</details>


### [118] [Multi-Rollout On-Policy Distillation via Peer Successes and Failures](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12652v2)
*Weichen Yu,Xiaomin Li,Yizhou Zhao,Xiaoze Liu,Ruowang Zhang,Haixin Wang,Yinyi Luo,Chen Henry Wu,Gaurav Mittal,Matt Fredrikson,Yu Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 多rollout在线蒸馏，利用成功失败信号，可迁移至agent训练

TL;DR: 提出MOPD，利用学生的多展开试错行为构建同伴条件教师信号，通过在成功和失败展开上条件化提供更密集监督，实验显示优于标准方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于策略的蒸馏方法独立处理每个展开，忽略了同一提示下其他尝试的信息，导致监督信号稀疏且不够信息丰富。

Method: 引入多展开基于策略的蒸馏（MOPD），使用学生的局部展开组构建同伴条件教师信号，包括正向同伴模仿和对比性成功-失败条件两种上下文。

Result: 在竞争性编程、数学推理、科学问答和工具使用基准上，MOPD一致优于标准的基于策略基线；教师信号分析显示混合成功-失败上下文能更好对齐验证器奖励。

Conclusion: 有效的基于策略蒸馏应利用学生的多展开试错行为，而不是将展开视为孤立样本；同伴条件蒸馏能提供更密集、实例自适应的监督。

中文摘要：大型语言模型通常使用稀疏的验证器奖励进行后训练，这种奖励指示采样的轨迹是否成功，但对于推理成功或失败的位置提供的指导有限。基于策略的蒸馏（OPD）通过在学生生成的轨迹上训练提供更密集的令牌级监督，然而现有方法通常独立地蒸馏每个展开，并忽略针对同一提示采样的其他尝试。我们引入了多展开基于策略的蒸馏（MOPD），这是一种同伴条件蒸馏框架，利用学生的局部展开组构建更具信息量的教师信号。MOPD 将教师条件建立在成功和失败的同伴展开上：成功为有效的推理模式提供正面证据，而失败则为需要避免的合情错误提供结构化的负面证据。我们研究了两种同伴上下文构建：正向同伴模仿和对比性成功-失败条件。在竞争性编程、数学推理、科学问答和工具使用基准上的实验表明，MOPD 持续优于标准的基于策略基线。进一步的教师信号分析显示，混合成功-失败上下文能更好地使教师分数与验证器奖励对齐，表明改进来自于更忠实、实例自适应的监督。这些结果表明，有效的基于策略蒸馏应利用学生的多展开试错行为，而不是将展开视为孤立样本。

Original abstract: Large language models are often post-trained with sparse verifier rewards, which indicate whether a sampled trajectory succeeds but provide limited guidance about where reasoning succeeds or fails. On-policy distillation (OPD) offers denser token-level supervision by training on student-generated trajectories, yet existing methods typically distill each rollout independently and ignore the other attempts sampled for the same prompt. We introduce Multi-Rollout On-Policy Distillation (MOPD), a peer-conditioned distillation framework that uses the student's local rollout group to construct more informative teacher signals. MOPD conditions the teacher on both successful and failed peer rollouts: successes provide positive evidence for valid reasoning patterns, while failures provide structured negative evidence about plausible mistakes to avoid. We study two peer-context constructions: positive peer imitation and contrastive success-failure conditioning. Experiments on competitive programming, mathematical reasoning, scientific question answering, and tool-use benchmarks show that MOPD consistently improves over standard on-policy baselines. Further teacher-signal analysis shows that mixed success-failure contexts better align teacher scores with verifier rewards, indicating that the gains arise from more faithful, instance-adaptive supervision. These results indicate that effective on-policy distillation should exploit the student's multi-rollout trial-and-error behavior rather than treating rollouts as isolated samples.

</details>


### [119] [Plan Before You Trade: Inference-Time Optimization for RL Trading Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12653v1)
*Eun Go,Rohan Deb,Arindam Banerjee*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 交易agent的推理时优化框架，可迁移至coding agent的规划优化

TL;DR: FPILOT是一个在推理时利用价格预测优化交易策略的插件框架，无需重新训练即可提升多种强化学习策略的回报和风险调整指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习投资组合管理策略在推理时无法利用价格预测，导致策略静态且性能受限。

Method: 提出FPILOT框架，基于模型预测控制思想，在推理时使用预测价格轨迹构建想象回报目标，并优化策略参数，再执行一步交易。

Result: 在TradeMaster DJ30基准上，FPILOT在五种策略上一致提升总回报和夏普、索提诺、卡尔玛比率，随机策略提升更显著，且收益随预测质量提升。

Conclusion: FPILOT能有效利用价格预测改进交易策略，性能与预测质量正相关，有望随金融预测进步进一步提升。

中文摘要：用于投资组合管理的强化学习智能体通常作为静态策略进行训练和部署，在推理时没有使用价格预测的机制。我们提出FPILOT（金融插件推理时学习优化交易），这是一个受模型预测控制（MPC）启发的插件式推理时优化框架。我们的关键结构性洞察是，未来价格大多不依赖于单个智能体的投资组合分配，因此合适的预测模型可以生成多步价格轨迹，而无需像典型强化学习那样进行迭代的、依赖于动作的展开。在每个决策步骤，我们使用预测器的预测价格轨迹构建基于分配的想象回报目标，并在执行一步交易之前在推理时优化策略。我们的框架与任何预训练智能体兼容，并且无需重新训练即可使策略适应预测器的预测。在TradeMaster DJ30基准测试上，跨五种策略学习算法评估，FPILOT在总回报和基于回报的风险调整指标（夏普比率、索提诺比率、卡尔玛比率）上产生一致的改进，其中随机策略比确定性策略受益更多。此外，使用校准质量水平的合成预测，我们显示收益随预测器质量一致提高，表明我们的性能将随着金融预测的进步而提升。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning agents for portfolio management are typically trained and deployed as static policies, with no mechanism for using price forecasts at inference time. We propose $\text{FPILOT}$ (**Fin**ancial **P**lugin **I**nference-time **L**earning for **O**ptimal **T**rading), a plugin inference-time optimization framework inspired by Model Predictive Control (MPC). Our key structural insight is that future prices mostly do not depend on one agent's portfolio allocation, so a suitable predictive model can produce a multi-step price trajectory without iterative action-conditioned rollouts as in typical reinforcement learning. At each decision step, we use the forecaster's predicted price trajectory to construct an allocation-based imagined return objective, and optimize the policy at inference-time before executing one step of the trade. Our framework is compatible with any pre-trained agent and adapts the policy to the forecaster's predictions without any retraining. Evaluated across five policy learning algorithms on the TradeMaster DJ30 benchmark, $\text{FPILOT}$ produces consistent improvements in total return and return-based risk-adjusted metrics (Sharpe, Sortino, Calmar), with stochastic policies benefiting more than deterministic ones. Further, using synthetic forecasts at calibrated quality levels, we show that gains consistently improve with forecaster quality, suggesting that our performance will improve based on advances in financial forecasting.

### [120] [ODRPO: Ordinal Decompositions of Discrete Rewards for Robust Policy Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12667v2)
*Nirmal Patel,Fei Wang,Inderjit S. Dhillon*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 离散奖励的序数分解，改进RL稳定性，可迁移至agent奖励设计

TL;DR: ODRPO通过将离散奖励分解为有序二元指标来隔离自动评分器的噪声，无需额外计算即可提升RLAIF中LLM对齐的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLAIF中自动评分器的随机性会破坏梯度估计，导致学习信号退化；而增加采样成本高，需更鲁棒的框架。

Method: 将离散奖励分解为一系列有序二元指标（成功阈值），独立计算并累计各阈值的优势，避免异常值影响全局更新，形成方差感知学习课程。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-7B和Qwen3-4B上，ODRPO相比GRPO等基线在FACTS-grounding-v2和Alpaca-Evals上分别提升14.8%和7.5%，且无额外计算开销。

Conclusion: ODRPO提供了一种可扩展且稳健的RLAIF对齐框架，通过结构降噪实现高效优化，理论分析保证稳定性。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）的对齐利用来自AI反馈的强化学习（RLAIF）处理非可验证领域，如长形式问答和开放式指令跟随。这些领域通常依赖基于LLM的自动评分器提供细粒度的多级离散奖励（例如1-10分制），由于提示敏感性和采样随机性，这些奖励本质上是随机的。我们实证验证了自动评分器的随机性，这种随机性可能传播并破坏标准优势估计器（如GRPO和MaxRL），因为噪声奖励样本可能会扭曲归一化统计量并降低全局学习信号。实验表明，采样更多奖励并采用多数投票可能减少噪声并提升性能，但这种方法计算开销大。为解决这一瓶颈，我们提出了面向鲁棒策略优化的有序分解（ODRPO）框架，通过将离散奖励分解为一系列有序二元指标，在结构上隔离评估噪声。通过独立计算并累计这些逐步具有挑战性的成功阈值上的优势，ODRPO防止了异常评估破坏全局更新，同时建立了隐式的方差感知学习课程。实验表明，ODRPO在Qwen2.5-7B和Qwen3-4B模型上取得了稳健的性能，在FACTS-grounding-v2和Alpaca-Evals上分别相比基线实现了高达14.8%和7.5%的相对改进。关键的是，这些增益是在可忽略的训练时间开销下实现的，因为与标准估计器相比，ODRPO每步无需额外计算。在理论分析支持其优化稳定性的基础上，ODRPO为在现代RLAIF的噪声离散评估环境中对齐模型提供了一个可扩展且稳健的框架。

Original abstract: The alignment of Large Language Models (LLMs) utilizes Reinforcement Learning from AI Feedback (RLAIF) for non-verifiable domains such as long-form question answering and open-ended instruction following. These domains often rely on LLM based auto-raters to provide granular, multi-tier discrete rewards (e.g., 1-10 rubrics) that are inherently stochastic due to prompt sensitivity and sampling randomness. We empirically verify the stochasticity of auto-raters that can propagate and corrupt standard advantage estimators like GRPO and MaxRL, as a noisy reward samples can skew normalization statistics and degrade the global learning signal. Empirically, sampling more rewards and taking majority voting may reduce the noise and improve performance, but this approach is computationally expensive. To address this bottleneck, we introduce $\textbf{O}$rdinal $\textbf{D}$ecomposition for $\textbf{R}$obust $\textbf{P}$olicy $\textbf{O}$ptimization ($\textbf{ODRPO}$), a framework that structurally isolates evaluation noise by decomposing discrete rewards into a sequence of ordinal binary indicators. By independently computing and accumulating advantages across these progressively challenging success thresholds, ODRPO prevents outlier evaluations from corrupting the global update while establishing an implicit, variance-aware learning curriculum. Empirically, ODRPO achieves robust performance on Qwen2.5-7B and Qwen3-4B models, outperforming baselines with relative improvements of upto 14.8% on FACTS-grounding-v2 and 7.5% on Alpaca-Evals. Critically, these gains are achieved with negligible training-time overhead, as ODRPO requires no additional compute per step compared to standard estimators. Supported by theoretical analysis confirming its optimization stability, ODRPO provides a scalable and robust framework for aligning models within the noisy, discrete evaluation landscape of modern RLAIF.

</details>

### [121] [Ensuring Logic in the Fog: Sound POMDP Synthesis with LTL Objectives](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12581v1)
*Can Zhou,Yulong Gao,Pian Yu*

中文摘要：合成能夠在不確定環境中導航並遵守複雜時間約束的自主代理仍然是一個基本挑戰。雖然線性時序邏輯（LTL）為指定此類任務提供了嚴謹的語言，但在部分可觀測馬可夫決策過程中定性驗證LTL滿足性的固有不可判定性使得定量合成變得困難，尤其是在為近似求解器設計可靠獎勵信號時。在本文中，我們通過一種新穎且健全的獎勵塑造機制來填補這一空白，該機制動態生成基於認證LTL滿足性的信念相關獎勵。通過將此機制整合到增強的蒙特卡羅規劃框架中，我們使代理能夠在部分可觀測性的“迷霧”中導航，其搜索過程專注於最大化可驗證的成功。我們的實驗表明，這種方法不僅在現有求解器失敗的場景中表現出色，而且在多個基準領域中保持有效性和可擴展性。

Original abstract: Synthesising autonomous agents that can navigate uncertain environments while adhering to complex temporal constraints remains a fundamental challenge. While Linear Temporal Logic (LTL) provides a rigorous language for specifying such tasks, the inherent undecidability of qualitatively verifying LTL satisfaction in partially observable Markov decision processes renders quantitative synthesis difficult, especially when designing reliable reward signals for approximate solvers. In this paper, we bridge this gap with a novel, sound reward-shaping mechanism that dynamically generates belief-dependent rewards grounded in certified LTL satisfaction. By integrating this mechanism into an enhanced Monte Carlo Planning framework, we empower agents to navigate the `fog' of partial observability with a search process focused on maximising verifiable success. Our experiments demonstrate that this approach not only thrives in scenarios where existing solvers fail but also maintains effectiveness and scalability across diverse benchmark domains.

### [122] [Large Language Models for Agentic NetOps and AIOps: Architectures, Evaluation, and Safety](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12729v2)
*Muhammad Bilal,Jon Crowcroft,Ruizhi Wang,Xiaolong Xu,Schahram Dustdar*

Main category: cs.NI

Selection reason: LLM for NetOps/AIOps agent综述，涉及架构、评估、安全，可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: 大型语言模型在NetOps和AIOps中的应用依赖于围绕模型的机制（如权限、检查、回滚）而非模型本身来保证可靠性，评估应从静态问答转向工作流为中心的评估，并需关注安全、隐私和治理风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型正被用于网络运维和AI运维，但它们的直接应用存在可靠性风险，需要系统化的框架来保证操作的可靠性、可审计性和安全性。

Method: 通过组织文献，围绕自主性层级、工具范围、证据踪迹和保证契约四个维度进行分析，提出工作流为中心的评估方法，包括踪迹质量、有界工具使用、安全提议生成、沙盒回放和回滚感知金丝雀试验。

Result: 识别出一致模式：运维可靠性不依赖模型本身而依赖周围机制；静态问答评估不足；代理靠近控制面时安全、隐私和治理风险加剧。

Conclusion: 智能NetOps和AIOps的进展取决于将自主性视为受限的运维控制问题，确保输出可靠、可审计且可安全部署。

中文摘要：大型语言模型越来越多地被用于支持网络运维（NetOps）和人工智能驱动的IT运维（AIOps），包括事件调查、根因分析、配置合成以及有限的自我修复。在NetOps和AIOps中，这种转变正在改变任务的管理方式。基于代理的运维作为工作流运行，从收集证据到采取行动，遵循权限、策略和检查，并在必要时提供回滚选项。这一点至关重要，因为运维决策可能会产生即时影响。为了使论证具体化，我们围绕自主性层级、工具范围、证据踪迹和保证契约来组织相关文献。这些契约定义了代理可以观察、提议和执行的内容。它们还定义了在任何操作允许之前必须通过的检查。在遥测查询推荐、诊断、根因分析、配置合成、变更规划和有限的自我修复等工作中出现了一致的模式。运维可靠性并非主要来自模型本身，而是依赖于模型周围的机制。我们还认为，评估应该超越静态问答。基于代理的NetOps和AIOps系统需要以工作流为中心的评估，包括踪迹质量、有界工具使用、安全的提议生成、沙盒环境中的回放，以及具有回滚感知评分的金丝雀试验。如果没有这些措施，系统可能看似鲁棒，但实际上仍然脆弱。最后，我们审视了当代理接近运维控制面时变得尖锐的安全、隐私和治理风险。综上所述，本调查得出结论：智能NetOps和AIOps的进展将取决于将自主性视为一个受限的运维控制问题，其输出必须可靠、可审计且可安全部署。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly being used to support network operations (NetOps) and artificial intelligence for IT operations (AIOps), including incident investigation, root-cause analysis, configuration synthesis, and limited self-healing. In both NetOps and AIOps, this shift is changing how tasks are managed. Agent-based operations work as workflows, from gathering evidence to taking action, following permissions, policies, and checks, and providing rollback options when necessary. This is crucial because operational decisions can have instant impacts. To make the argument concrete, we organise the relevant literature around the hierarchy of autonomy, tool scope, evidence traces, and assurance contracts. These contracts define what an agent may observe, propose, and execute. They also define the checks that must pass before any action is allowed. A consistent pattern appears across work on telemetry query recommendation, diagnosis, root-cause analysis, configuration synthesis, change planning, and limited self-healing. Operational reliability does not come chiefly from the model itself. It depends on the machinery around the model. We also argue that evaluation should go beyond static question answering. Agentic NetOps and AIOps systems require workflow-centred evaluation, including trace quality, bounded tool use, safe proposal generation, replay in sandboxed environments, and canary trials with rollback-aware scoring. Without these measures, a system may appear robust yet remain too fragile. Finally, we examine security, privacy, and governance risks that become acute when agents sit close to operational control surfaces. Taken together, the survey concludes that progress in intelligent NetOps and AIOps will depend on treating autonomy as a constrained operational control problem, whose outputs must be reliable, auditable, and securely deployable.

</details>

### [123] [EvoNav: Evolutionary Reward Function Design for Robot Navigation with Large Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11859v1)
*Zhikai Zhao,Chuanbo Hua,Federico Berto,Zihan Ma,Kanghoon Lee,Jiachen Li,Jinkyoo Park*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 基于LLM的进化奖励函数设计用于机器人导航，通用奖励优化方法可迁移到代码优化agent

TL;DR: 提出EvoNav，利用LLM自动设计机器人导航奖励函数，并通过渐进式三阶段评估实现高效探索，生成更优策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手工设计的奖励函数需要大量领域知识且难以调整，导致策略次优。

Method: EvoNav使用LLM生成候选奖励函数，并通过渐进的三阶段（分析代理、轻量级rollout、完整训练）评估进行筛选，以降低计算成本。

Result: 实验表明EvoNav产生的导航策略优于手工设计的RL奖励和现有最先进的奖励设计方法。

Conclusion: EvoNav通过自动化奖励函数设计，有效提升了机器人导航策略的性能。

中文摘要：机器人导航是一项关键任务，应用于动态人类环境中的社交机器人。虽然强化学习（RL）对此问题显示出巨大潜力，但策略质量对奖励函数的规范高度敏感。手工设计的奖励需要大量的领域专业知识，并嵌入难以审计或适应的归纳偏差，限制了其有效性并导致次优性能。在本文中，我们提出EvoNav，一种通过大型语言模型（LLM）自动设计机器人导航奖励函数的进化框架。为了克服成本高昂的策略训练，EvoNav通过渐进的三阶段预热-提升过程评估LLM的每个候选提议。EvoNav从使用低成本替代（如小数据集和分析规则）的分析代理开始，逐步过渡到轻量级rollout，最后到完整的策略训练，从而在有效反馈下实现计算高效的探索。实验结果表明，EvoNav比手工设计的RL奖励和最先进的奖励设计方法产生更有效的导航策略。

Original abstract: Robot navigation is a crucial task with applications to social robots in dynamic human environments. While Reinforcement Learning (RL) has shown great promise for this problem, the policy quality is highly sensitive to the specification of reward functions. Hand-crafted rewards require substantial domain expertise and embed inductive biases that are difficult to audit or adapt, limiting their effectiveness and leading to suboptimal performance. In this paper, we propose EvoNav, an evolutionary framework that automates the design of robot navigation reward functions via large language models (LLMs). To overcome prohibitively costly policy training, EvoNav evaluates each candidate proposal from the LLM via a progressive three-stage warm-up-boost procedure. EvoNav advances from analytical proxies with low-cost surrogates, such as small datasets and analytic rules, to lightweight rollouts and, finally, to full policy training, enabling computationally efficient exploration under effective feedback. Experiment results show that EvoNav produces more effective navigation policies than manually designed RL rewards and state-of-the-art reward design methods.

</details>


### [124] [TMRL: Diffusion Timestep-Modulated Pretraining Enables Exploration for Efficient Policy Finetuning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12236v1)
*Matthew M. Hong,Jesse Zhang,Anusha Nagabandi,Abhishek Gupta*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 扩散时序调制预训练用于机器人策略微调，通过控制探索-利用平衡提升效率，其方法可迁移至agent自我改进与探索策略。

TL;DR: 提出CSP预训练和TMRL微调框架，通过扩散噪声和动态时间步调制，提升机器人策略微调的探索效率和样本效率，实现快速真实世界微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决BC预训练导致动作分布狭窄，限制RL微调中探索的问题。

Method: 预训练时注入扩散噪声（CSP），微调时动态调节扩散时间步（TMRL）。

Result: 提高RL微调样本效率，在不到一小时内成功完成真实世界复杂操作任务微调。

Conclusion: 提出统一框架，有效桥接BC预训练和RL微调，提升探索能力。

中文摘要：使用强化学习（RL）微调预训练的机器人策略通常会继承通过行为克隆（BC）预训练引入的瓶颈，即产生狭窄的动作分布，缺乏下游探索所需的覆盖范围。我们提出了一个统一框架，通过桥接BC预训练和RL微调，实现了探索，从而能够高效地进行机器人策略微调。我们的预训练方法，上下文平滑预训练（CSP），将正向扩散噪声注入策略输入，在精确模仿和广泛动作覆盖之间创建了一个连续体。然后，我们通过时间步调制强化学习（TMRL）微调预训练策略，该方法训练代理在微调期间通过调制扩散时间步动态调整这种条件设置，从而实现对探索的显式控制。与任意策略输入无缝集成，例如状态、3D点云或基于图像的VLA策略，我们表明TMRL提高了RL微调样本效率。值得注意的是，TMRL使得在不到一小时内对复杂操作任务进行成功的真实世界微调成为可能。视频和代码可在https://weirdlabuw.github.io/tmrl/获取。

Original abstract: Fine-tuning pre-trained robot policies with reinforcement learning (RL) often inherits the bottlenecks introduced by pre-training with behavioral cloning (BC), which produces narrow action distributions that lack the coverage necessary for downstream exploration. We present a unified framework that enables the exploration necessary to enable efficient robot policy finetuning by bridging BC pre-training and RL fine-tuning. Our pre-training method, Context-Smoothed Pre-training (CSP), injects forward-diffusion noise into policy inputs, creating a continuum between precise imitation and broad action coverage. We then fine-tune pre-trained policies via Timestep-Modulated Reinforcement Learning (TMRL), which trains the agent to dynamically adjust this conditioning during fine-tuning by modulating the diffusion timestep, granting explicit control over exploration. Integrating seamlessly with arbitrary policy inputs, e.g., states, 3D point clouds, or image-based VLA policies, we show that TMRL improves RL fine-tuning sample efficiency. Notably, TMRL enables successful real-world fine-tuning on complex manipulation tasks in under one hour. Videos and code available at https://weirdlabuw.github.io/tmrl/.

</details>

### [125] [Options, Not Clicks: Lattice Refinement for Consent-Driven MCP Authorization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11360v1)
*Ying Li,Yanju Chen,Peiran Wang,Issac Khabra,Faysal Hossain Shezan,Yu Feng,Yuan Tian*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Conleash是一种客户端中间件，通过风险晶格和策略引擎实现边界作用域授权，在984个真实轨迹上达到98.2%准确率，用户研究显示其优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法（宽泛的始终允许或基于LLM的决策）无法处理危险调用参数并导致同意疲劳，需要更细粒度的用户同意机制。

Method: 提出Conleash客户端中间件，包含风险晶格（自动允许安全调用并升级风险）、策略引擎（用户定义不变量）和细化循环（将用户决策转为可重用规则）。

Result: 在984个真实轨迹上准确率98.2%，捕获99.4%升级，开销8.2ms；用户研究（N=16）中参与者显著偏好Conleash，信任度更高且提示更少。

Conclusion: Conleash通过边界作用域授权有效提升了工具调用的安全性和用户体验，未来可进一步优化策略生成和扩展应用场景。

中文摘要：随着模型上下文协议（Model Context Protocol）的广泛采用，通过有意义的用户同意来保护工具调用已成为一项关键挑战，因为现有方法——宽泛的始终允许开关或基于LLM的不透明决策——未能考虑危险的调用参数，并且常常导致同意疲劳。在这项工作中，我们提出了Conleash，一种客户端中间件，通过利用风险晶格自动允许已知边界内的安全调用同时升级风险、一个用于用户定义不变量的策略引擎，以及一个将用户决策转换为可重用规则的细化循环，来强制实施边界作用域授权。在984个真实世界轨迹上的评估中，Conleash实现了98.2%的准确率，捕获了99.4%的升级情况，并且策略验证仅增加了8.2毫秒的开销；此外，在一项N=16的用户研究中，参与者显著更偏好Conleash的作用域权限而非传统方法，理由是更高的信任度和更少的提示。

Original abstract: As Model Context Protocol adoption grows, securing tool invocations via meaningful user consent has become a critical challenge, as existing methods, broad always allow toggles or opaque LLM-based decisions, fail to account for dangerous call arguments and often lead to consent fatigue. In this work, we present Conleash, a client-side middleware that enforces boundary-scoped authorization by utilizing a risk lattice to auto-permit safe calls within known boundaries while escalating risks, a policy engine for user-defined invariants, and a refinement loop that converts user decisions into reusable rules. Evaluated on 984 real-world traces, Conleash achieved 98.2% accuracy, caught 99.4% of escalations, and added only 8.2 ms of overhead for policy verification; furthermore, in a user study where N=16, participants significantly preferred Conleash scoped permissions over traditional methods, citing higher trust and reduced prompting.

</details>


### [126] [Can a Single Message Paralyze the AI Infrastructure? The Rise of AbO-DDoS Attacks through Targeted Mobius Injection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11442v1)
*Zi Liang,Ronghua Li,Yanyun Wang,Qingqing Ye,Haibo Hu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: Mobius注入攻击使agent成为DDoS节点，agent安全威胁可迁移

TL;DR: 本文提出Mobius注入攻击，利用语义闭合漏洞将智能体武器化为僵尸节点发起AbO-DDoS攻击，并基于智能体组件能量分析提出防御机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究忽视了智能体在用户-智能体-服务链中作为破坏性枢纽的系统性风险。

Method: 通过利用智能体逻辑中的语义闭合漏洞，实施单次文本注入诱导递归执行，实现轻量、隐蔽且可配置的Mobius注入攻击。

Result: 在多种智能体上实现单节点调用放大51.0倍、多节点延迟膨胀229.1倍，攻击性能随节点数超线性增长。

Conclusion: 提出基于智能体组件能量分析的主动防御机制，通过检测组件图中的异常能量来识别恶意递归触发器。

中文摘要：大语言模型（LLM）智能体已成为关键中介，协调人类用户与各种数字服务和LLM基础设施之间的复杂交互。虽然先前的研究广泛考察了LLM和智能体在孤立状态下的安全性，但智能体作为用户-智能体-服务链中破坏性枢纽的系统性风险在很大程度上仍被忽视。在这项工作中，我们通过引入Mobius注入揭示了一种新的威胁范式，这是一种复杂的攻击，将自主智能体武器化为僵尸节点，以发动我们定义的基于智能体且面向智能体的分布式拒绝服务（AbO-DDoS）攻击。通过利用智能体逻辑中名为语义闭合的结构性漏洞，攻击者可以通过单次文本注入诱导智能体组件的持续递归执行。我们证明这种攻击异常轻量、对传统DDoS监控器和当代AI安全过滤器均具有隐蔽性，且高度可配置，允许针对特定环境或模型提供商进行精确打击。为评估实际影响，我们在三个代表性爪型智能体和三个主流编码智能体上进行了广泛实验，这些智能体集成了12个前沿专有或开源权重的大语言模型。我们的结果表明，Mobius注入在多种任务上实现了显著攻击成功率，驱动单节点调用放大高达51.0倍，多节点p95延迟膨胀高达229.1倍。攻击性能随中毒节点数量呈超线性增长。为缓解Mobius注入，我们提出了一种利用智能体组件能量（ACE）分析的主动防御机制，通过在智能体组件图中测量异常能量来检测恶意递归触发器。

Original abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents have emerged as key intermediaries, orchestrating complex interactions between human users and a wide range of digital services and LLM infrastructures. While prior research has extensively examined the security of LLMs and agents in isolation, the systemic risk of the agent acting as a disruptive hub within the user-agent-service chain remains largely overlooked. In this work, we expose a novel threat paradigm by introducing Mobius Injection, a sophisticated attack that weaponizes autonomous agents into zombie nodes to launch what we define as gent-based and -Oriented DDoS (AbO-DDoS) attacks. By exploiting a structural vulnerability in agentic logic named Semantic Closure, an adversary can induce sustained recursive execution of agent components through a single textual injection. We demonstrate that this attack is exceptionally lightweight, stealthy against both traditional DDoS monitors and contemporary AI safety filters, and highly configurable, allowing for surgical targeting of specific environments or model providers. To evaluate the real-world impact, we conduct extensive experiments across three representative claw-style agents and three mainstream coding agents, integrated with 12 frontier proprietary or open-weight LLMs. Our results demonstrate that Mobius Injection achieves substantial attack success across diverse tasks, driving single-node call amplification up to 51.0x and multi-node p95 latency inflation up to 229.1x. The attack performance exhibits a superlinear increase with the number of poisoning nodes. To mitigate Mobius Injection, we propose a proactive defense mechanism using Agent Component Energy (ACE) Analysis, which detects malicious recursive triggers by measuring anomalous energy in the agent's component graph.

</details>


### [127] [Cochise: A Reference Harness for Autonomous Penetration Testing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11671v1)
*Andreas Happe,Jürgen Cito*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Cochise，一个轻量级的自主渗透测试实验框架，包含分离的规划器-执行器架构和多种分析工具，旨在作为可复用的基准设施。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM驱动的渗透测试系统架构复杂，难以评估简单组件带来的增益，需要一个最小化、可复用的实验基础设施来公平比较不同方法和模型。

Method: 设计并实现Cochise框架，共597行Python代码，采用分离的Planner-Executor架构，长期状态存于LLM上下文外，通过SSH执行命令并自纠正，场景提示可适应不同目标。

Result: 在GOAD测试平台上评估，并发布回放和分析工具以及JSON轨迹日志数据集，证明框架有效性且便于其他研究者使用。

Conclusion: Cochise不是最先进的渗透测试代理，而是作为可重用的实验基础设施，用于比较模型、代理架构和渗透测试轨迹。

中文摘要：近期关于LLM驱动的自主渗透测试的研究报告了有希望的结果，但现有系统通常结合了多种架构、提示和工具集成选择，使得难以判断相对于简单的智能体框架获得了什么。我们提出了cochise，一个由597行Python代码组成的自主渗透测试实验参考框架。Cochise通过SSH将LLM驱动的智能体连接到Linux执行主机，并支持从该跳板主机可达的受控目标环境。该原型实现了一个分离的规划器-执行器架构，其中长期状态维护在LLM上下文之外，而ReAct风格的执行器通过SSH发出命令并根据命令输出进行自我纠正。场景提示可以适应不同的目标环境。为了演示我们最小框架的有效性，我们在一个名为Game of Active Directory (GOAD)的实时第三方测试平台上对其进行了评估。除了框架，我们还发布了回放和分析工具：(i) cochise-replay用于离线可视化捕获的运行，(ii) cochise-analyze-logs和cochise-analyze-graphs用于成本、令牌、时长和入侵分析，以及(iii) 来自GOAD运行的JSON轨迹日志语料库，允许研究人员在不配备48-64 GB RAM / 190 GB存储测试平台的情况下研究智能体行为。Cochise旨在作为可重用的实验基础设施，用于比较模型、智能体架构和渗透测试轨迹，而不是作为最先进的渗透测试智能体。

Original abstract: Recent work on LLM-driven autonomous penetration testing reports promising results, but existing systems often combine many architectural, prompting, and tool-integration choices, making it difficult to tell what is gained over a simple agent scaffold. We present cochise, a 597 LOC Python reference harness for autonomous penetration-testing experiments. Cochise connects an LLM-driven agent to a Linux execution host over SSH and supports controlled target environments reachable from that jump host.
  The prototype implements a separated Planner--Executor architecture in which long-term state is maintained outside the LLM context, while a ReAct-style executor issues commands over SSH and self-corrects based on command outputs. The scenario prompt can be adapted to different target environments. To demonstrate the efficacy of our minimal harness, we evaluate it against a live third-party testbed called Game of Active Directory (GOAD).
  Alongside the harness, we release replay and analysis tools: (i) cochise-replay for offline visualization of captured runs, (ii) cochise-analyze-alogs and cochise-analyze-graphs for cost, token, duration, and compromise analysis, and (iii) a corpus of JSON trajectory logs from GOAD runs, allowing researchers to study agent behavior without provisioning the 48--64 GB RAM / 190 GB storage testbed themselves. Cochise is intended not as a state-of-the-art pen-testing agent, but as reusable experimental infrastructure for comparing models, agent architectures, and penetration-testing traces.

</details>


### [128] [Behavioral Integrity Verification for AI Agent Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11770v1)
*Yuhao Wu,Tung-Ling Li,Hongliang Liu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 直接研究LLM agent技能的完整性验证，结合代码分析和LLM能力提取，对agent安全与可靠性至关重要。

TL;DR: 提出行为完整性验证（BIV）框架，结合代码分析与LLM能力提取，在大量Agent技能中发现80%存在声明-实现偏差，但多数源于疏忽；恶意技能检测F1达0.946。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全工作忽视技能工件本身的验证，导致Agent技能可能包含未声明的恶意或错误行为，需要系统化的行为完整性审计。

Method: 形式化行为完整性验证（BIV）问题，采用类型化集合比较；提出结合确定性代码分析与LLM辅助能力提取的BIV框架，生成结构化证据用于偏差分类、根因分析和恶意检测。

Result: 在OpenClaw的49,943个技能上，80%存在偏差，识别四种新型复合威胁；81.1%偏差为疏忽，18.9%为恶意，5%含多阶段攻击链；恶意检测F1=0.946，优于基线。

Conclusion: BIV框架能大规模审计Agent技能的行为完整性，揭示普遍但多数非恶意的实现差距，并有效检测恶意技能。

中文摘要：Agent技能扩展了LLM代理，使其具有特权第三方能力，如文件系统访问、凭证、网络调用和shell执行。现有的安全工作能够捕获恶意提示和危险的运行时行为，但技能工件本身却未经检验。我们将此形式化为行为完整性验证（BIV）问题：在一个共享的分类体系上，对声明能力与实际能力进行类型化集合比较，该分类体系连接代码、指令和元数据。BIV框架通过将确定性代码分析与LLM辅助的能力提取相结合来实现这种比较。由此产生的结构化证据支持三种下游分析：偏差分类、根因分类和恶意技能检测。在OpenClaw注册中心的49,943个技能上，偏差分类揭示了普遍存在的描述-实现差距：80.0%的技能偏离了声明行为，并浮现了四种新型复合威胁类别。根因分类发现偏差主要是疏忽而非恶意：81.1%归因于开发者疏忽，18.9%归因于对抗意图，其中5.0%的技能携带预测的多阶段攻击链。在一个906个技能的恶意技能检测基准上，BIV的F1值达到了0.946，优于最先进的基于规则的基线模型和单次LLM基线模型。这些结果表明，行为完整性审计能够在规模上应用于Agent技能。

Original abstract: Agent skills extend LLM agents with privileged third-party capabilities such as filesystem access, credentials, network calls, and shell execution. Existing safety work catches malicious prompts and risky runtime actions, but the skill artifact itself goes unverified. We formalize this as the behavioral integrity verification (BIV) problem: a typed set comparison between declared and actual capabilities over a shared taxonomy that bridges code, instructions, and metadata. The BIV framework instantiates this comparison by pairing deterministic code analysis with LLM-assisted capability extraction. The resulting structured evidence supports three downstream analyses: deviation taxonomy, root-cause classification, and malicious-skill detection. On 49,943 skills from the OpenClaw registry, the deviation taxonomy reveals a pervasive description-implementation gap: 80.0% of skills deviate from declared behavior, with four novel compound-threat categories surfaced. Root-cause classification finds that deviations are mostly oversight, not malice: 81.1% trace to developer oversight and 18.9% to adversarial intent, with 5.0% of skills carrying predicted multi-stage attack chains. On a 906-skill malicious-skill detection benchmark, BIV reaches an F1 of 0.946, outperforming state-of-the-art rule-based and single-pass LLM baselines. These results demonstrate behavioral integrity auditing for agent skills at scale.

### [129] [IPI-proxy: An Intercepting Proxy for Red-Teaming Web-Browsing AI Agents Against Indirect Prompt Injection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11868v1)
*Chia-Pei,Chen,Kentaroh Toyoda,Anita Lai,Alex Leung*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提供针对web浏览agent的间接提示注入红队工具，对coding agent安全测试有直接借鉴意义

TL;DR: IPI-proxy是一个开源工具包，通过拦截代理重写白名单域名的HTTP响应来嵌入攻击负载，用于对Web浏览AI代理进行间接提示注入的红队测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有红队工具无法模拟白名单场景下代理实际访问的页面，且缺乏可重复的测试环境。

Method: 构建拦截代理，实时修改HTTP响应，嵌入来自6个基准测试的820个攻击字符串，支持多种嵌入技术和插入点的参数化配置。

Result: 实现了无需模拟页面的参数扫描评估，并提供了泄露跟踪器记录成功攻击。

Conclusion: IPI-proxy桥接了静态基准测试和实际部署，为安全团队提供了可重复的评估和加固工具。

中文摘要：Web浏览AI代理越来越多地部署在企业环境中，这些环境有严格的批准域名白名单，但对手仍然可以通过在这些域名提供的HTML页面中嵌入隐藏指令来影响它们。现有的红队资源在这种场景下不足：提示注入基准测试提供的是预构建的对抗性页面，白名单代理无法访问；而通用LLM扫描器探测的是模型API而非其检索的内容。我们提出了IPI-proxy，一个用于对Web浏览代理进行间接提示注入（IPI）红队测试的开源工具包。其核心是一个拦截代理，它在飞行中重写来自白名单域名的真实HTTP响应，嵌入来自统一库的820个去重攻击字符串的负载，这些字符串从六个已发布的基准测试（BIPIA, InjecAgent, AgentDojo, Tensor Trust, WASP, LLMail-Inject）中提取。一个YAML驱动的测试工具独立参数化负载集、嵌入技术（HTML注释、不可见CSS或LLM生成的语义散文）和HTML插入点（从head_meta到script_comment的6个位置），无需模拟页面或沙箱环境即可进行参数扫描评估。配套的泄露跟踪器记录成功的回调。本文描述了威胁模型，将IPI-proxy置于当代IPI基准测试和红队工具中，并详细介绍了其架构、设计决策和配置界面。通过在静态基准测试和实际部署之间架起桥梁，IPI-proxy为AI安全团队提供了一个可重复的基础，用于在攻击者在生产环境中利用的相同检索表面上测量和加固Web浏览代理以抵御间接提示注入。

Original abstract: Web-browsing AI agents are increasingly deployed in enterprise settings under strict whitelists of approved domains, yet adversaries can still influence them by embedding hidden instructions in the HTML pages those domains serve. Existing red-teaming resources fall short of this scenario: prompt-injection benchmarks ship pre-built adversarial pages that whitelisted agents cannot reach, and generic LLM scanners probe the model API rather than its retrieved content. We present IPI-proxy, an open-source toolkit for red-teaming web-browsing agents against indirect prompt injection (IPI). At its core is an intercepting proxy that rewrites real HTTP responses from whitelisted domains in flight, embedding payloads drawn from a unified library of 820 deduplicated attack strings extracted from six published benchmarks (BIPIA, InjecAgent, AgentDojo, Tensor Trust, WASP, and LLMail-Inject). A YAML-driven test harness independently parameterizes the payload set, the embedding technique (HTML comment, invisible CSS, or LLM-generated semantic prose), and the HTML insertion point (6 locations from \icode{head\_meta} to \icode{script\_comment}), enabling parameter-sweep evaluation without mock pages or sandboxed environments. A companion exfiltration tracker logs successful callbacks. This paper describes the threat model, situates IPI-proxy among contemporary IPI benchmarks and red-teaming tools, and details its architecture, design decisions, and configuration interface. By bridging static benchmarks and live deployment, IPI-proxy gives AI security teams a reproducible substrate for measuring and hardening web-browsing agents against indirect prompt injection on the same retrieval surface attackers exploit in production.

</details>


### [130] [Proteus: A Self-Evolving Red Team for Agent Skill Ecosystems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.11891v1)
*Zhaojiacheng Zhou*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提出自适应红队框架Proteus评估agent技能生态风险，为agent安全评测提供新思路

TL;DR: 提出Proteus灰盒自进化红队框架评估LLM Agent技能的自适应泄露风险，实验表明当前技能审查在面对迭代攻击时严重低估残余风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单次审计或提示级红队无法充分评估技能部署风险，因为攻击者可基于反馈反复重写技能。

Method: Proteus通过形式化五轴攻击空间搜索，利用审计-沙箱-预言机流水线评估候选并指导变异，同时执行路径扩展和表面扩展以生成多样化攻击。

Result: 8个第一阶段单元中ASR@5达40-90%，学习曲线正向；第二阶段产生438个变体，SkillVetter绕过率≥93%，AI-Infra-Guard仍接受高达41.3%的联合成功。

Conclusion: 当前技能审查面对自适应攻击者时大幅低估残余风险，需更鲁棒的防御机制。

中文摘要：Agent技能通过可重复使用的指令、工具接口和可执行代码扩展LLM Agent，用户越来越多地从市场、仓库和社区渠道安装第三方技能。由于一个技能既暴露出可执行行为，也暴露出上下文设置的文档，其部署风险不能仅通过单次审计或提示级别的红队测试来评估：一个现实的攻击者可以利用审计和运行时反馈反复重写技能。我们将这种风险定义为自适应泄露——一个有预算的攻击者能否迭代修改技能，直到它通过审计并产生经过验证的运行时危害——并提出了Proteus，一个用于测量该风险的灰盒自进化红队框架。Proteus搜索一个形式化的五轴技能攻击空间。每个候选者通过统一的审计-沙箱-预言机流水线进行评估，该流水线返回结构化的审计结果和运行时证据，以指导跨轮次的变异。除了初始规避，Proteus还执行路径扩展，寻找成功攻击的替代实现，以及表面扩展，将学到的实现模式转移到原始种子目录之外的新攻击目标。在8个第一阶段单元中，Proteus在5轮攻击中达到40-90%的攻击成功率（ASR@5），并且对两个评估的审计者都有正向的学习曲线斜率。第二阶段的路径/表面扩展产生了438个同时逃避和致命的变体，其中SkillVetter在每个单元中都被绕过≥93%，而AI-Infra-Guard（我们评估的最强公共审计者）仍允许高达41.3%的联合成功。这些结果表明，当面对自适应、反馈驱动的攻击者进行评估时，当前的技能审查大大低估了残余风险。

Original abstract: Agent skills extend LLM agents with reusable instructions, tool interfaces, and executable code, and users increasingly install third-party skills from marketplaces, repositories, and community channels. Because a skill exposes both executable behavior and context-setting documentation, its deployment risk cannot be measured by single-shot audits or prompt-level red teams alone: a realistic attacker can use audit and runtime feedback to repeatedly rewrite the skill. We frame this risk as \emph{adaptive leakage} -- whether a budgeted attacker can iteratively revise a skill until it passes audit and produces verified runtime harm -- and present \ours{}, a grey-box self-evolving red-team framework for measuring it. Proteus searches a formalized five-axis skill-attack space. Each candidate is evaluated through a unified audit-sandbox-oracle pipeline that returns structured audit findings and runtime evidence to guide cross-round mutation. Beyond initial evasion, Proteus performs path expansion, which finds alternative implementations of successful attacks, and surface expansion, which transfers learned implementation patterns to new attack objectives beyond the original seed catalogue. Across eight phase-1 cells, Proteus reaches 40--90\% Attack Success Rate at $5$ rounds (ASR@5) with positive learning-curve slopes on both evaluated auditors. Phase-2 path/surface expansion produces 438 jointly bypassing and lethal variants, with SkillVetter bypassed at $\geq 93\%$ in every cell and AI-Infra-Guard, the strongest public auditor we evaluate, still admitting up to 41.3\% joint-success. These results show that current skill vetting substantially underestimates residual risk when evaluated against adaptive, feedback-driven attackers.

</details>


### [131] [SkillSafetyBench: Evaluating Agent Safety under Skill-Facing Attack Surfaces](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12015v2)
*Chang Jin,An Wang,Zeming Wei,Kai Wang,Biaojie Zeng,Qiaosheng Zhang,Chao Yang,Jingjing Qu,Xia Hu,Xingcheng Xu*

Selection reason: LLM agent安全评估benchmark，属于agent评测方法，可迁移到coding agent安全。

TL;DR: 技能中介的安全故障被忽视，SkillSafetyBench评估表明非用户攻击能诱导不安全行为，且智能体安全依赖于多因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全评估忽略技能、工件和执行环境中的不安全影响，即使用户请求良性。

Method: 构建SkillSafetyBench，包含47任务、155个对抗案例，使用基于规则的验证器，在多个CLI智能体和模型后端上实验。

Result: 非用户攻击可一致诱导不安全行为，存在跨领域、攻击方法和配对的不同失败模式。

Conclusion: 智能体安全不仅依赖模型对齐，还依赖对技能解释、工作流信任和执行环境交互。

中文摘要：可复用的技能正在成为扩展大型语言模型智能体的常见接口，它将程序性指导与对文件、工具、记忆和执行环境的访问打包在一起。然而，这种模块化引入了现有安全评估大多未发现的攻击面：即使当用户请求是良性的，不安全的影响也可能存在于技能指导、本地工件或执行环境文件中，从而引导智能体走向不安全的行动。我们提出了SkillSafetyBench，一个可运行的基准测试，用于评估这种由技能中介的安全故障。SkillSafetyBench包含47个任务、6个风险领域和30个安全类别中的155个对抗性案例，每个案例都使用特定于案例的基于规则的验证器进行评估。通过在多个CLI智能体和模型后端上的实验表明，非用户攻击可以持续诱导不安全行为，不同领域、攻击方法和脚手架-模型配对之间存在不同的失败模式。我们的研究结果表明，智能体安全性不仅依赖于模型层面的对齐，还取决于智能体如何解释技能、信任工作流上下文以及通过可执行环境行动。

Original abstract: Reusable skills are becoming a common interface for extending large language model agents, packaging procedural guidance with access to files, tools, memory, and execution environments. However, this modularity introduces attack surfaces that are largely missed by existing safety evaluations: even when the user request is benign, unsafe influence may reside in skill guidance, local artifacts, or execution-environment files that steer the agent toward unsafe actions. We present SkillSafetyBench, a runnable benchmark for evaluating such skill-mediated safety failures. SkillSafetyBench includes 155 adversarial cases across 47 tasks, 6 risk domains, and 30 safety categories, each evaluated with a case-specific rule-based verifier. Experiments with multiple CLI agents and model backends show that non-user attacks can consistently induce unsafe behavior, with distinct failure patterns across domains, attack methods, and scaffold-model pairings. Our findings suggest that agent safety depends not only on model-level alignment, but also on how agents interpret skills, trust workflow context, and act through executable environments.

### [132] [The Misattribution Gap: When Memory Poisoning Looks Like Model Failure in Agentic AI Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22842v1)
*Tanzim Ahad,Ismail Hossain,Md Jahangir Alam,Sai Puppala,Syed Bahauddin Alam,Sajedul Talukder*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究多agent系统中记忆层攻击导致的误判，对agent安全有启发

TL;DR: 提出语义规范漂移（SND）攻击，利用共享向量存储中的文档注入操控多智能体系统，现有防御无效；提出反事实组合测试和内存持久信息流控制来检测和防御。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有防御假设智能体不当行为源于模型对齐失误，但实际存在内存层攻击导致的归因差距，需要新的视角和防御方法。

Method: 形式化语义规范漂移（SND）攻击，提出反事实组合测试（CCT）用于检测，以及内存持久信息流控制（MP-IFC）用于防御。

Result: CCT检测准确率87.5%、零误报；MP-IFC阻挡97%攻击；攻击在5个会话内生效且持久；四个安全分类器均未检测到攻击。

Conclusion: SND是一种有效的多智能体系统攻击方式，需采用新的检测和防御机制，未来应关注跨会话信息流控制。

中文摘要：多智能体AI管道通常假设智能体不当行为源于模型对齐失误。我们发现该假设存在结构性缺陷，即“归因差距”：内存层攻击产生的行为与模型故障无法区分，导致防御者应用错误的补救措施。我们将“语义规范漂移”（SND）形式化为导致智能体不当行为的第三条路径，不同于涌现性错位和共谋。在SND中，一份策略格式的文档通过正常上传进入共享向量存储，并在经过“信任洗白链”失去来源后，重新作为受信任的系统上下文出现。在64次记录故障中，归因系统一致归咎于模型。四个安全分类器（包括一个针对内存投毒训练的）在510个检查点中均未检测到任何异常。在65个有效案例中的59个中，智能体在合规前明确引用注入文档作为规范权威。该攻击无需触发器、无需模型访问或重复交互，在五个会话内达到完全效果，并无限持续。我们提出了“反事实组合测试”，该测试以87.5%的准确率和零误报识别因果入口，而取证基线在所有25个场景中均失败。我们进一步证明了“检索-覆盖困境”，表明更强的规避本质上会削弱攻击效果，限制了自适应绕过策略。最后，我们提出了“内存持久信息流控制”，在先前防御失败的跨会话边界阻挡了97%的攻击。我们发布了SND语料库，这是首个具有时间持久性和多智能体组合的对抗性记忆基准，涵盖金融和医疗保健领域。

Original abstract: Multi-agent AI pipelines typically assume that agent misconduct originates from model misalignment. We identify a structural failure in this assumption, the \emph{Misattribution Gap}, where memory-layer attacks produce behaviors indistinguishable from model failure, causing defenders to apply the wrong remediation. We formalize \emph{Semantic Norm Drift} (SND) as a third path to agent misconduct, distinct from emergent misalignment and collusion. In SND, a policy-formatted document enters a shared vector store through normal uploads and later reappears as trusted system context after provenance is lost through a Trust Laundering Chain. Across 64 documented failures, attribution systems consistently blamed the model. Four safety classifiers, including one trained on memory poisoning, produced zero detections across 510 checkpoints. In 59 of 65 valid cases, agents explicitly cited the injected document as normative authority before complying. The attack requires no trigger, model access, or repeated interaction, achieves full effect within five sessions, and persists indefinitely. We introduce Counterfactual Composition Testing, which identifies the causal entry with 87.5% accuracy and zero false positives, while a forensics baseline fails across all 25 scenarios. We further prove the Retrieval-Coverage Dilemma, showing that stronger evasion inherently weakens the attack, limiting adaptive bypass strategies. Finally, we propose Memory-Persistent Information-Flow Control, which blocks 97% of attacks at the cross-session boundary where prior defenses fail. We release the SND Corpus, the first adversarial memory benchmark with temporal persistence and multi-agent composition across financial and Health Care domains.

</details>


### [133] [CoT-Guard: Small Models for Strong Monitoring](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12746v1)
*Nirav Diwan,Han Wang,Berkcan Kapusuzoglu,Ramin Moradi,Supriyo Chakraborty,Giri Iyengar,Sambit Sahu,Huan Zhang,Gang Wang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: CoT-Guard在提示和代码操纵攻击下G-mean^2为75%，超过GPT-5.4（56%）、GPT-5-mini（41%）和Qwen3-32B（54%），接近Gemini-3-Flash（83%）。

Conclusion: CoT-Guard提供实用且成本效益的用户端防御，显著提升隐藏目标检测，避免大型监控器部署成本。

中文摘要：监控推理模型的思维链（CoT）是检测代码生成任务中隐蔽不当行为（即隐藏目标）的一种有前景的方法。虽然大型模型（GPT-5、Gemini-3-Flash）可以作为有效的CoT监控器，但由于冗长的推理轨迹和高昂的API成本，它们部署成本高昂，这凸显了对更小、更便宜替代方案的需求。然而，我们发现当前的小型模型（4B-8B）尽管可以访问CoT，但在检测隐藏目标方面仍存在困难，经常将其误认为是用户查询的一部分。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种结合监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）的后训练流程，其中SFT通过从更强的监控器中蒸馏检测行为来缩小领域内任务的差距，而RL针对困难且巧妙构造的隐藏目标帮助模型泛化到领域外监控任务。为了验证这种泛化能力，我们在一种由实际供应链攻击启发的现实威胁模型下进行评估，其中对手是第三方LLM路由器，通过提示操纵或代码操纵攻击将隐藏目标注入到代码生成请求中。为了超越大型监控器已经饱和的目标，我们还引入了四个对强监控器也具挑战性的新任务。最后，我们介绍了CoT-Guard，一个4B参数的监控器，在提示操纵和代码操纵攻击下都表现出卓越的泛化性能，实现了75%的G-mean^2（即TNR x TPR），超过了GPT-5.4（56%）、GPT-5-mini（41%）和Qwen3-32B（54%），同时缩小了与Gemini-3-Flash（83%）的差距。这些结果表明，CoT-Guard提供了一种实用且具有成本效益的用户端防御，显著提高了隐藏目标检测能力，同时避免了大型监控器的部署成本。

Original abstract: Monitoring the chain-of-thought (CoT) of reasoning models is a promising approach for detecting covert misbehavior (i.e., hidden objectives) in code generation tasks. While large models (GPT-5, Gemini-3-Flash) can serve as effective CoT monitors, they are expensive to deploy due to the lengthy reasoning traces and high API cost, emphasizing the need for smaller, cheaper alternatives. Nevertheless, we find that current small models (4B--8B) struggle to detect hidden objectives despite access to the CoT, frequently misattributing them as part of the user query. To address this, we propose a post-training pipeline combining supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and reinforcement learning (RL), where SFT narrows the gap for in-domain tasks by distilling detection behavior from stronger monitors, and RL on hard and subtly crafted hidden objectives helps the model generalize to out-of-domain monitoring tasks. To validate this generalization, we evaluate under a realistic threat model motivated by practical supply-chain attacks, where the adversary is a third-party LLM router injecting hidden objectives into code-generation requests through either prompt manipulation or code manipulation attacks. To push beyond objectives that large monitors already saturate, we also introduce four new challenging tasks even for strong monitors. Finally, we introduce CoT-Guard, a 4B-parameter monitor that demonstrates superior generalization performance under both prompt and code manipulation attacks, achieving a G-mean^2 (i.e., TNR x TPR) of 75% and outperforming GPT-5.4 (56%), GPT-5-mini (41%), and Qwen3-32B (54%), while closing the gap to Gemini-3-Flash (83%). These results demonstrate that CoT-Guard provides a practical and cost-effective user-side defense, substantially improving hidden-objective detection while avoiding the deployment cost of large monitors.

</details>
